Nti apú bɛsɨŋ be bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ̌ bakoŋo Yesu. Mandɛm yímbɔŋ anáŋ átɔ́ŋ be ɛnyu bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkɔŋ batɨ.
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ́ nchí ghati yɛ wɔ chí bɛ bǎkɛ́ rɔ mɛnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bo mankɛm. Ɛ́rɨ mǎnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ bhɔ nɛ ɛ̌ti bo báchák. Ɛ́rɨ mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ́chyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ ntá bho mankɛm.
Bo bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyu yɔ, bɔ mankɛm nɛ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti barɛm yɛ bɛ, nkaysi Mandɛm achi tɛtɛp. Barɛm ɛnyu yɔ, mbɔnyunɛ manaŋ baka nyaka nkwɔ bɛ́ Jɔ̌n anjwiti bhɔ́.
Nɛka ɛnɛn Josɛ́f nɛ Mandɛm kɛ̌ nɛ́kʉ́ bɛ́ mpok yi arɔbhɛ chi bɛ́gu, arɛm ɛ̌ti nɛfú anɛ bo Israɛl bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛfu ɛtɔk Íjip, nɛ aghati bhɔ bɛ mpok bɔ báfù, mánsɔt bɛghɛp ɛbhi mandɔk nɛ bhɔ.
Satan arɔ yɛ Yesu arɔk, bɔángɛl Mandɛm barɔk bachyɛ Yesu nɛkwak. 
Bɔ̌ma bǎkɛ́ bhak mǎmbɔ ndǔ nkaysi yɛka. Bák ká mbɔ bɔ abhɛn babhʉɛt amɔ ndu barak bɛbʉ́, kɛ ndǔ nkaysi ayɛka bák ká bɛsɛ́nɛ́ bho.
Tɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ fyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ bo mángɔ́k bhɔ.
Bo mankɛm báchí bǒnto kɛ́? Bo mankɛm báchí barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ kɛ? Bo mankɛm báchí batɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ? Bo mankɛm bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay kɛ?
Mbák mmu ywɛka ánkóŋó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báyàŋ bɛkʉ, ǎgú. Kɛ mbák mǎnkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó áyàŋ mǎnkʉ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Sɛ́rɛ̀m nɔ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́ghok bɛ mbɔk ywɛka bǎbhɔ̀t abhɔt nɛ bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhap chi bɛ́fyɛ nnyu ndǔ barak bo bachak.
Ápɛ́rɛ rɔŋ, abhɨŋɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi bati byo. Achyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ɛbhǎ nkáp, arɛm bɛ ‘Kɔ nɔ́kɔ́ ká ɛsiɛ nɛ nkáp wu kpátɛ̌ mpok nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ɛná.’
Ɔ́yàŋ bɛ́way mɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́wáy mmu Íjip ɛ́yú?’
Píta nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bati apay bákwɛ́n kɛnɔ́, kɛ máŋɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bághɔ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Yesu nɛ bǒ bati apay abhɛn bachi nyaka téé nɛ yi.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mpok mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ kway bɛ́kɛpntɨ, ntó Tímɔti bɛ ántwɔ́, ángɔ́ mbák babhʉɛ́t bɛ́sɨ́kɨ ntɨ nɛ Kristo. Mbɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛcháy bɛ ngufú Satan mmu ámɔ̀ bo ndu bɛkʉ bɔ bákɛ́pɛrɛ noko Yesu, abhɔŋ mbi nɛ bhe nɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ mɛnkɛm bɛrɔŋ ndɛ́ndɛm.
Yesu apɛt achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl angati nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Mmu amɔt abhak amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyɔ anɛ awɔ́ ywi ágú.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Moses ághɔ́ ɛkʉ yi abhak maknkay. Nɛ nɛrɔŋ yi árɔ̀ŋ kɛkwɔt bɛyɨŋɨ, aghók Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ndu ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ,
Ánáŋ ántwɔ́ awu, syɛptí ká yi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǒ Mandɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsyɛpti ntɨ mǔnkwɔ, nɛ mǎnkwak bɛchyɛ yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ yi. Yímbɔŋ anáŋ akwak bɛyǎ bho, nɛ yɛ̌ chi mɛmbɔ̌ŋ nkwɔ.
“Mbák manywɔp anɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ ámay, mmok ánɛm tɛ́mté, ntaŋ kɛpɛrɛ ghɔɔ, mambe ámfu amfay ánkwɛnti, nɛ bɛtaŋ mfáy mɛnyɨkɨsi.
Táytɔs mmu ákɔ̀ nɛ mɛ abhak mmu Grik. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bákɛ te mbɔŋ kákáti bɛ mánsíɛ́p yi.
Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm yɛ bɛ yi? Sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ́, nɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm kɛ bɛ́rɔ́hɛ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ kɛ? Wáwák!
Mbok Yesu atɨŋ ataka atú Gálili ankɛm. 
Bo abhɛn bákwak bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm, bábhɔŋ bɛbhak bo abhɛn bápú kʉ ntok nɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhap nkwɔ́. Bábhíkɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak bǒ bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ, bábhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ bɛbhak manyǔ mmɛ́m, nɛ bákɛ́ bhák bǒ ngoŋó nkáp.
Yesu achyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋá bɛbʉ́ mɛnkɛm nɛ ndu bɛso batɨ ywɛsɛ. Akʉ nɔ, bɛ sɛ́mbák bǒbhi yímbɔŋ, nɔ chi bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛkʉ chi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ.
Arɔ bhɔ arɔk ndɔŋ anɛ ajwi ɛ́rát are nɨkmʉɛt ɛnyumɔt mbɔ ndɔŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɨ ɛpay.
Mandɛm anáŋ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfakari nɛ Yesu bɛkoŋo nkaysi yi. Báfyɛ́ yɛ́ yi amɔ yɛká bɛ mǎnchyɛ yi ntá bo bɛbʉ́ bɛ mángó ndǔ ɛkotákátí, mángway.
Ngɛ́mtay ɛ́fú yɛ ndu mɔ́ngo wu, ɛjwi amɨk. Báchyɛ yɔ bɛtaŋ bɛtiɛ bho mbɔ ngá-nɛghay.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mpok ɛyɔ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ Kristo. Bě kɛbhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ bǎbhak mankɔ ndu nkwɔ bo abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ afyɛ́ bariɛp ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ bɛkʉ ntá yap, kɛ ɛyɔ ɛbhɨkɨ yɨŋɨ nyaka bhe. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhaka ntɨ arɛ́ mǎnòŋ nɔkɔ fá ndǔ mmɨkɨ nɛ, nɛ be kɛrɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
Tɛ́mté wu, batú yi ánɛ́nɛ, nɛrɨ́ nɛ́káŋári yi anyu abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ sayri.
Píta atɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ághátí nyaka yi bɛ, “Nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kók, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ.” Afú nɛfí, adi kɛbhɔ, nɛ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ.
Mpok bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ bɛ́ghɔ̀ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ, bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ ɛnyu yɔ ɛchi,
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ bɔ́ báté bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi bɛti nɛ ngósí. Nɛ yí mmu achi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ǎbhák chɔŋ ɛkuti ɛyap.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm chi bɛ, “Mbák chí nkaysi Mandɛm, chɔŋ ambʉɛrɛ bɛsɛ́ nɛpɛ́m, anchyɛ bɛsɛ́ bɛtaŋ sɛ́nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ.”
Yesu abhɨ́kɨ́ re ghaka nyaka ɛtɔk, abhak chí ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Matá atɛmɛri yi.
Ngɛ́mtay bǒbhɔ bápɛt babho bɛbɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Haleluya! Mɔngo anɛ áfù Bábilɔn ǎkò amfay mpoknkɛm.”
Bɔ̌ma, mmu ákɛ́ rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti ntɨ. Mbák mmu ándɛ́m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti ntɨ, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, ansɔt mmʉɛt mbɔ ntaŋá manyé bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ́ ntɨ abɛp, nɔ́ ǎrɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ ǎtáŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm. Kɛ dɨŋɨ ká bɛ mbák mmu ǎrɛm bɛ́ ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛ́bɛp, nɔ́ yí ápú bhʉɛrɛ yɔ́, kɛ ǎsɔ̀t mmʉɛt mbɔ ntaŋá manyé bɛrɛm bɛ́ ɛbhé ɛ́bɛp.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bare rɔŋ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ndu nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát nɛ ngósí mpok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt.
Chi-bɛtɨk akaka yí tontó arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɔkʉ sayri! Ɔchí ɛrɨ́tí mǔbɛtɨk nɛ ɔchí mmǔ tɛtɛp. Ɔtɔ̌ŋ ndǔ mandú nkáp bɛ́ ɔchí mmǔ tɛtɛp. Nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ amfay bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Twɔ́ sɛ́nkʉ́ maŋák!’
Sɛ́fyɛ̀ nyaka bhe ntɨ nɛ sɛ́kpɛ̀mɛ nyaka bhe bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nɛ́nchyɛ Mandɛm maŋák. Yí kɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe bɛ mǎmbak bo abhɛn yi achi Mfɔ wap nɛ bɛ mǎmbák ndu kɛnɛ́m ɛki nɛ yi.
Báchɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́ nɛ bhɔ́ ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok, bǒnkwɔ́ Yesu bátɨ́k bhɔ́, nɛ maŋák bɛ mámpɛ́tnsɛm Yerúsalɛm ntá bo abhɛn bátó bhɔ́. [Kɛ Sáilas akʉ ntɨ bɛ́rɔp Antiɔk.]
“Nokó ka manɔ nɛ bachi bhɛka.” Ɛnɛ, chí ɛbhé mbɨ ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp amɛn abhak nɛ mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ yɔ.
Mbák ɔ̌nàk ɛpa, bɨŋɨ́ bachɛ́bhɛ́bho, nɛ babák, nɛ bakɛm, nɛ manɛmamɨ́k.
Mpok yɔ, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, nchí to bɔángɛl bha mǎmfɛrɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ bɛbʉ́, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkʉ bɛbʉ́ ndǔ nkwɔ bo abhɛn mɛ nchí Mfɔ wap.
Tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm achi tɛtɛp, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí bhe puyɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ nkwǎ mmu ákà ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ankʉ chi ɛchak.
Bɛ́kóŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ máyi aghati yi, arɔk arɛm ntá Hɛ́rɔd bɛ, “Chiɛ́ mɛ ntí Jɔ̌n Njwiti amɛm nchán myákátí-nɛ nɛ́nɛ!”
Bɔ́ bati arat bábhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses bárɛ̀m bɛ Ɛláija abhɔŋ bɛpɛtnsɛm fá amɨk kɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ ǎtó antwɔ́?”
Ɛchi ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka maŋák bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyu mmu yi achi, Mɔ́ywi nkwɔ achi.
Mɛmbɔŋ nchí kʉ ɛnyu yɔ. Nchí nu chí bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ́kʉ̀. Mpú kʉ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛmbɔŋ nkɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɨ́ ntá ya. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɨ́ ntá bo bachak kɛ̌ mɛ́kʉ̀, mbɔnyunɛ nchí yaŋ bɔ mántwɔ ntá Mandɛm bɛ yi ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ, arɔ njiɛ asɛp amɨk. Bɛyǎ bo bábhó bɛkoŋo yi.
Kɛ chɔŋ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi ambɨ nɛ́nɛ, mándɔp ansɛm, nɛ abhɛn bachi ansɛm, mandɔp ambɨ.” 
apɛmɛ bhɛsɛ. Ɛ́pú nyaka chí bɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛrɨtí mɛnyɨŋ, chi ɛ̌ti ntínso ɛni. Apɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ ndu ákʉ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ yi áfɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ bɛbʉ́ antɨ, akʉ sɛ́rɔp chí bo bakɔ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ.
Bo abhɛn bachi nɛ Yesu mpok yi ákʉ́ Lásárɔs afu ndǔ nnɛm báre ghati bo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí mbɔ batísiɛ Yesu.
Jɔ̌n arɛm bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ndu bɛfyɛ bhɔ ntɨ ndu ánù bɛkʉ mánóko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ yi aghati bhɔ.
Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ́, mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ndak, anjɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ nnyɛ́n ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ, ayɨ́kɨ́ nɔ nkwɔ ndǔ nnyɛ́n yɛ̌ntɨkɨ akap anɛ achi ndǔ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ yɔ.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛpe manyu, bákó ɛbhɨ, atú Gɛnɛ́sarɛt.
Kʉ yɛka bakwɔ́ bho Kristo mángɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ bho, nɛ bɛ ntí achi anɛ sɛ́dɛ̀p awɔ antɨ ɛ̌ti ɛyɛka bɛsí bhap.
Bɔ̌ma, nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt bɛ mǎmbák mbɔ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ ndɔp chí mbɔ bhe. Bǎbhɨkɨ kʉ mɛ bɛbʉ́.
Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bhe akap mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛkwak ntɨ nɛ aywi akap mbɔ ɛrɨ́tí nkʉbɛtɨk Mandɛm.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ bo abhɛn bǎsɔt bɛ bachi manɛm bǒnto bacha mɛ.
Bɛti nɛ ngósí, arebɨk, andakati nɔkɔ mmʉɛt nɛ batay ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt manɛm nɛ ndǔ njiɛ.
Bǎkɛ́ pɛrɛ rɔ yɛ bɛbʉ́ mɛ́mbɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛnɛ ɛ́gùgu bɛkʉ be mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yɔ ɛŋwaka bɛ mǎnkʉ.
Jóda mmɔ̌ Joánan, Joánan mmɔ̌ Résa, Résa mmɔ̌ Sɛrúbabɛl, Sɛrúbabɛl mmɔ̌ Síltiɛl, Síltiɛl mmɔ̌ Nɛri,
Mpok yɔ, mbák mmu ángátí bhe bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm átó fá’, yɛ̌ chi bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ yi awu!’ Bǎkɛ́ noko bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp.
Bǒ mankɛm bábʉɛ mɛ, kɛ Yesu Acha abhɨkɨ rɔ mɛ. Achi nɛ mɛ mpoknkɛm ankwaka nɔkɔ mɛ ndu áchyɛ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ yi. Ngátí bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nkɛm bɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mángók. Yesu afɛ́rɛ́ mɛ ndu nɛwú nkwɔ, afɛrɛ mɛ anyǔ nkʉ.
Kɛ ndǔ manywɔp anɛ ɛchɔŋ, anɛ́ achí kɛkwɔt nɛ ngwɛnti mmɨk, afʉɛ́t chi ntá Mɔ́ywi kɛ ǎrɛ̀m kɛpɨ ntá yɛsɛ. Yí kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ́ ámbák mmu anɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak ɛbhi. Nɛ afʉɛ́t chí ntá yi kɛ ǎghoko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ghɔ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ kɛmɛ bɛbʉ́ amfǎy bɛbʉ́. Nu nɔ́kɔ́ ká bɛkʉ chi bɛrɨ̌ndu ntá batɨ bǒnkwɔ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, chɔŋ angɔ́ ntínso nɛ bǒ Táya nɛ Sídɔn ɛncha bhe!
Bo ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒ batí ɛtɔk bághɔ́ nɛtaŋántɨ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n ndǔ bárɛ̀m kɛpɨ kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ ndǔ bághɔ́ nkwɔ bɛ́ bɔPíta báchí chí ndɛ́ndɛmɛ́ bho, nɛ bɛ bɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔk ɛkáti, bábhák maknkay. Kɛ bághɔ́ bɛ bɔPíta mánáŋ bákɔ̀ nyaka nɛ Yesu.
Bǒnto nɛ bakoŋo Yesu báchák atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, bághók bɛ mbɔk bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mánóko Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nkwɔ.
Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nchyɛ bhe mbi bɛghati bɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ya.
Atwɔ́ bɛ́gháti bho ɛ̌ti ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛyɔ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m, anoko yɔ.
Tɛtɛp, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛbhʉɛ́rɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ ɛ̌ti yi ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo, bo báchyɛ́ yi nɛnyok.
nɛ ɛ̌ti yɛka, mbɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛ mpú arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ɛfakari chi bɛ be mǎnókó. Sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́ngɔ́ yi.”
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mánchyɛ́ běka bǒnkwɔ kpák, mánkwak be bɛ mǎnkɔŋ batɨ, nɛ bɛ mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Manɛm ánɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm akʉ bɛyǎ bo Mandɛm abhɛn mǎnáŋ bágú nyaka bapɛtsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ Yesu akɛ́m yi ndu awɔ, akwak yi afate.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn báchyɛ́ bhe, kʉ ka bhɔ nɛ batɨ ayɛka ankɛm tɛ̌ndu bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ bátòk nɔ chi Yesu Acha, puyɛ̌ nkwǎ.
- Ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bárɔ̀ŋ, báre rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Agha ábɨŋɨri chɔŋ ntay amfɛrɛ anyu nnɛm ntá yɛsɛ?” Bárɛ̀m nyaka nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ntay ɛnɔ nɛ́chɨk nyaka tontó. Bápɛ́rɛ chwɔp arɛ́, bághɔ́ bɛ́ bábɨŋɨri nɔ nɛ́rɔp chi nɛpak.
Mbɔ ɛnyǔ nɛwú nɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ ntá mmu amɔt, kɛ nɛ́twɔ́ fá mmɨk, nɔ kɛ nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nkwɔ nɛfʉɛrɛ ntá mmu amɔt kɛ nɛ́twɔ́.
Sɛptí yɛ ka mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́ mpok yi ankway, yí ankosi bhe.
Tɛ̌ndu yi ákʉ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ Mandɛm ǎsɔ́t bɛ yi achi chak bɛsí bhi, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyǔ mmu apu kway bɛbhak nɛpɛ́m mbák abhɨkɨ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ ɛ̌yú, nɔ́ kɛ ɛchi bɛ mbák mmu apú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mankʉ, nɛrɛm yi árɛ̀m bɛ abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm ǎbhak chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Mandɛm mmu nchí mmɔ̌bɛtok ywi abhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yá bɛ́chá. Nɛ chɔŋ anchyɛ bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ bhé ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ntá yɛsɛ.
Mbák mmu akɔŋ bo, ǎbhɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ bhɔ, ǎtɔŋ bɔ bɛrɨ́ntɨ, apú bhɔŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ bhɔ, nɛ apu pányu nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ sɛ́dɛ̀p awɔ antɨ chi bɛ batɨ̌ yɛsɛ ághàti bhɛsɛ bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ nɛchi sayri nɛ bǒ mmɨk, sayri sayri nɛ bhe. Sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bo Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt nɛ tɛtɛp ndu sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ koŋo nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk. Sɛ́kʉ nɔ chi ndǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm bɛchi nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Kɛ mbák chí bǒ abhɛn báyɨ̀ŋɨ mɛ nɛ amík abʉ́abʉ, mánjɛnti nɔkɔ mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ, bɔ́ bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo chí mbɔnyunɛ mánù bɛ́chá mɛ. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi. Báyàŋ bɛbay mɛ chí batú áchák antí nɛ́nɛ, fá amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ nkwɔ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ yi, ndu mpok Nóa. Ató ɛghorǐ manyiɛp ɛ́wáy bǒbhɔ mankɛm. Apɛmɛ chí ndiɛrɛ Nóa mmu ághàti bho bɛ mámbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Nɛ apɛmɛ bo bachak bati tándrámɔt.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta ábhɨ́kɨ́re naŋa ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí árɛ̀m ntá Yesu, ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ ɛnɛn nɛ́ghɔ̀ pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p ɛ́kúti bhɔ mankɛm. Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú ndǔ nɛbháŋ ɛnɔ ɛ́ré rɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ yí tontó. Ghók ka yi!”
Mandɛm ayap nkwɔ́ ndɛ́ndɛ́mɛ́ bho abhɛn bǒ mmɨk bábyàk mbɔ bɛ bápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Akʉ nɔ́ bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bǒ mmɨk bákáysí bɛ́ bɔ́ kɛ̌ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnwɔp bɛ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ bhák yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mǔnti anɛ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi, anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Jáyrɔs atwɔ́ arɛ nkwɔ, nɛ ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, arɔk akwɛ́n yi bɛkak
Tɨk yɛ ka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghókó nɛ bǎkóŋo. Tɨ́k ká nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka, nɛ kɔ́ŋ ká mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ́kɔ́. Mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ ŋɛmɛ, chɔŋ ntwɔ́ ntá yɛka mbɔ ngɛ́p, nɛ bapu rɨŋɨ mpok anɛ mɛ́twɔ̀.
Bo abhɛn bákɛ́mɛ́ Yesu, básɔ́t yi barɔk ndǔ ɛkɛt Káyfas, Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Batɔŋ-ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báchɛ́mɛ́ nyaka arɛ.
Ndǔ bǎchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha, mɛmbɔŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ yɛ̌ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ́pú ɛnɛn nɛpu pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Kɛ mbák mmu ánkáysí bɛ mbɔk nɛnyíɛ́ nɛpu pɛ́pɛ́p, nɔ nɛ́pú bhak pɛ́pɛ́p ntá yi.
Bʉrɛ́ ká batɨ yɛka pɛ́pɛ́p, bɛ mpok bo básɔ̀kɔti bhe ɛ̌ti ɛrɨ́tí ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛka mbɔ bakoŋó Kristo, ntíánwɔ́p ánkɛm bɔ.
Ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn báchɔ́kɔ́ bákábhɛ́ Yesu bágháti yi bɛ, “Máyɛ nɛ bɔ̌mayɛ báchí nɛfí téé báyàŋ wɔ”.
Mbɔk báfú atú Fríjia, báchák atú Pamfília. Mbɔk báfú Íjip, báchák báfú ndǔ batáp ɛtɔk Líbia anɛ achi kɛkwɔt nɛ Sírene. Ndú abhɛn báfú Rom, mbɔk chi bo Israɛl, báchák bǒ abhɛn bákòŋo Mandɛm mbɔ bo Israɛl,
Mandɛm amɔt kɛ achi, nɛ yi achi Ɛtayɛsɛ mankɛm. Achí Mfɔ bɔ̌bhi mankɛm, áfʉ̀ɛt ntá yɛsɛ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhi nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nɛ bɔ̌bhi mankɛm.
Ángɛl wu arɛm yɛ ntá ya bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ amɨk. Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bo abhɛn mánáká bhɔ ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn.” Arɛm nkwɔ bɛ, “Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp. Bɛ́fu ntá Mandɛm.”
Mɛmbɔ̌ŋ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nɛ awɔ́ wa bɛ́ chɔŋ ńkwɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ barɛm amɛn Ɔnɛ́simɔs ákɛ̀m wɔ. Nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛrɛm bɛ ɔ̌kɛ̀m mɛ barɛm nkwɔ, nɛ barɛmɛ́ mɔ chi nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛ.
Bǒbatí bachiǎkap Mandɛm báchyɛ́ yí bɛtaŋ, nɛ atwɔ fá chi bɛ́kɛmti bǒbhɛ.”
nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛtaya árɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ, mɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛtaya. Nɛ nchí chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ ɛ̌ti bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n.
Mandɛm bo Israɛl ayap nyaka bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ akʉ nnɛrɛ́kɛt bǒ bhɛsɛ áchɨk mpok báchí mankɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Íjip. Mandɛm afɛrɛ bhɔ́ ndu kɛsɛm arɛ́ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bɛcha.
Mbák ɛchi nɔ́, chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mpok bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, nɛ ndu bɛ́ghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ ndu bɛ́tɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.”
nɛ Jáson asɔt bɔ́ afyɛ́ anywɔ́p. Bɔ́ mankɛm bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ bápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé mfɔ ngo anɛ Rom mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ Mfɔ achák áchí anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Yesu.”
Sɛ́ngɔ́ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋ ndu ɛ́chí. Puyɛ̌ bɛ sɛkɔŋ Mandɛm, kɛ chí bɛ́ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhɛsɛ kpát ató Mɔ́ywi mbɔ akap anɛ́ ápɔ́kɔ́ bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ, bɛ yi amfoŋori bhɛsɛ.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ sɛ́pú nu chi nɛ bakwǎŋwaŋ. Sɛ́nù chi nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí bɛfóŋó, nɛ bafɔ bhap, nɛ mɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ bɛchak. Sɛ́nù nkwɔ nɛ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ ndǔ mmɨk ɛjuri nɛ, nɛ sɛ́nù nɛ ngɛ́mtáy bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ amfay ndǔ mbʉ́ɛ́p.
Ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛsɛ́ mɛnkɛm bɛ sɛ́nkwáy bɛchyɛ bo abhɛn báchí ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛpɔptǐntɨ́. Nkúbhɛ́ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ ɛnɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ mpok ɛsɔŋɔri, kɛ nɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́nkwáy bɛchyɛ bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛpɔptǐntɨ́.
Ɛ́chí nyaka chi nywɔp ɛnɛn bo bátòŋti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt, nɛ ɛ́rɔp chi mandú bɛgháká ndǔ mpok anɛ Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt nɛ́bho.
Pɔ̌l are rɔ́ŋ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnap ankɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉiti nɛ bhɔ nɛ anu nɔkɔ bɛ bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn Grik mánóko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághàti bhɔ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Yesu átɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn, bárɨŋɨ bɛ atɛ̌m nɛkay ɛnɔ chi ɛ̌ti yap. Báre yaŋ bɛkɛm yi, kɛ ndu báchày bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchi arɛ, bárɔ́ yi bárɔ́k. 
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ́mɔ́t ɛnɛn nɛyá nkáp tontó, arɔk atí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyi, aku ntǎy bɛyǎ nkáp ɛnɔ.” 
Báre rɔ́ŋ ɛkɛrákap mámbɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm.
Ɛ́r mmɔ̌ Jóshua, Jóshua mmɔ̌ Ɛliɛ́sa, Ɛliɛ́sa mmɔ̌ Jórim, Jórim mmɔ̌ Mátat, Mátat mmɔ̌ Lɛ́vi,
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mpú pɛrɛ nyiɛ́ chɔŋ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ kpátɛ mpok Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bo mándɨŋɨ ntí ɛpǎ ɛnɛ, nɔ́ chi mpok yi ábhák Mfɔ bǒ mankɛm.”
Yesu aghati yɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Nɔ́ kɛ̌ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mmu ákɛ́ bhɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m ɛni bɛ chɔŋ nyiɛ́ yi, chɔŋ mfyɛ́ yi?
Yesu arɔ atú Táya, afʉɛ́t Sídɔn achwe atú bɛtok byo anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Dikápolis, akɔ achwɔp ndǔ Manyu Gálili.
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛka nɛ yi. Mánsɔkɔti nɔkɔ yi. Akwɛt ndɛn ɛ́nɛ ɛchi yi amʉɛt, arɛm bɛ, “Ntǔ bɛbʉ́ bhɛka arɔp nɛ bhe. Amɔya achi pɛ́pɛ́p. Nɛbho ɛchɔŋ ntɨ̌knsɛm ntá yɛka nɛ ndɔbhɛ rɔ́ŋ chí ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl.”
Ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk bɛ mpɔŋɔ baso ámfʉɛ́t ndǔ mbok mbíábhan ɛ́cha mǔnkáp bɛ́ka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi.”
Maníɛ́ ama ndǔ ndak anɛ chi bɛ: Mmíɛ́ ɛ́yú, bě kɛ̌ bǎyambɨ bɛchyɛ akap, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ be kɛ̌ bǎyámbɨ bɛbhɔŋ ɛkwak bɛkʉ nɔ.
Báchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ bɛyǎ akap. Nɛ mpok sɛ́fá bɛ́rɔŋ bachyɛ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛkwak bhɛsɛ ndu nɛkɔ ɛnɔ. 
Yesu arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ́ bárɛ̀m abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti brɛt anɛ bǎhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ? Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re jwimɛm-ɛ? Batɨ ábhʉɛ́t be amɛm chóchókó?
Mbák ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti barak anɛ́ áfàkari fá amɨk be kɛnókó, ná bǎkwáy mɛnoko mbák ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti barak anɛ áfàkari awu amfay?
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ aghati mɛ bɛ, ‘Faté sɛp dɔ́k nɛ bhɔ. Ɔ́kɛ́ fyɛ ntí bɛ́ bápú bo Israɛl.’ Bɔ̌mayɛsɛ abhɛn batí átándát abhɛn Jopa bákóŋo mɛ sɛ́rɔk Seséria, nɛ bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛ́chwe ɛkɛrɛ́ mmu wu Kɔnéliɔs.
Yesu abɨk ndɔŋ achak, arɔ ɛfóŋó yi awɔ́ Mandɛm.
Mbɔk bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Seséria barɔk nɛ bhɛsɛ́ básɔ́t bhɛsɛ́ ɛkɛt Násɔn mmǔ Sáyprɔs anɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́chɔ́kɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi. Násɔn áchi nyaka mmu amɔt anɛ áyámbɨ bɛbhak nkoŋo Yesu. 
Kɛ ntá Mɔ́ywi arɛm chi bɛ, “Ɛ̌ Mandɛm, kɛfɔ ɛkɛ kɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Mpok ɔ́kɛ̀m bǒbhɛ, ɔ́kʉ̀ nɔ ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchí chak.
Pú mmu ǎkwáy bɛku bɔ̌kɛnɛn bapay nɛ nkáp anɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ? Yɛ̌ nɔ́, yɛ̌ mɔ́sɛnɛn amɔt apú kway bɛkwɛn amɨk ɛnɛ́ Ɛtayɛka mmu achi amfay abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ.
Yesu atɔk yɛ amɨ́k ayap arɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́mbák nɛ bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ mǎnókó.”
Mbɔk bho básɔ̀t pú nɛ silbha nɛ batay ŋaŋaŋ bɛ́tée ɛkɛt ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɔ. Báchák básɔ̀t mɛnɔk nɛ tákɔ anɛ nnya ɛ́nyìɛ nɛ tákɔ anɛ nnya ɛ́bhʉ̀rɛ arɛ́ ndu bɛ́tée ɛkɛt ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɔ.
Sɛ́ghátí bhe Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mbɔ mmu ǎpɨ̀ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ. Ɛ́bɛp bɛ bě bho bǎbhɔ̀ŋ nsáy ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ mǎnchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak kɛ?
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ ɛnɔ ákwàŋ mbaŋ nɛ anjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ nsɛm, abhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbhak mǔbɛtok anɛ Mandɛm achi Mfɔ ywi.”
Mbɔ mɛmbɔŋ kɛ̌ njábhɛ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn, mbʉ́ ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ bo mánchyɛ́ mɛ́ akap ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhá. Kɛ mɛ̌kʉ̀ chí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm ayabhɛ mɛ, afyɛ́ bhɔ́ amɔya, nɛ mbɔŋ bɛkʉ bhɔ.
Ákɔ́rɛ́ ábhak chɔŋ ɛnyunɛ́ chi ápap mɔ́ywi anɛ mbakanɛm, mmɔ̌ anɛ mbakanɛm ampap ɛtayi, nnɔ ampap mɔ́ywi anɛ ngɔrɛ́, mɔ́ywi anɛ ngɔrɛ́ ampap nnɔ. Nnɔnɛ́m ampap ngɔrɛ́ mɔ́ywi, ngɔrɛ́ ampap nnɔnɛ́m ɛ́ywi.” 
Ɛ́chí yɛ́ bɛ mpok sɛ́ghàti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ, sɛ́pú kʉ nɔ chi nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn nɛ́fú ntá bakwǎŋwaŋ. Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ̌ ákʉ̀ sɛndiŋi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́rɛ̀m. Nɛ sɛ́gháti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm chi ntá bo abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɔ.
Bɛbhé mɛnkɛm bɛchɛm ndu ɛbhé ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ ɛpɔkɔ bɔ, nɛ yɔ ɛrɛm bɛ, “Kɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu mbɔ mmʉɛt yɛ.”
Yesu ágú ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ́ bɛ yi ánáŋ ántwɔ́, yɛ̌ sɛbhʉɛt chí pě, yɛ̌ sɛ́gǔ gu, sɛ́nkwáy bɛ́bhak nɛ yi.
Kɛ Mandɛm akɛka bɛ́ mpányu ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chi ɛ̌ti nɛwú Yesu Kristo Acha ndu ɛkotákátí. Ɛ̌ti nɛwú Yesu ndu ɛkotákátí. Mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk bɛrɔp ntá ya chi mbɔ bɛgú mɛnyɨŋ, nɛ mɛ ndɔp chi mbɔ ngú ntá mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́yàŋ chi bɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́kʉ̀, sɛ́ntɔ́ŋ bɛ sɛ́chí bǒ bɛtok Mandɛm tɛtɛp. Sɛ́bhɔŋ maŋák mpoknkɛm. Sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu, yɛ̌ nɔ sɛ́bhɔŋ maŋák mpoknkɛm.
Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ báte ɛyu ndu bɛway yi. Afa, arɔk ɛbhak ɛ́chák. Bɛyǎ bho bákóŋo yi, abú bo mankɛm abhɛn mámè.
Ángɛl akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ántwɔ́ ntá yɛ, nɛ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm Acha mɛ́nkʉ ɔ́mpɔkɔ mɛniɛ. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mmɔ́ anɛ ɔ́bhe, ǎbhák nyáŋá nɛ mámbɨŋɨ yi bɛ, ‘Mmɔ Mandɛm.’
Aghók ɛ̌ti Yesu. Ɛ́kʉ atɔti amɛm bɛyǎ bho kpát arɔk, atɔk nkokoŋ nkú yi.
Ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt ajɛt tɛ́mté arɔk asɔt ɛkuchá fofok asɛbhɛ ndǔ ɛchyɛ́ mmɛ́m, asɔt akpaŋ anti mɔ́nɔk, asá amfay ntá Yesu, bɛchyɛ yi anyu.
Yesu arɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákári nɛ yí. Afú ndǔ nkwɔ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, atɛ́n mmʉɛt ambɨ arɛm bɛ, “Agha bǎyáŋ?”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bɔ́ŋ ká nɛka nɛ Mandɛm.
Nɛ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnɔk ɛ́nyu chi bɛbɛ́ptí kɛpɛm, ɛ́pú kwáy mɛ́nyú bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm.
Kɛ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká mǎmbɔ mantwɔ ntá ya, bǎkɛ́ chyɛt bhɔ mbi mbɔnyunɛ bǒ abhɛn bachi mbɔ bhɔ kɛ̌ Mandɛm ábhak Mfɔ awap.”
Nkoŋo Yesu amɔt achi nyaka Damáskɔs anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Ananías. Aghɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k ántífú ndu Yesu Acha abhɨŋɨ yí bɛ, “Ananías.” Aka arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ.”
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Acha ayap bakoŋo bhi bachak bɛsa bɛrat nsɛm byo nɛ apay ató ambɨ bati apay apay bɛ mándɔ́k ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yí mbɔ̌ŋ áyàŋ nyaka bɛrɔŋ.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́k ɛtɔk Kapɛ̌naum. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, Yesu arɔk téé ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyap abho bɛtɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kwak bɛ mǔbɛtok Mandɛm ánkwáy ndǔ yɛntɨkɨ mbi nɛ bɛ ámbɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yàŋ ndu bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ bɛtɨk.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mmu achí fá anɛ áchá ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm.
Atɔŋ mɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu yɛ̌ndu nchí chí mmɔ̌bɛtok ywi nɛ mpú yɛ̌nyɨŋ! Nɛbho nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ mkpáká bho ɛnkɛm mámbɨŋɨ mɛ bɛ, ‘Ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ɛyi ɛrɨ ɛcha!’
Nɛ mbák ɛ́mfákárí ɛnyu yɔ, chi-bɛtɨk ǎtɛmsi yi sayri, antɛ́n yi ándɔ́k ámbák nɛ bǒ bɛtábhá, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ́ ámɛ́n.”
Abho nɛ abhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ bhɔ ndǔ bɛtɨk nkárɛ́nká ɛtay beku, achyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ wap nkáp nywɔp nɛmɔt ankɛm.
Básɨŋ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́fu amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm Acha, nkwǎŋwaŋ chí agha anɛ ɔ́re kaysi yi? Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm chi agha anɛ ɔ́re fyɛ ntí nɛ yi?
Nɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ chí Ɛfóŋó yi yímbɔŋ, puyɛ̌ chí ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛ́fú fá amɨk. Mandɛm ato bhɛsɛ Ɛfóŋó yi bɛ Ɛ́fóŋó yi ankwak sɛndiŋi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhi.
Yesu aghati Matá bɛ, “Chɔŋ mɔ́mayɛ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu anɛ áchí ndǔ bɛtɨk nɛ ǎnù bɛ mǔnti ywi ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ yi, apú fyɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ baraká ɛtɔk áchák.
Achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ ntá mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bɛ́ ámfyɛ́ Pɔ̌l anywɔ́p, mambabhɛri nɔkɔ yi, kɛ ámbɔ́ŋ ngangaŋ mandú. Nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ kaŋ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bɛrɔŋ bɛghɔ yi nɛ bɛchyɛ yi nɛkwak. 
Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi bárɔ́k baghaka Kapɛ̌naum. Ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ báchí arɛ, babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti abhɛn ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bárɔ́k ntá Píta bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ ywɛka ǎchyɛ̀ nkábhɛ́nti anɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm-ɛ?”
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, abhesi ntá ya nkwɔ, mmɛ mmu nchí mbɔ mmɔ̌ anɛ bábhé ndu mpok anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhakantɨ bɛ chɔŋ mámbe yi.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chi bɛkɔŋ batɨ, nɛ bɛrɛm chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti Mandɛm bɛ sɛ́ngo nɔkɔ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi kpátɛ sɛ́ndɔp chi mbɔ Kristo mmu achi ntí ntá Nkwɔ Kristo.
Nɛ ngɔ́ ɛtaŋtí ángɛl Mandɛm ndu árɛ̀m nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Agha ǎkway bɛfɛrɛ ɛ́bhánɛ́ ɛnɛ́, anɛnɛ ɛkáti ɛnɛ?”
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bayambɨ bátwɔ́ kɛ mɛ̌twɔ̀, chí baghɛ́p nɛ baghɛ́p bataŋ bataŋ. Baghɔŋɔmɛn ábhɨ́kɨ́ ghók bhɔ.
Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Acha, mbák chí wɔ, chyɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ bɛ nsɛ́p anyɛ́n, nkɔ, ntɛmɛri wɔ.”
Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l bárɔk mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ átó bhɔ. Bárɔ́k Sɛlusia básɔt achwǐnyɛ́n anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ndǔ ɛtɔk nɛ́ntɨ́nyɛn ɛnɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ Sáyprɔs.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, puyɛ̌ Moses kɛ áchyɛ́ nyaka bachǐmbɨ bhɛka nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay. Ɛtaya kɛ áchyɛ̀ bhe nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn mbɔŋ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fú amfay.
Bǒ abhɛn bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ wɔ bábè nyaka ntɨ nɛ wɔ. Kɛ mpok akway anɛ ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɔ ɛbhɛ bɛběntɨ. Mpok akway anɛ ɔ́tàŋ bo abhɛn bagú. Mpok akway anɛ ɔ́kap bǒ bɛtok bhɛ, ɔ́nkap barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bǒbhɛ mankɛm, ɔ́nkap bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ wɔ kɛnókó, yɛ̌ chi ndɛ́ndɛmɛ bho, yɛ̌ chi manɛm bho, mpok akway anɛ ɔ́nàŋa nɛ bo abhɛn báwày batɨ fá amɨk.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛriŋɨ mpok anɛ Ɛta afyɛ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛmfakari. Ɛta mmu afyɛ́ mpok ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi kɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́.
Táytɔs, ɔ́chí mɔ́wa mbɔnyunɛ ɔbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu mbɔ mɛ. Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛta nɛ Yesu Kristo Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ mántɔŋ wɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu, manchyɛ wɔ kpák. 
Achɔ́ŋtí bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhé Moses mɛnkɛm. Mbɔk bɛbhé bɛbhak ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo babhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ. Bɛchak bɛkóŋo bɛpɨŋɨ́tɔk. Akʉ́ ɛnyuyɔ bɛ bakwɔ́ bho apay andɔp chi nkwɔ amɔt, nɔ chi, nkwɔ bo bakɔ abhɛn Mandɛm ábhárɛ́ nɛ yi. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ yi akʉ kpák ámbák nɛntɨ bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl.
Kɛ kɛ́yɛnti sɛnta ɛkɛrákap. Dɔ̌ nɛbhʉɛt wu, mbɔnyunɛ bárɔ yi ambak ntá bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm. Nɛ chɔŋ bɔ́bhɔ mánjati ɛtɔk Mandɛm   nɛ bɛtaŋ ndǔ bataŋ bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm apay.
Kɛ Páílet abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́ptí ndak yi ákʉ́?” Bɔ́ mankɛm bápɛ́t bábhó bɛ́bɨ́k bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!”
Ɛta mmu achi nɛpɛ́m kɛ átó mɛ, nɛ ɛ̌ti yi kɛ nchí nɛpɛ́m. Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ, mmǔ anɛ ányìɛ mɛ ǎbhák nɛpɛ́m ɛ̌ti ya.
Ndu Mandɛm achyɛ nɔ bhe nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛkɔ, fɛrɛ́ ká barak abʉ́abʉ ankɛm antɨ. Bǎkɛ́ pɛrɛ sénse, dɔ̌ ká bɛtábhá, dɔ̌ ká mpabhamɨ́k, nɛ dɔ̌ ká bɛrɛm barak abʉ́abʉ ɛ̌ti bho ndu bɛchɔŋti manyɛ́n ayap.
Mpok mɛnyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ bo Israɛl arɔp kɛkwɔt. Bɛyǎ bho báfa ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk bhap bako, barɔk Yerúsalɛm ɛnɛ́ mpok ɛpǎ ɛyɔ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re ghaka, ndu bɛkʉ bɛ mámbák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyu bo Israɛl bákʉ nɔkɔ nyaka.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bɔ̌mayi bátó ɛyɔŋ ntá Yesu Acha bɛ, “Acha, mmʉɛrɛ ywɛ anɛ ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ ǎme.”
Símiɔn aghɔ nɔkɔ mɔ̌rɛ́ asɔt yi akɛ́m amɔ abɨti Mandɛm bɛ́:
Yí kɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m nyaka ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, ‘Mmǔ ǎtwɔ̀ mɛ ansɛm anɛ acha mɛ mbɔnyunɛ bápɛrɛ bhe mɛ, yi achi.’
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu ándɛ́m bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ kway, ansɛt nkwɛrɛ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ ɛnyǔ nɛsɛptímʉɛt ɛnɛn nɛ́pú tɛtɛp, nɛ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó ntá bɔángɛl. Bǒbhɔ bápà bɛ Mandɛm ǎtɔ̀ŋ bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k anti fúú, nɛ báyòŋ mmʉɛt ndɛ́ndɛm. Nkaysi yap achí chí anɛ bǒ mmɨk.
Bámák batɨ̌ bawǎnsi abhɛn bachi ndǔ áchwí achak nɛ awɔ bɛ mántwɔ mánkwak bhɔ. Bárɔ́k bachɛm nɛ bhɔ, bafɛrɛ nsi báfyɛ́ amɛm bachwi apay kpát ábhó bɛbɛt.
Kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ, sɛ́chí bo nsay nɛ nchɛbhɛ manyiɛp mɛnyu nɛ ndɛn bɛfyɛ amʉɛt. Sɛ́chí bǒ mantɛm, nɛ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ mmu ywɛsɛ ábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ ɛyi ɛ́pú.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm, báré nywinti, nɛ bábhɛ́p bakoŋo Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí mǎnyìɛ mǎnyu nɔkɔ nɛ babhɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛntí nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak?”
“Dɔ́k ká amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, mǎnte, mǎngati bo yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛn.”
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ nsɛm anɛ Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ apɛt apú nsɛm bɛsí Mandɛm. Mbɔnyunɛ abhat mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha, nɛ apɛt apú ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ mmu anɛ ápú nsɛm fá amɨk, ndǔ Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ yí, arɔp chí nsɛm Yesu Kristo.
Kristo ákʉ́ nɔ bɛ bo mankɛm abhɛn yi áchyɛ́ batí bɛtɨk ayɔ, mánkwak bo Mandɛm bɛ mánkwáy bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhi ɛnyu ɛnɛ mmʉɛt Kristo átaŋ andɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
Mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛbhak awu nɛ bhe nɛ́nɛ bɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyu nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, mbɔnyunɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛrɛm. 
Ɛyɔ ɛkʉ bɛ tɛ ndiɛrɛ nɛwú, bǎkɛ́ pɛrɛ ŋwaka bɛkʉ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒ mmɨk bábhɔ̀ŋ ɛkwak arɛ. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkwak chí bɛ́kóŋo nkaysi Mandɛm.
Kɛ mmu anɛ átì mɛ achí fá chɔkɔ ǎnyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ mɛ.
BɔPíta bachwɔp nɔkɔ Samária, bare nɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ántwɔ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko Yesu.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛ́chák ntɨ ɛni kɛ ansɔt brɛt nɛ nkɔ́p Acha.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ bɛyǎ bo báfù chɔŋ bɛbhě mɛnkɛm mántwɔ manchɔkɔ nɛ Ábraham nɛ Áisek nɛ Jekɔ́p ndǔ mɛnyiɛ ɛpǎ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛrɛ kɛfɔ mfay.
kpátɛ nkʉ bǒmpap abhɛ mámbak mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɔ́chɔkɔ ɔ́nyaŋa bɛkak arɛ́.”’
Bo abhɛn bárɔ̀ŋ ambɨ báré sayti yi bɛ ánchɔ́kɔ́ kpák; kɛ akpɨk are bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋɛtaŋ bɛ, “Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít! Ghɔ́ mɛ́ ntínso!”
Bɛ́kwɛn amɔ́ Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́cháy.
Stífin arɛm bɛ, “Ghók ka! Ngɔ ndǔ mánɛ́nɛ́ mbǐnywɔp ɛtɔkɔ́ mfay, Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm abhak téé ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm.”
kpát bɛ́gháka nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi akó amfay. Ápɛ́rɛ ko amfay, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ yi angati bo abhɛn yi ayabhɛ bɛ mámbák bǒnto bhi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ babhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ.
Afa yɛ arɛ́, arɔk achɔkɔ ɛkɛt mmu amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Títiɔs Jɔ́stɔs. Jɔ́stɔs abhak mmǔ anɛ áchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ɛkɛrɛ yi ɛ́bhák kɛkwɔt nɛ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl.
Pɔ̌l arɛm chi bɛ, “Mbák chí nkaysi Mandɛm chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm fá ntá yɛka.” Arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, arɔ bhɔ achwe áchwí bare rɔŋ.
Mpok anɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu árɔ́ árɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛtɔk, bakoŋo Yesu báré nɨk yí mmʉɛt bɛ́ “Ntɔŋ, nnyiɛ́ mbɔ nɛnyíɛ́.”
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ chí mpok anɛ nchí ɛtɔk Tɛsalónika ɛnɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́re rɔ atú ɛtɔk ɛyɛká Masidónia, be bǎtó mɛ nkáp, puyɛ̌ chí ndɔŋ amɔt, kɛ ndɔŋ ɛ́páy, mpok mɛnyɨŋ bɛtaŋa mɛ amʉɛt.
Mǔmpap anɛ Mandɛm ánaŋa chɔŋ ndǔ ngwɛnti chi nɛwú.
Bádɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́ sayri, bágʉɛ́p bhɔ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bágháti mmu anɛ ábhàbhɛri ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ bɛ́ ánsɔ́t mpok bɛ́ bákɛ́ bʉɛ.
Mpú rɔ bɛ́fyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ njɛt téé tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, mbɔ́ŋ nsáy. Nsáy yɔ achí bɛ Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ ntwɔ bɛ mbak amfay nɛ yi ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo mmu ágú ɛ̌ti ya.
Nɛ́ chi nku anɛ mɛ̌nyú chɔŋ nɛ bo Israɛl ndǔ manywɔp anɛ átwɔ̀. Mmɛ Acha nchí rɛm bɛ chɔŋ mfyɛ́ bɛbhé ɛbha bɔ́ antí, nsɨŋ bhɔ amɛm batɨ yap. Chɔŋ mbak Mandɛm awap, nɛ bɔ mámbak bǒbha.
Hága chi njiɛ Sináy amɛm ɛtɔk Arébia. Nɛ Hága até mbɔ Yerúsalɛm anɛ manywɔp anɛ ɛchɔŋ, mbɔnyunɛ achi nyaka ndǔ kɛsɛm nɛ bɔ̌bhi.
Áfɔ́k wu achí yɛ chi ntá bo abhɛn básiɛ̀p bhɔ, kɛ ntá bo abhɛn bapu syɛp bhɔ nkwɔ? Sɛ́rɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mandɛm asɔt nyaka bɛ Ábraham achi chak bɛsí bhi mpok yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ yi.”
Áchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, arɔk achwe ɛkɛt Sakaría, akaka Ɛlísabɛt;
“Mbák ɔ́mfóŋórí bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ wɔ bɛbʉ́, chɔŋ Ɛtayɛ Mandɛm mmu áchí amfay nkwɔ amfoŋori wɔ.
Sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́ré fʉɛt chi ansɛm mɔ́kpɔkɔ́ mmɨk anɛ ate nnyɛ́n. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Kaúda. Mmɨkɨ yɔ achɛ́t mbʉ́ɛ́p mandú. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kwák bhɛsɛ, sɛ́nú sɛya áchwí nɨŋɨnɨŋɨ anɛ achi anɛt áchwí bɛ ákɛ́ rakati ansɛm áchwí.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ Yesu arɔk amɛm baso bɛ Satan amɔ yi.
Nnáŋ nkʉ ntɨ bɛ ɛ́chí sayri bɛto Ɛpafrodáytɔs ámpɛ́tnsɛm awu ntá yɛka. Ɛpafrodáytɔs mmu bǎtó bɛ ántwɔ́ ankwak mɛ mɛnu mbɔ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu ndu bɛtɨk Yesu chí nkoŋo Yesu nkwɔ́ mbɔ mɛ.
Mandɛm Acha Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm ǎrɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi nɛbhʉɛt achak amɛm Ɛkáti ɛyi bɛ,“Chɔŋ mbak Ɛtayɛka, mǎmbak bɔ̌bha.”
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápú rɛm kpóŋóróŋ bɛ Yesu atwɔ nyaka fá amɨk mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ, ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛ́bhak nɛ yi ɛpu fu ntá Mandɛm. Ɛnyu mmu wu ǎbhɔŋ chi ɛfóŋó mǔmpap Kristo anɛ bǎghòk nyaka bɛ ǎtwɔ̀ fá amɨk, nɛ anáŋ achi fá amɨk nɛ́nɛ.
Pɔ̌l árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɔt brɛt anɨkmʉɛt achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm bɛsí bhap mankɛm, abɔ́k abho mɛ́nyiɛ́.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛsɛ abhɔŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bǒnkwɔ mámbɔ́ŋ maŋák ndǔ bɛkwak bhɔ bɛ mángó ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛn bábhɔŋɔ nɛ Mandɛm.
Mǔnti chí mmu anɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́pu nɛ yi, abhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ chi ngɔrɛ́ amɔt, chí mmu anɛ bɔ̌bhi mánókó nɛ mmu apú kwáy bɛ́ji bhɔ́ bɛ́ bábhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ kɛnókó nɛ máyap nɛ ɛtayap.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛ́kwɛ́n be amʉɛt, nchí nɨkmʉɛt nkaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛká!
Kɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛrɨ bábhɔŋ kɛnɛ́m nɛ kɛnókó nɛ kpák. Ɛ́bhàk ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛbho nɛ bo Israɛl bɛghaka amʉɛt bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ sɛ́fú ndǔ nɛwú sɛ́chwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́kɔŋ batɨ bǒnkwɔ. Mmǔ anɛ ábhɨkɨ kɔŋ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ abhʉɛ́t ndǔ nɛwú.
Mandɛm atɛ́msí bo ɛtɔk Bábilɔn mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ kɛ báwáy barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bo Mandɛm bachak mankɛm. Manoŋ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm abhɛn bɔ baway achí bɔ anti.”
Bɛsɛ mankɛm nkwɔ sɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka mbɔ bhɔ, sɛ́nkoŋo nɔkɔ chi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ nɛ batɨ̌ yɛsɛ áŋwàka bɛ sɛnkʉ. Ndǔ ntee ayɛsɛ yɔ, Mandɛm abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɛ́msí mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak ndu ábé nyaka ntɨ tontó ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́.
Bɛ́yɨŋɨ yɛ ndak anɛ, nchí ghati beka bɛ mǎndɔ́ bǒbhɛn, bǎkɛ́ kʉ bhɔ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Mbák nkaysi-nɛ, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ batɨ̌ bɛkʉ bɛfu chí ntá nkwǎ, chɔŋ mánkwɛn.
Ɔ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛ́kʉ nɛ bɛchákárí mbok ɛ̌ti bachǐmbɨ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú ka mmu ánchyɛ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Fíɛ́ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ nɛmbak mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyaŋ.
Kɛ Píta akɛm yí ndu awɔ, bɛ yí amfate, arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ nkwɔ́ nchí chí nkwǎ mbɔ wɔ.”
Mmǔ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ ánáŋ áchí nyaka amɨk ndǔ nɛme mamiɛ́ ɛsǎ nsɛm nɛku nɛ arat.
Cháá! Bághátí mɛ́ ɛpúsí ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛká. Nɛ ɛnyǔ ɛpúsí ɛnɛ, yɛ̌ chí bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mandɛm bápú kwáy bɛ́ká bɛ ɛ́mbák ndǔ nkwɔ́ wap. Mmu áre bhʉrɛ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ɛ́táyi ná?
Chɔŋ ansɔt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́pti ɛnyɨŋ bɛrwɔ bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ mbi nɛwú. Chɔŋ ankʉ nɔ ndu bábhɨkɨ ka bɛkɔŋ tɛtɛp anɛ áyɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu Kristo bɛ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Ɛyɔ ɛnkʉ yi anchyɛ ntɛ́msí ntá bo mankɛm abhɛn bábhɨkɨ noko tɛtɛp anɛ ayɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu, kɛ bakɔŋ bɛkʉ chí bɛbʉ́.
Bě bho bǎpú bo Israɛl, bǎkɛ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyǔ bǎchí nyaka ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm. Bo Israɛl básyɛp bho, nɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ mmʉɛt yap bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bǎsyɛphɛ bho nɛ bǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bɛ, bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ syɛp bhɔ.”
Bǒbatí nɛ bǒtɔk bághók nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, batí átáka bhɔ amɛm.
Su nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ ká bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛká ntá batɨ, mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ámbú bo abhɛn mámè. Nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt mmu anɛ áchí chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ́bhɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ.
Píta arɨŋɨ yɛ bɛ́ tɛtɛp yí afuu ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, arɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́nɛ, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ tɛtɛp bɛ́ Mandɛm ato ángɛl aywi ántwɔ́ ámfɛ́rɛ́ mɛ́ amɔ Hɛ́rɔd nɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo Israɛl batɨ bɛ́kʉ mɛ.”
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́ghàti bhe ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo Acha bɛ bǎkɛ́ chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ yɛntɨkɨ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ anɛ ábhɔ̀t abhɔt kɛbháká koŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́tɔ́ŋ be.
Píta nɛ bǒnto Yesu mankɛm bakɛmɛ bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛghok chi Mandɛm, puyɛ̌ nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Ɛ́kʉ́ ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛ́móko, bábhó bɛ́rɔŋ ntá Yesu.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bakɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bo abhɛn ɛyap ɛrɨ ɛcha chi abhɛn bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ mánkʉ nɔkɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́yàŋ!” 
Ɛ́bhák chí mbɔ bájwítí bhɔ́ amɛm nɛbháŋ nɛ amɛm Manyu, bɛ́ mámbat mmʉɛt nɛ Moses mǔnti wap.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt mbɔ mǎmbɔ, yí wu kɛ ákway bɛchwe ndǔ kɛfɔ̌ mfay.” 
Eghorǐ manyiɛp ɛ́pɛ́rɛ twɔ ndǔ mpok Nóa, bo mányìɛ̀ nyaka mányu nɔkɔ, nɛ mámbay nɔkɔ babhay, nɛ mántoko nɔkɔ bɔ, kpátɛ mpok anɛ Nóa áchwe amɛm ɛrɛmɛ́ áchwí anɛ Mandɛm ághátí nyaka Nóa ángókó.
Akʉ mɛ̌mbák mmǔ bɛtok Yesu Kristo ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mbɔ nchiakap anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm. Nchí ghati bhɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm bɛ́ mánókó yi, nɛ bɛ mámbák mbɔ akap anɛ yi áká bɛ́sɔt nɛ anɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ábhʉ́rɛ́ nyáŋá ntá yi.
andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Acha, mmɔ̌bɛtok awa achí anywɔ́p bɨ́ŋɨ́rí nɛ bɛyǎ bɛbe.”
Aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nkáp ankɛm wu amʉɛt. Mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbhǎ nɛkɔ ánsɔ́t yɔ. Anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ akparɛnja, ántí ndɛ́ yi anku akparɛnja.
Aghati mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ wu bɛ ‘Yɨŋɨ́, ndǔ mamiɛ́ árát nchí twɔ bɛyaŋ kɛpɛm ndǔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ, kɛ mpu ghɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Kpɔ́t yɔ́ gʉ́ɛ́p amɨk! Ɛ́kʉ̀ kpɨ́k yi fá téé, ɛ́nchɛt nɔkɔ mmɨk ndɛ́ndɛm?’
Ndaká yí ɛ́bemʉɛt ntá yɛ̌chi mmǔ ywɛka amɔt mɛnoko bɛ Mandɛm ǎkway bɛkʉ bawú mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m?
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ nkwɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnɛ́m abhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ ngɔrɛ́ ywi mbɔ mmʉɛt yi. Mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ŋ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ǎkɔ̀ŋ chi mmʉɛt yi.
Nɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bo abhɛn babhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu ndǔ nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu. Bǒ mbɨ chí abhɛn yi áchyɛ́ akap bɛbhak bǒnto Yesu. Abhɛn bákòŋo chí bo abhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ akap bɛ́gháti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛfu ntá yi. Abhɛn bapɛt bákòŋo chí abhɛn yi áchyɛ akap bɛ́tɔŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Ǎchyɛ̀ báchák akap bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay, abhɛ́nɛ́fú anchyɛ akap bɛ́bu bǒmame, báchák akap bɛ́kwak bho. Ǎchyɛ̀ abhɛnɛfu akap bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ bɛkɛm bo sayri. Achyɛ bachak akap bɛrɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛ́n bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
antɛ́n bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ɛyi, antɛn mmɛ́n ɛbhě awɔghɔ.
Píta ayibhiri mmʉɛt aghɔ́ nkoŋo anɛ Yesu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ ndu ákòŋo bhɔ́ ansɛm. Nkoŋo wu kɛ ághɔ́kɔ́ nyaka amʉɛt Yesu mpok mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́, nɛ yí wu kɛ ábhɛ́bhɛ́ nyaka Yesu bɛ, “Acha, agha áti chɔŋ wɔ?”
Ɛ́chí nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Mmǔ anɛ anókó mɛ, manyiɛp amɛn áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ǎfu yi antɨ ansɛp nɔkɔ mbɔ nyɛ́n.’”
Pɔ̌l asɛp yɛ amɨk akuri akɛ́m yí nɛ amɔ́ ápáy abhɛnɛ, arɛm bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ cháy, achí nɛpɛ́m”.
Ngɔ yɛ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨ́k anɛ achi bɛ̌mm nɛ nnyɛ́n mmǔ anɛ ákɔ̀ yɔ nɛ́bhak bɛ Nɛwú, nɛ Ɛtɔkɔ́ Bawú ɛnkoŋo nɔkɔ yi ansɛm. Báchyɛ Nɛwú nɛ Ɛtɔkɔ́ Bawú bɛtaŋ bɛ mánsɔt nɛnu, nɛ nsay, nɛ ɛghorǐ nɛme, nɛ nnya mběmbe ɛnɛ fá mmɨk mángwáy bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́mɨk ɛ́mɔt ndu bɛbhɔkɔ mmɨk mɛnkɛm mɛnwi.
Are tɔ́ŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl, nɛ bo báré chyɛ yi kɛnókó. 
Chɔŋ bɛtɔk mɛ́nu nɛ bɛtɔk bɛ́chák, bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk mánu nɛ batɨ̌ bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk nɛ chɔŋ mmɨk anyɨkɨsi ndǔ bɛyǎ bɛbhak, nsay ankwɛ́n ɛtɔk. Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi mbɔ nɛbhǒnɛt ɛnɛn bɛbe ntá ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ánòŋsi.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok ayɔ, nnɛ́m nkɔk akók ndɔŋ anɛ́ ajwí ɛ́pay. Píta atɨk ndǔ Yesu ághátí yi bɛ, “Nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kók ndɔŋ ɛpay, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛrat bɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ.” Agbɔkɔ kɛbhɔ, are di.
Nɛ yɛ̌ndu nɛme ɛna nɛchyɛ nyaka bhe bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, bǎbhɨkɨ byak mɛ. Bǎsyɛpti mɛ mbɔ ángɛl Mandɛm, mbɔ bɛ nchí chi Yesu Kristo.
Bo bákʉ manoŋ bo Mandɛm nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm arɔŋ amɨk. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ɔ́chyɛ́ bhɔ́ manoŋ mányu. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kway nɛ bhɔ”.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l mǔnto Yesu Kristo kɛ nchí sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Puyɛ̌ bakwǎŋwaŋ kɛ báyábhɛ́ mɛ, nɛ puyɛ̌ nkwǎ kɛ átó mɛ. Chi Yesu Kristo nɛ Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ mmu akʉ Yesu ampɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
Mmǔ anɛ ájɛ́t ntiɛt nɛ batɨ, apú kway bɛbhɔŋ nsáy mbák abhɨkɨ jɛt ankoŋo bɛbhé ntiɛt.
Aka bɛkʉ nɔ yɛ̌ndu Áisek ɛ́rɛ kɛ̌ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka Ábraham bariɛp ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, “Áisek kɛ achi mmɔ́ anɛ ákʉ chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ.”
Ɔkʉ mɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mbi nɛpɛ́m. Ndǔ ɔ́chí nɛ mɛ mpoknkɛm, chɔŋ ɔ́nkʉ mɛmbɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák.”
Mmu anɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ mánkɛ́m yi, chɔŋ mánkɛm. Mmu anɛ áwày bho nɛ akparɛnja, chɔŋ mángwáy yi nɛ akparɛnja. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, bo Mandɛm babhɔŋ bɛ́tée kpirí nɛ mándɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ ndǔ nɛka ɛnap nɛ Yesu.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n áchák anɛ́ ápú ndǔ nkwɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ. Mbɔŋ bɛ́sɔt yɔ́ nkwɔ, ntwɔ́ nɛ yɔ, bɛ́ ánchɛ́m mmʉɛt nɛ anɛ́fú. Chɔŋ ánkoŋo ɛyɔŋ ɛya. Ɛnkʉ yɔ́ ankɛm ámbak ndǔ nkwɔ́ ámɔt anɛ́ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n amɔt.
Aghati yɛ̌ bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm ghati nɔkɔ ká Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá bǒ mankɛm.
Nɛ mbák ɛ́nyu kɛpɛm mmíɛ́ mbúrɛ́ ɛ́ndɨ, kɛ mbák ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ nyu kɛpɛm, ɔ̌kwáy bɛghati mɛ mkpɔt yɔ ngʉɛp amɨk.’” 
Nchi yaŋ yɛ̌ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bǒnkwɔ báchɛ́mɛ́, babhakanɛm abhɛn báchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap ntá Mandɛm mánsá amɔ anɛ achi pɛ́pɛ́p amfay mánɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt kɛbhɔŋ bɛběntɨ nɛ bɛ́táŋá nɛ batɨ.
Ghatí bǒ bakáp fá ammɨk bɛ bákɛ́ yoŋ mmʉɛt, nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ bhakantɨ ndǔ kɛfɔ̌ mmɨk, mbɔnyunɛ kɛ́fʉ̀ɛrɛ fʉɛt. Ghatí bhɔ́ mánsɨ́kɨ́ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ sɛ́mbɔŋ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɔnéliɔs abhak mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́ baraká Mandɛm nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ nyaka Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm. Abhak mmu anɛ ánɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mpoknkɛm, anchyɛ nɔkɔ bɛyǎ nɛkwak ntá bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi bachɛ́bhɛ́bho.
Mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ yɨŋɨ chi ndiɛrɛ mmʉɛt yi. Abhɔŋ bɛ́fyɛ́ ntí nɛ batɨ nkwɔ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku, bo báré sɔt bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ mándɔk nɔkɔ ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ. Yesu are sɔt chí ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛyi amboko nɔkɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ mɛ́ndɔ́ bho, nɛ ambu nɔkɔ bǒmame.
Ngɔrɛ́ nɛkɔ amɔt anɛ achi nyaka ɛtɔk ɛyɔ, ághók bɛ Yesu ǎnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi wu. Asɔt ɛ́kpɛ́mɛ́ bawɛrɛ́riɛp arɔk arɛ́ nɛ yɔ.
Ndǔ mpok yɔ, Yesu afú Násárɛt atú Gálili arɔk Jɔ̌n ajwiti yi ndǔ Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan.
“Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásìɛpti mandú mɔ mbɔ anɛ́, ɛ̌ti ya, ǎsìɛpti chí mɛ.
Abho bɛ́rɛ́m bɛbɛptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm, nɛ ɛ̌ti nnyɛ́n Mandɛm nɛ ɛ̌ti nɛbhʉɛt bɛ́chɔkɔ Mandɛm nɛ ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bachi amfay.
Mmu anɛ akɔŋ bo, apú fɛrɛ ntɨ nɛ bo abhɛn bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́, ápú rɔ bɛ́fyɛ ntí nɛ bo mpoknkɛm, ápú rɔ bɛbhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛmbak sayri, nɛ ǎte kpirí ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Nokó ka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí bhe bɛ́ nchí babhat nɛ Ɛtaya nɛ Ɛtaya achi babhat nɛ mɛ. Mbák bápú kway mɛnoko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌rɛ̀m, nokó ká ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Ɛnɛ́ bárɛ̀m nɔ ɛ̌ti yi, mbɔŋ Yesu abhesi bɛsí bhap! Arɛm bɛ, “Kpák ámbák nɛ bhe.”
Bǎkɛ́ ŋwaka ndǔ barak ɛ́pusi, kɛkɛ́m mmʉɛt mbɔ bo abhɛn babhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
Yímbɔŋ ápɔ́kɔ́ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ mɛnkɛm amʉɛt ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Akʉ nɔ bɛ sɛ́ndɔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ sɛ́mbak chak. Bɛfʉɛt ɛbhɛ́n báfyɛ́ yi amʉɛt bɛ́bǔ bhe.
Yesu arɔk nɛpakámʉɛt ɛni akɛ́m yí ndu awɔ́ akwak yí afate achɔkɔ chɔ́kɔ́. Mbʉ́ɛ́p wu ámáy. Abho mɛne bhɔ.
Bɔ́ŋ ká maŋák yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ ɛ́fákárí nɔ́ nɛ bhe, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm abhʉ́rɛ́ ɛrɛm ákap ntá yɛka awu amfay. Nchí ghati bhe mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ bachǐmbɨ bhap bǎchyɛ̀ nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm ɛsɔŋɔri.
Bǒbatí bhɛka mánkóŋó mɛ Seséria nɛ mbák yi abhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ chɔŋ mǎndɛm bɛsí ɛbha arɛ́.”
Ɛ́rɨ bɛ ɔ́nkʉ́ bɛrɨ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ nɛ chɔŋ Ɛtayɛ Mandɛm mmu ághɔ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ákʉ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ankap wɔ.” 
Bakoŋó Jɔ̌n Njwiti nɛ abhɛn nkwɔ Fárisi báchí nyaka ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay mpokófu. Mbɔk bho bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ndaká yí bakoŋó Jɔ̌n Njwiti nɛ abhɛn nkwɔ Fárisi bátarɛ nɔkɔ nsay, kɛ babhɔk abhɛ bápu kʉ nɔ?”
Nchí ghati bhe nɔ́ nɛ ntí bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǒ mmɨk básɔ̀t mbɔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak chí ɛchɨŋti bɛsí Mandɛm. Ɛ́chí nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mbɔk bo bákáysí bɛ́ báchí barɨŋɨ́ndak. Kɛ nkúbhɛ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnap kɛ̌ Mandɛm ásɔ̀t bɛ́dɛ́p bɔ́ amɨk.”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn bátòŋti mmʉɛt mɛnyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, Páílet arɛm ntá bo Israɛl bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ ka Mfɔ ywɛka nɛ!”
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ maŋɔk nywɔp arat, ngɔrɛ́ Ananías achwe anywɔ́p, yi kɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Gurɛ́, nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ.” Tɛ́mté wu, abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ, nɛ abho bɛ́kóŋo Yesu.
Ntiɛt ákwɛ́n atú ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ankɛm ndu bápɔ̀kɔ bǒmame ndǔ bɛ̌sák ɛbhap mándɔk nɔkɔ mbǎŋ ɛnkɛm ɛnɛ bághókó bɛ́ Yesu achí arɛ́.
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ wɔ mmu ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɔ́kʉ́, ɛ́nchɔŋti nɛpɛ́m mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re sɛnɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm. Kɛ ɔ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ́ yí wu chí ntɨ manɔ anɛ Kristo ágú ɛ̌ti yi nkwɔ́.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛpu amɛm ɛkáti nɛpɛ́m, básɔ́t yi bágʉɛ́p amɛm nɛpǐngo.
Nɛ ntá bo abhɛn báfyɛ mmɛ́m ndǔ bɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛnya, bápú fyɛ mmɛ̌m bakɔ amɛm ɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛnya ɛnɛ́ ɛsɨ. Mbák mánkʉ́ nɔ, ɛbha ɛ́sɛn, ɛnchɔŋɔ, nɛ mmɛ́m andɔk amɨk.
Nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ yí áchyɛ́ mbɔ ɛbhé ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m yɛ chí ɛnɛ́ Ɛta ágháti mɛ ndɛm.”
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Jɔ̌n Njwiti ápɛ́rɛ twɔ, bo bátɔ̀ŋ nyaka chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm basɨŋ Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Basɨŋɨ́ mɔ kɛ̌ bo bákòŋo nyaka. Jɔ̌n átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, bábho bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu are nu bɛchwe arɛ́ nɛ bɛtaŋ.
Kɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyu ɛ́fákárí kɛ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ nɛ́nɛ. Nɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mmǔ anɛ anɛnɛ yi amɨ́k. Bɛ́p ká yi. Apú chí mandú mmɔ́. Chɔŋ yímbɔŋ angati bhe.”
Mbɔ̌ŋ Mandɛm mmu áchɨ̀ɛ kpák ánkʉ́ mǎmbák nyáŋá ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi. Yímbɔŋ ámbʉ́rɛ́ nkaysi, nɛ ɛfóŋó, nɛ mmʉɛt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ápú bhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ kpátɛ mpok Yesu Kristo Acha átwɔ.
Mpok yɔ, Píta abhak nɛfí, amɛm sɛnta chɔ́kɔ́. Ngɔrɛ́ anɛ achi mmɔ̌-bɛtɨk Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm arɔk ntá yi arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí nyaka nɛ Yesu mmu Gálili wu.”
Kɛ mbák ndak áchák áchí anɛ́ bǎyàŋ bɛrɨŋɨ, chɔŋ mányurɛ wú amɛm áchá ɛtɔk ndu nywɔp ɛnɛn manyé.
Nɛ mǎmpa nɔkɔ chí nyu? Pú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak chí ndǔ nɛdǐ-kɛbhɔ̌? Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ́ ɛyɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɔ̌ndak ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka.
Baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bátɨk yɛ bɛyɔŋ Yesu.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ nkaysi ɛnyǔ mmu wu apú chak. Ǎkʉ bɛbʉ́ mpǒknkɛm nɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ yi.
Ɛsakámu yɔ ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔbhɛ rɔŋɛrɔŋ nsónso mbɔnyunɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ.
Bǎkɛ́ kɛm mmu barɛm kɛ kwɔ. Barɛ̌m amɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛkɛm bo chi amɛn bɛkɔŋ bɔ. Mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋ bo ǎbhʉrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm mɛnkɛm.
Ɛkáti nɛwú mmu ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ chi mpok yi ánáŋ ágú, tɛ̌ndu ɛ́pú bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mpoknkɛm anɛ mmu anɛ ásɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛkáti yɔ achi nɛpɛ́m. Ɛchi mbɔ nku.
Mbák sɛ́ndɛm bɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́re kʉ bɛbʉ́ wáwák, nɔ́ sɛ́sɔ̀t Mandɛm mbɔ nsěnse, nɛ nɔ́ Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́pú amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ.
Bábilɔn akwɛn mbɔnyunɛ ákʉ́ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm mányú mmɛ́m ɛpúsí yi. Bafɔ̌ mmɨk bákʉ̀ nyaka nkwɔ ɛpúsí nɛ yi. Bakɔ̌síɛ mankɛm fá amɨk bákwɛ̌n bǒ bakáp ɛ̌ti ɛpúsí yi.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fu ntá ya. Bɛ́fú chi ntá mmu anɛ átó mɛ.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Apú rɔ yɛ̌ mmu anɛ ánókó yi ambɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p.”
Símun Píta arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ anyɛ́n nɛ ási.” Bakoŋo Yesu báchák bárɛ́m bɛ, “Sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ nɛ wɔ.” Bɔ́ bárɔ́k básɔ́t áchwí, báré gháp anyɛ́n amɛm áchwí wu bɛti mɛnkɛm ndu bɛkɛm nsi, kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɔ́kɛ kɛ́m.
Bǎghok nɛ bǎghɔ bɛ manɛ́mámɨk bághɔ̀ mbaŋ nɛ́nɛnɛ, nɛ bakɛm báfáté bákɔ̀. Bǒ ɛbhaŋákwa bátáŋ nɛ bachókó batú bághòk mbaŋ. Bawú bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ bo bághàti bachɛ́bhɛ́bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́mbak nɛ bhe mankɛm.
Chɔŋ Yesu Acha amfɛrɛ mɛ ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́pti ɛnyɨŋ, ampɛmɛ mɛ bɛ́ mbák amfay nɛ yí mmu achí Mfɔ bo Mandɛm. Kɛnókó kɛ́mbák nɛ yi mpoknkɛm, Amen. 
Yesu abho yɛ bɛkɔ atú Gálili ankɛm angati nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkímʉɛt bo Israɛl, ankʉ nɔkɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛn bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bho mɛ́mfu bɔ́ amʉɛt. 
Nkáká Mandɛm bɛ, ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ, ndɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ncha bhe mankɛm.
Yɨŋɨ́ ká Ɛláija. Áchí nyaka ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ bhɛsɛ́. Anɨkmʉɛt nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm bɛ́ manyiɛp ákɛ́ kwɛn, nɛ yɛ̌ nɛkɔŋ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ chɨ amɨk ndǔ mamiɛ́ arat nɛ ɛbhɔk.
Pɔ̌l anáŋ atɨ nyaka bɛ sɛ́mfʉɛt kɛte Ɛ́fɛsɔs, mbɔnyunɛ abhɨkɨ yáŋ nyaka bɛ sɛ́nchɔ́ŋti mpok atú Esia. Are wɛ̀nɛ bɛ mbák Mandɛm ánkwák, yi ánchwɔ́p Yerúsalɛm ndǔ nywɔp Ɛpǎ Pɛntɛkɔs. 
Ángɛl anɛ árɛ̀m nɛ mɛ akɛ́m ɛnɔk bɛyɛnti mɛnyɨŋ awɔ. Ɛnɔk ɛyɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ pú. Ayɛnti ɛtɔk nɛ ɛnɔk ɛyɔ. Ayɛnti nkwɔ manyǔbha nɛ nkók.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt anɛ aká nnyɛ́n bɛ Lídia afʉ́ ɛtɔk ɛgho ɛnɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ Tiatíra. Abhak nkɔsíɛ́ ndǔ ndɛn ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí mmʉɛt chu nɛ ɛ́yá nkáp. Ǎchyɛ nyaka Mandɛm kɛnókó. Mandɛm akʉ yi anɛnɛ ntɨ ɛni aghók sayri nɛ anoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m.
Yɛ̌ndu sɛ́chí ndǔ mmɨkɨ nɛ sɛ́pú nu mbɔ bǒ mmɨk.
Ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo kɛ Mandɛm atɔŋ mɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu, akʉ mɛ mbák mǔnto. Akʉ nɔ́ bɛ nkʉ́ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm mámbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, mángoko nɔkɔ chi yi nɛ mánchyɛ nɔkɔ nnyɛ́n ɛni kɛnókó.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánsɔt yɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀, bɛ mpok ɛsɔŋɔri ántwɔ́, mǎnu tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, nɛ mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛte kpirí.
Abhɛn bati bɛsa bɛrat nsɛm byo nɛ apay bápɛtnsɛm nɛ maŋák, báré ghati Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, yɛ chi bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɛ̀pti mmʉɛt ntá yɛsɛ.”
Yesu abhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ nyaka bɛ́gu chí ndiɛrɛ ɛ̌ti bo Israɛl. Abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛ́gu ɛ̌ti bɔ̌ Mandɛm abhɛn bátáká mmɨk nkɛm bɛ mambak ndǔ nkwɔ́ amɔt.
Sɛ́fǔ bɛtɔk nyáŋá nyáŋá: Mbɔk báfu Pátia, báchák Mídia, abhɛ́nɛ́fú Ɛ́lam; mbɔk báfú Mɛsopotemia, báchák atú Judéya, abhɛ́nɛ́fú atú Kapadóshiya; mbɔk báfú atú Pɔ́ntɔs, báchák atú Ésia.
Ɛtɛm ɛyɔ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɔ̌bɛkɛt bapay. Anɛ mbɨ abhak Nɛbhʉɛt Bɛdiɛrɛ. Arɛ́ kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpɔkɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mkpak ɛchi nyaka, nɛ brɛt Mandɛm.
Kɛ yɛ̌ndu bǎrɛ̀m bɛ yi achi Mandɛm aywɛka, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi, mɛ kɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yi. Mbɔ ndɛm bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi, mbʉ nchí se chi nse mbɔ běka. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yi nɛ nchí bhʉɛrɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.
Bǎghok ndu ngátí bhe bɛ, ‘Mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ, kɛ chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm ntá yɛká.’ Mbɔ bǎkɔ̀ŋ mɛ mbʉ bǎbhɔŋ maŋák bɛ́ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ ntá Ɛtaya, mbɔnyunɛ Ɛtaya acha mɛ.
Mbák mmu apú babhát nɛ mɛ, ǎbhák mbɔ ntábhɛ́nɔk anɛ́ bákpɔ́t báfɛ́rɛ́, ágú. Mányókóti mɛnyǔ batap ayɔ mámɛsɛ ango, ánsɔŋɔ.
Kɛ dɔ̌ ká Yesu Kristo Acha ámbɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo báyɨŋɨ bhe mándɨŋɨ ɛnyu mmu yi achi mbɔnyu bayɨŋɨ mmu mandɨŋɨ ndɛn anɛ yi afyɛ́ amʉɛt. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ chyɛ mbi ntá bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛpɛ́m nkwǎŋwaŋ nɛ́ŋwàka bɛ bo mǎnkʉ.
Bɔ́mayɛsɛ abhɛn fá mankɛm bátǒ bakak. Kaká ká batɨ nkwɔ sayri mbɔ bǒ Kristo.
Mpok nchwi ágó, abho mɛnyu kɛpɛm, kɛ bághɔ́ nchaŋ arɛ́.
Kɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhak kɛkúrí! Kɔŋ ka bǒmpap abhɛka, nɛ mǎnkʉ bhɔ bɛrɨ. Pwɔ ka bhɔ́, kɛbhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ mánkɛmɛ bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Mbák bǎkʉ̀ ɛnyu yɔ, chɔŋ akap aywɛká ánja ancha, nɛ mǎmbak bɔ Mandɛm Acha. Ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ntá bǒ bɛbʉ́ abhɛn bápú kaka yi nɛ abhɛn máŋɛ̀m mɛŋɛ́mɛ.
Pú mmɔ̌ nchwě mɛnɔk nɛ́? Pú María kɛ̌ achi máyi? Pú Jems, nɛ Josɛ́f, nɛ Símun, nɛ Júdas, chi bɔ̌mayi abhɛn babhakanɛm?
“Ntɔŋ, Moses asɨŋ ndǔ ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ bɛ, mbák mmu ángú ándɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́, mɔ́mayi abhɔŋ bɛsɔt ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ́ ámbé bɔ nɛ yi ndǔ nnyɛ́n manɔ anɛ ágú.
Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm Acha bɛ ankwak yi, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi.”
“Sɛ́yɛp be batu bɛ bǎkɛ́ pɛrɛ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n mmǔ-nɛ? Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎtàk mbok Yesu amɛm Yerúsalɛm nkɛm nɛ bǎyàŋ bɛkʉ ɛmbak bɛ bɛsɛ́ kɛ sɛ́kʉ́ báwáy yi.”
Bɔ́ bhɔ bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi ndu bákɔ́ŋ mɛ. Bákɔŋ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm ayap mɛ nɛ ákʉ́ bɛ mbák fá amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ chí ndu bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achí tɛtɛp.
Satan arɔk ntá yi, arɛm bɛ, “Mbák ɔ́chí Mmɔ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, chyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ batay anɛ anjibhiri andɔp bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt.”
Nɛ sɔt ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ Acha mbɔ mbi anɛ́ yi áchyɛ̀ bho bɛ mándɔ́ yi ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ. Ɛchi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɔ́mayɛsɛ Pɔ̌l mmu sɛ́kɔ̀ŋ ásɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka nkwɔ ntá yɛka nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn Mandɛm achyɛ yi.
Mbák Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ sɛ́ghàti bho achí bɛ Kristo ápɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ná yɛ mbɔk yɛka bákway bɛrɛm bɛ bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m?
Nchí to yi ampɛtnsɛm ntá yɛ, nɛ ɛchi mbɔ bɛ ntɨ ɛna kɛ mɛ̌tò nɔ ntá yɛ.
Bápɛt babho bɛyaŋ mbi ndu bɛkɛm yi, afori bɔ́ amɔ arɔk ɛbhakayi.
Mbák mmu anɛ ápú nkoŋo Yesu ámbɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu ywɛká ɛkɛt ɛyi ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́, nɛ mmu wu anka bɛ́rɔ́ŋ, ánáŋ ándɔ́k, ányiɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yí bɛsí. Ákɛ́ bhɛp mbák chí nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn báchyɛ́ mbɔ akap ntá njɔfú. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ bɛ yi ankʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛchɔŋti ntɨ ɛni amɛm.
Mpok Mandɛm ákú bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, bo bábhak mbɔ bɔángɛl awu amfay. Bápú pɛrɛ bháy nɛbhay.
Mɛ Jɔ̌n mǔnti bakoŋo Yesu amɔt kɛ̌ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛ, wɔ máyɛsɛ anɛ Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ nɛ ntá bɔ̌bhɛ. Nkɔŋ be tɛtɛp, nɛ puyɛ̌ chi mɛ awánti kɛ̌ nkɔ́ŋ bhe. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu áchák anɛ árɨŋɨ tɛtɛp Mandɛm akɔŋ be.
Kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ amɔt abhak nkwɔ́ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ. Are rɔ́ŋ ntá ntaŋá manyé wu anɨk nɔkɔ yí mmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Ɛta, táŋ manyé ya sayri fɛrɛ mɛ amɔ́ mǔmpap awa.’
Ɛ́kɔ̀ ná kɛ mmu ywɛká ansɔt ndak andɔk bɛsí bataŋá manyé abhɛn bápú bakoŋo Yesu mpok yí ábhɔ̀ŋ ndak nɛ ntɨ mmǔ Mandɛm, ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɔŋ ntá batɨ bo Mandɛm?
Aku bhe chi nɛ manoŋ mi nɛ mɔ́ acha nkáp tontó. Yí achi mbɔ mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛ abhɨkɨ kʉ nchɔŋtí nɛ yɔ kɛnyɔp mmʉɛt.
Mɛ́tò yi ampɛtnsɛm ntá yɛka, mbɔnyunɛ abhɔŋ ɛ́kwak bɛghɔ bhe mankɛm ndu bǎghókó nyaka bɛ yi ǎmè.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghàti nyaka bhe ɛ̌ti nɛtwɔ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́pú bakay. Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́ghɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛki nɛ amɨ́k.
Bɛkak ɛbhi bɛbhak mbɔ *brɔ́ns anɛ básɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ɛtaŋtí ngó ndu bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mɛ́nyɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ́nkɛm arɛ́. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛwarɛ́ tutunyɛ́n.
Nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ́ yɛ̌ chí bɛkɛt, yɛ̌ chi bɔ̌mayi, yɛ̌ chí ɛ́táyi, yɛ̌ chí máyi, yɛ chí bɔ̌bhi, yɛ̌ chí bakɨ yi ɛ̌ti yí ákòŋo mɛ, chɔŋ ampɛt ambɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay, ambɔ́ŋ nkwɔ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ bájwítí yi bɛ ambat mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo arɔp chí mbɔ Kristo, ndu asɔrɛ́ ɛpɨŋɨ́ Kristo.
Nkaysi yap akwɛ́n amʉɛt bo bati apay: Josɛ́f nɛ Matías. Josɛ́f abhɔ́ŋ manyɛ́n áchák ápáy. Nɔ́ chí Jústɔs nɛ Básabas.
“Mbák mmu ywɛka ǎyàŋ bɛte ɛkɛt ɛgho, pú ǎyambɨ anchɔkɔ amɨk ankay, angɔ mbák nkáp anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akway anɛ yi áte ɛkɛt anaŋa?
Bághátí Nkwɔ Kristo abhɛn fá ɛ̌ti ɛkɔŋ ɛyɛ nɛ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ́ ntá yap. Mpok anɛ bɔ bárɔ̀ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, chyɛ bhɔ nɛkwak ɛnɛn nɛ́kwáy ndǔ bɛtɨk Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀.
Yɛ̌ chí Moses atɔŋ nyaka kpoŋoroŋ ndǔ mbok ɛnɔk ɛnɛ́ ngó ádù arɛ bɛ bawú bápɛt chɔŋ nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ndǔ basɨŋɨ́ mi ɛ̌ti mbok ɛyɔ, Moses ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ Mandɛm mmu achi Acha bɛ, ‘Mandɛm Ábraham, Mandɛm Áisek, Mandɛm Jekɔ́p!’
Mpok nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ bachiǎkap áwúpsí, ɛwúpsí ɛbhak ndu ɛbhé nkwɔ.
Mbák mǎnkɛ́m nnyɔ́ nɛ awɔ, apú kʉ bhe yɛ̌nyɨŋ, nɛ mbák mǎnyú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́wày mmu, ɛ́pú kʉ bhe yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Chɔŋ mǎnyaŋa bǒmame amɔ́ anti mántaŋ.” 
“Bɔta, ndaká yi bákʉ̀ ɛnyunɛ? Sɛ́chí nkwɔ chi bakwǎŋwaŋ mbɔ bhe! Sɛ́twɔ fá bɛ́gháti bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu bɛ́ mǎntɨk nsɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nsay mǎntwɔ́ ntá Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Yí kɛ ághókó mfay nɛ mmɨk nɛ manyɛ́n nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi arɛ́.
Mpú kwáy bɛ́bɨti bhe mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Acha ághátí mɛ́ kɛ̌ ngátí bhé nkwɔ́. Ɛ́chí bɛ́ ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛ́n bátí yi, asɔt ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt,
Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́só bɛkak ɛbhap, akɛmɛ nkú amʉɛt, apɛtnsɛm, arɔk, achɔkɔ amɨk. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎjwímɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nkʉ́ ntá yɛka?
Nɛ ngók ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay, nɛ ɛbhɛn amɨk, nɛ ɛbhɛn ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú, nɛ ɛbhɛn amɛm manyu, bɔ mɛnkɛm bɛre kway bɛ, “Sɛ́mbɨ́tí mmu anɛ achi ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n. Sɛ́nchíɛ bɔ kɛnókó. Kɛfɔ kɛnkɛm kɛchi chi ntá yap. Bɔ kɛ babhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ mpoknkɛm!”
Ghók ká, chɔŋ ntɛmsi yí nɛ nɛme, nɛ mbák bo abhɛn bákwɛ̀n bɛrwɔp nɛ yi bábhɨ́kɨ́ tɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí barak ayi, chɔŋ nkʉ bɔ́ mámbɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Bakoŋo bhi bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɛtɔk ɛ́pú fá, chɔŋ mmu ambɔŋ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́kwày bǒbhɛn mankɛm fá?”
Bágwɔ́t yi amɨ́k nkwɔ, mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ yi bɛ, “Wɔ mmu ɔ́chí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ, ghatí bhɛsɛ! Agha ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́ wɔ?”
Nɛrɛm anɛ Mandɛm árɛm ɛ̌ti Nku Nkɔ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ anɛ mbɨ abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́náŋá ɛ́fʉ́ɛrɛ́ mpok, yɔ kɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ, ɛ́nɛmɛnɛm.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ,
Ɛwak Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, mfɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áchí nyaka ɛtɔk Shɛ́ba ǎfate andɛm bɛ bǎkʉ bɛbʉ́. Ǎrɛm bɛ bǎkʉ́ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ yi afu nyaka nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ arɔk bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mfɔ Sólomon átɔ̀ŋ bho nɛ bɛyǎ nɛrɨŋɨ́kɛpɨ. Nɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ mmu achi fá nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛka anɛ acha Sólomon, Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bǎpú ka bɛghok yi.” 
Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛ́bɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́pú chwe arɛ. Bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ barak abʉ́abʉ nɛ basěnse bápu chwe arɛ́. Bo abhɛn báchwe arɛ chi bo abhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ manyɛ́n ayap amɛm ɛkáti nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn.
Píta abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɔtɛ̌m nɛkay ɛnɛn chí ntá yɛsɛ kɛ chi ntá bo mankɛm?”
Mmɛ Pɔ̌l, kɛ nchí sɨŋ bakak amɛn nɛ awɔ́ wa.
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka ǎnyìɛ chí nɛnyíɛ́, yɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ kɛ̌ yí ányù, abhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɔ́ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo bághɔ̀ mánchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Tɛ́mté wu, ngɛ́mtay bɔángɛl Mandɛm babhesi bare kway mámbɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm bɛ
Yesu aghati mmu ywi wu bɛ, “Kɛmɛ́ akparɛnja ywɛ amɛm kɛ́nkwɔ́p. Mmu anɛ ánù nɛnu nɛ akparɛnja, ǎgu nɛwú akparɛnja.
Bápɛ́rɛ yɨŋɨ, bɛsí Yesu bɛ́yíbhiri bɛrɔbhɛ ghɔɔ ghɔ́ɔ mbɔ mmok. Ndɛn ɛ́yi nkwɔ ɛ́yíbhiri ɛrɔp pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p, ɛ́nkɔt nɔkɔ ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ.
Ápɛ́rɛ tó bhɔ, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ndǔ mɔ́tɔk anɛ achi afɔ ambɨ. Nɛchwe bǎchwè ɛtɔk, chɔŋ mǎngɔ́ mpɔŋɔ batu sɛsɛ́t, nɛ mɔ́ywi. Kaŋárí ká, mǎntwɔ fá nɛ yɔ.
Bě bho bǎpu bo Israɛl bǎpɛt bǎpú yɛ mankɔ, nɛ bǎpú bo abhɛn báfú nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ. Bǎrɔp chí bǒ ɛtɔk mbɔ bo Mandɛm bachak, nɛ bǒ nnɛrɛkɛt Mandɛm anɛ áchí mbɔ ɛfo ɛ́mɔt.
Ɛtɔk ɛ́kɔ́rɛ bɛbhe bɛpay, mbɔk bábhak ansɛm bo Israɛl, bo báchák bábhak nɛ bǒnto Yesu.
Yesu árɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́, arɔk anywɔ́p. Arɛ́, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábhɛ́p yi ntí bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɔ.
Mandɛm ánjɛ́t kɛfɔ ɛtayɛsɛ Debhít ɛkɛn kɛ́twɔ̀! Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm mfay!”
“Ndǔ nchí rɔŋ, ngáká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t ɛtɔk Damáskɔs, mbɔ nkárɛ́nká byó nɛ ɛpay nɛ ngósí, ɛtaŋtí bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ bɛ́fú amfay tɛ́mchok bɛ́kwɛ́n bɛkap mɛ, mbaŋ aghɔ tontó.
Kɛ mbák mmǔ ywɛka achɛp kɛboŋ bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ yi abhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ, ánɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ yi kɛboŋ. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ Mandɛm apɛrɛ́ chyɛ mmu ɛnyɨŋ, ǎchyɛ yi nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt, kɛyáŋ bɛji mmu.
Satan asɔt yi bárɔ́k Yerúsalɛm, bákó ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ áchí tɛ amfay ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Arɛ́, arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Mbák ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm, dók,
Nɛ ánáŋ ántɛ́n yɔ́ ankɛm nɛfí, ǎrɔ́ŋ ambɨ, yɔ́ ánkoŋo nɔkɔ ansɛm, mbɔnyunɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.
Kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛbhɛp. Bo Israɛl, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re ghók Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo kɛ? Bǎghok. Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ básɔ́rɛ́ bɛ́ghátí bhɔ mbok, ɛ́kɔ ɛghaka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉɛt fá amɨk, yɛ̌ chí ndǔ bɛbhak ɛbhɛn bɛ́sábhɛ́ nɛkɔ tontó.”
Mpok yɔ, akwɛ́n nɛme agú. Báso yi bábhʉrɛ amɛm mɔ́kɛrɛ́mfay ndu ɛkɛrɛ́ mfay.
Kɛ bo mankɛm abhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ yí nɛ maŋák, básɨ́kɨ ntɨ nɛ yi, ǎchyɛ bhɔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ mándɔp chí bɔ Mandɛm.
Mbɔŋ yɛ́ bɛ́dɨk nyaka be chí nɛ nɛ́bhɨ, puyɛ̌ nɛ nɛnyiɛ́ mbɔŋ mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re kwáy nyaka bo abhɛn mǎnyìɛ nɛnyiɛ́ mbɔŋ. Kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re kwáy bo abhɛn mǎnyìɛ nɛnyiɛ́ mbɔŋ.
Yɛ̌ mmu anɛ ábhat mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo kɛ andɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ apú. Mmu anɛ ábhʉɛ́t bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ yi abhɨkɨ re ghɔ Yesu nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi wáwák.
Bɔ́ mankɛm báré way Yesu way ndu bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mɔ̌rɛ́ agǔ tɛtɛp.
Báyàŋ nyaka chi ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́rɨ́ ɛ́chá, nɔ chi ɛnɛ ɛchí amfay. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ ntíánwɔ́p apu nɛ Mandɛm bɛ bɔ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ yi bɛ Mandɛm awap. Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm aghókó ɛtɔk abhʉrɛ ntá yap.
Bʉrɛ́ ka nkaysi chi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfay, puyɛ̌ ndǔ ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá amɨk.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ chi bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎdì ɛnyunɛ? Bǎyɛ̀m ntɨ ɛna amɛm! Mɛnká bɛ mámfyɛ mɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ chí nɛwú nká bɛgu ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha.”
Bábɨ́ŋɨri yɛ ntay ɛnɔ báfɛ́rɛ anyǔ nnɛm. Yesu ayoŋ amɨ́k ayɨŋɨ mfay arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, nkáká wɔ bɛ́ ɔghok mɛ.
Kɛ Kristo kɛ abhɔŋ bhe. Nɛ Mandɛm kɛ abhɔŋ Kristo.
Mandɛm ǎkʉ bɛběntɨ bhi mɛ́mfú amfay mɛ́nsɛp amɨk ndǔ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bápú koŋo mbi ywi bákʉ̀. Bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́chyɛ̀t bo báchák mbi bɛrɨŋɨ tɛtɛp Mandɛm.
Bǒbhɛn mankɛm babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nɛka nɛ Mandɛm tɛ ndiɛrɛ nɛwú. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu wap abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ. Bághɔ̀ nyaka bhɔ ghɔ tɛ nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ báchi chi mankɔ abhɛn báfʉ̀ɛrɛ fʉɛt fá amɨk.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Mandɛm afyɛ́ mpok achak anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ”. Debhít kɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm afʉɛt nyaka ntá yi tɛntɛp arɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mánáŋ bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ yi arɛm bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ, mpok bǎghoko ɛyɔŋ ɛyi, bǎkɛ́ gwɔt ntɨ.”
Baghɔk Yesu mányókóti nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́. Nɛ́jwí bɛkay byo nɛ bɛpay.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Yesu are nɨkmʉɛt nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́fu. Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́, nkoŋo ywi amɔt arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Acha, tɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ ɛnyu mánɨkmʉɛt mbɔ ɛnyǔ Jɔ̌n átɔ́ŋ nyaka baghɔk abhi.”
Nɛrɛm anɛ bárɛ̀m nɔ ǎtɔŋ bɛ bě bǎbhɔŋ bárɛ̀m nɛ manyu yɛka bɛ bǎchi ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka abhɛn báwáy nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Ɛtarɛ nɔkɔ sɛ́pɛ́t sɛ́chwé áchwí sɛ́ré rɔ́ŋ. Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ábhó bɛ́fú bhɛsɛ́ ambɨ. Ɛ́kʉ́, sɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t Sáyprɔs, ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí nɛ́ntɨ́ nnyɛ́n, sɛ́rɔ́bhɛ nók sɛ́mfʉɛt nɔkɔ chí ɛbhě ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí tɨɨɨ.
Sɔ̌l abhak arɛ́ téé, aka bɛ́ ɛrɨ mángwáy Stífin. Sɔ̌l are chyɛ bǒnkwɔ bɛyǎ nɛnyok Bɛ́bhó ɛwak ɛyɔ, báré chyɛ nkwɔ Yesu abhɛn báchí Yerúsalɛm bɛyǎ nɛnyok. Ɛkʉ bɔ́ mankɛm bábʉɛ́ bataka atúɛtɔk Judɛ́ya nɛ átú Samária ankɛm. Ɛrɔp chi bǒnto Yesu bɔ́bhɔ́ amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm.
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɛ́m ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, tɔ́ŋ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ ɛ́kway bɛtɔŋ bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm.”
Nɛchwɔp yí áchwɔ́bhɛ́ fá Rom, ayáŋ mɛ mbǎnkɛm kpát aghɔ́ mɛ.
Básɔt mɔ̌rɛ bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ yi. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ ɛghɔ nɔkɔ Yesu, tɛ́mté wu, ɛ́nyɨ́kɨ́si mɔ́wu gbogbǒgbok, akwɛ́n amɨk are bɨŋɨri, ɛfɛn ɛ́mfu nɔkɔ yi anyu.
“Mpok mánáká wɔ ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay, ɔ́kɛ́ tɨŋɨ yap ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛnókó ɔ́nchɔkɔ arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́kwáy bɛfakari bɛ mának mmǔ anɛ acha wɔ.
Yɛ̌ chi mpok sɛchi nɛ bhe sɛ́ghàti nyaka be bɛ mbák mmu apú kʉ bɛtɨk bǎkɛ́ chyɛ yi nɛnyíɛ́.
Nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n nɛ́ sɛ́ghàti bho chí ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fù ntá Mandɛm. Nɛ́chí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka nɔ́. Tɛ ndǔ mpok anɛ mmɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́ re bho, Mandɛm anáŋ aghókó nyaka nɔ́ abhʉrɛ ntá yɛsɛ́ ndu bɛ́kwák bɛsɛ́ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ kɛnókó.
Sɛ́ghok bɛ mbɔk bo báfu fá ntá yɛsɛ́ batwɔ awu nɛ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnap bɛ́chyɛ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bafyɛ bhe ɛbyɔk antɨ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tó bhɔ́.
Bǎkɛ́ noko bɛ́ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ bǒ bɛtábhá mantwɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ yi kɛ achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Chɔŋ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé nkwɔ mántwɔ. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ǎtwɔ, ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndu bɛrwɔ bho. Nɛ mándwɔ́ yɛ̌ chí bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ mámbák abhi, mbák bábhɔŋ mbi bɛkʉ nɔ.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́bhak chi ndɛ́ndɛm ndaká yí? Nti achi nyaka bɛ bɔ bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ndu mɛnu bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, ɛkʉ bɔ kɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm bɛ yi ankʉ bɔ mambak chak. Ɛchi nyaka mbɔ bɛ bo Israɛl báchɨ́ŋtí nɛkwɛ́n ndǔ ntay ɛnɛn nɛkwáy bɛkʉ mmu ankwɛn.
Tɛ̌ndu yɛ̌ mmu apú kwáy bɛ́táŋa mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, bǎbhɔŋ mbʉ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ chí kpák kɛchyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri.
‘Bǒbhɛn báchyɛ̀ mɛ kɛnókó chi nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́nyu bhap, batɨ yap asap nɛkɔ nɛ mɛ.
Bakʉ̌-bɛtɨk báfá bárɔ́k ntá mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ barɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta, pú nchwi kɛ sɛ́pɨ́ amɛm nkɨ? Nchaŋ ɛ́fu árɛ́ fá?’
Mandɛm atɔ́ŋ nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo achi Mmɔ Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ Ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛchi nyáŋá mpok ákʉ́ Acha ápɛ́tnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
Bú ká bǒmame abhɛn ɛtɔk ɛyɔ, mǎngati bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, ‘Mpok anɛ Mandɛm abhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap arɔp chi kɛkwɔt.’
“Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mpok ǎtwɔ̀, nɛ anáŋ akway, anɛ bawú bághòk ɛyɔŋ ɛya, Mmɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm, nɛ abhɛn bághókó mámbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Mmɔ arɛm ntá yi bɛ, ‘Ɛta, nkʉ Mandɛm bɛbʉ́, nɛ nkʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ kwáy mmu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mɔ́ywɛ.’
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ nsɔ́ŋtí anɛ mánɛ̀p ndu bɛtɨk, nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ bǎté kpirí ndu ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎpú chyɛ mbi ntá bǒ babʉ́abʉ. Kɛ mǎmɔ bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ bachi bǒnto ɛnɛ́ bápú, nɛ bǎghɔ bɛ bápú bǒ tɛtɛp.
Twɔ́ yɛ ka ntá Acha. Yí achi mbɔ ntay ɛnɛn nɛchi nɛpɛ́m, ɛnɛ́n bǒ mmɨk bábyaka bɛ nɛpu yɛ̌nyɨŋ, kɛ Mandɛm ayap nɔ nɛbhɔŋ mɛnwɔp bɛsí bhi.
Bǒbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ kwɛ́n chi mmɛ́m mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎkàysi. Nywɔp nɛchi ndiɛrɛ nkárɛ́nká nɛ́nɛ́namɔt běti.
báchwe amɛm áchwi bárè pé nnyɛ́n bɛrɔŋ Kapɛ̌naum. Bɛti mɛ́naŋ bɛ́gʉ nyaka ɛnɛ́ Yesu ábhɨ́kɨ́ re tɛmɛri bhɔ.
Bakoŋo Yesu bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bɔ́ mankɛm babho mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ; “Ɛta, wɔ ɔchí Acha, wɔ kɛ ɔ́ghókó mfay nɛ mmɨk, nɛ manyɛ́n nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí arɛ.
Ɛta, mɛ̌yáŋ bɛ bɔ́ nkwɔ, bǒ ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ mámbák nɛ mɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɛnchí, bɛ́ mángɔ́ kɛnókó ɛkɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ ɔkɔŋ mɛ tɛ mpok ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghoko mmɨk.
Mpok Yesu ábhó bɛtɨk ɛbhi, achi nyaka mbɔ mamiɛ́ ɛsǎ nsɛm byó, bo mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ Yesu chí mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f mmɔ̌ Héli,
Nɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm aghati nyaka Ɛtayɛsɛ Ábraham, ayɨkɨ bɛ́ yí ǎkʉ yɔ;
Ngɔ́ yɛ ángɛl tě amɛm mmok: Anak kɛnɛn kɛnkɛm ɛkɛ́n kɛ́rè amfay nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká manchɛm manyíɛ́ ɛpǎ ɛgho ɛnɛ Mandɛm ánáká.
Bǎkɛ́ bhak bakwɛnɛ́ mmɛ́m. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ kway bɛkɛm mmʉɛt, ɛ́ntwɔ yɛ yi nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́. Kɛ dɔ̌ ká Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ambak nɛ bhe, ambɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka.
Abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bábhɛ́mɛ́ yi fá?” Bákɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Acha, twɔ́ ghɔ́.”
“Bǎkɛ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ basɛ́mɛ́, mǎndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ sɛ́nyiɛ yi? Chɔŋ sɛ́nyú yi? Chɔŋ sɛ́mfyɛ́ yi?’
Fílip ápɛ́rɛ yɨŋɨ arɔp chí ɛtɔk Asótus. Abho bɛ́ghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ arɛ. Arɔk ambɨ bɛ́kʉ nɔ ndu bɔ̌bɛtɔk mankɛm abhɛn báchi ambi kpátɛ mpok yi aghaka Seséria.
Yɛ̌ chi mɛmbɔŋ mbɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ nkway bɛ́twɔ ntá yɛ. Chiɛ̌ chí ɛyɔŋ, chɔŋ mǔbɛtok wa antaŋ.
Júdas mmu abhɔŋɔ bɛti Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, chi mɛ kɛ?” Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́.” 
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bafɔ abhɛn bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk babhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay bǒbhap nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bho, ǎyàŋ mámbɨŋɨ yi bɛ, ‘Nkwaka-bho.’
Nɛ yi aghátí bhɛsɛ bɛ́ sɛ́kɛ́rɔ bɛghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ yɔ ntá bo, nɛ bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ bo mándɨŋɨ bɛ́ yí kɛ̌ Mandɛm ayabhɛ bɛ ambak mmu nɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́táŋ bo abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m nɛ abhɛn bágú.
Nkɨ chí mmɨk nkɛm, nɛ nchwi chi bo abhɛn Mandɛm áchí Mfɔ wap. Nchaŋ chí bǒ Satan.
“Toŋtí ká mmʉɛt mǎndurɛ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛka.
Mmǔ anɛ ányíɛ́ nyamwʉɛ́t ya nɛ anyú manoŋ ma, ǎbhɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, nɛ chɔŋ nkʉ yi ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn ngwɛnti.
Nɛ ndǔ mǎnòŋ nɛ nɛbhakántɨ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm átwɔ̀, kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ nɛ́ntwɔ́ ayak. Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ, ngó ásɔŋ mmɨk nkɛm, nɛ bɛsɔŋɔ́ ngó mɛ́nkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay ɛnsayri.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ́, “Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mmu abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó chi ntá Mandɛm Acha, antók chí yí aywǐntí.’”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu átɔ̀ŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm ɛkɛrákap abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Ná batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bárɛ̀m bɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò chi ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít?
Mandɛm Acha arɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́ chi nku nkɔ anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyu nɛ bǒbha mpok anɛ manywɔp ayɔ áfʉɛ́rɛ́. Chɔŋ mfyɛ́ bɛbhé bha amɛm batɨ yap, nsɨŋ bhɔ amɛm nkaysi yap.”
Nchí sɨ́ŋ ntá yɛka bǒnkwɔ abhɛn atú Galéshia, nɛ batɨ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báchí fá nɛ mɛ bachɛm nɛ mɛ bɛ́to be bakak.
Mbuɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ até ndǔ mmu anɛ ághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, anoko tɛ́mté nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.
Ndɔŋ ayɔ, Píta arɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm ántɛ́msí mɛ mbák mɛ̌sɛ̀ chi nsé! Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mmú anɛ bǎrɛ̀m nɔ ɛ̌ti yi!”
Ndǔ nkwɔ́ bǒnto Yesu, mmɛ kɛ nchí ansɛm mankɛm, nkɛ kwáy mmu anɛ bo bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ mǔnto mbɔnyunɛ mɛ̌chyɛ̀ nyaka bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́ bǒ batí ɛtɔk bátó bǒ mbɨ̌ŋ nkú ntá mbabhɛri ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ bǒbhɔ mándɔk!”
Yesu abho bɛ́tɛm bɔ́ nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Mmǔfú achí nyaka. Atɨ́ nkɨ apɨ mɛnɔk vain arɛ́. Atɛp ɛbhá ɛnɛ ɛghabhɛri nkɨ ankɛm. Atɛ́m mbok aghoko nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báyàt kɛpɛm váin, bɛ nnok ywi ámfu, mánsɔt, máná mmɛm. Ate mɔ́kɛrɛ́mfay amɛm nkɨ wu bɛ́ ámbák nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mmu áchɔ̀kɔ ndǔ bɛ́bhábhɛ́ri nkɨ. Afyɛ́ yɛ bo arɛ́ bɛ mánkʉ bɛtɨk mánkɔrɛ nsáy nɛ yi. Arɔ, arɔk nɛkɔ ɛtɔk ɛchak.
Ɛ́kʉ́ Páílet arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔpú ghók nɔ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bárɛ̀m bɛ́ ɔkʉ?”
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kɨŋɨ ndiɛrɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ mpok sɛ́yambɨ sɛ́twɔ́ ntá yɛka. Bɛsɛ babhɔŋ kɛ sɛ́yambɨ sɛ́twɔ́ bhe nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo.
Kɛnókó kɛ́mbák ntá Mandɛm mmu árɨ́ŋɨ́ wu mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm mpoknkɛm. Sɛ́chyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́. Amen.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛbhé Mandɛm. Bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Ɔ́kɛ́ kwɛn bɛrwɔp. Ɔ́kɛ́ wáy mmu. Ɔ́kɛ́ ghɛp. Ɔ́kɛ́ te ntísiɛ ákwárɛ́. Chiɛ̌ máyɛ nɛ ɛtayɛ kɛnókó.’”
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká nkwɔ ndǔ nkɨ wa mankʉ́ bɛtɨk arɛ́. Mǎnáŋ mǎmfáté beku, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ bhe nkáp anɛ ákwáy.” Báfʉɛ́t bárɔ́k.
Árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, atɔ́ŋ bɔ amɔ yi nɛ mbeápak ɛyi. Bakoŋo abhi bájwí nɛ maŋák ndu bághɔ́ Yesu Acha.
Bɛ́rɔ́ŋ nkárɛ́nká ɛtay beku, apɛt afú, arɔk ɛtɔk, aghɔ́ bo báchák tété, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákʉ̀ ti. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎchí fá tété, nywɔp nɛnkɛm, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkʉ ti?”
Yesu asɔt bɛyǎ bakay mbɔ ɛnɛn ndu bɛtɔŋ bho mpoknkɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bákwày bɛjwimɛm.
Mbák bǎtɔ̀ŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ anɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛpu arɛ́, mbák bǎkʉ̀ nɔ nɛ ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi, kʉ ka nɔ́ mpoknkɛm, puyɛ̌ chi ndyɛrɛ ndǔ mpok anɛ nchi nɛ bhe.
Mbák ɛ́kway bɛ́bhak nyaka ɛnyu yɔ ndǔ mpok nku nsɨ́, ná nɛ ɛchɔŋ, ndǔ mpok nku nkɔ? Bɛtɨk Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m bɛbhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm tontó ɛncha mpok nku nsɨ́.
Símun Píta abhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɔ̌rɔ̀ŋ fá?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ, ɔpú kway bɛ́twɔ arɛ́ nɛ́nɛ, kɛ chɔŋ ɔ́nkoŋo mɛ arɛ́ ansɛmpok.”
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɔ́k bátɛ́mɛri Páílet.
Bǎpú kwáy bɛsɔt nkɔ́p Acha mǎnjibhiri mmʉɛt mǎnyú nɔkɔ mmɛ́m bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ. Nɛ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ Acha, mǎnjibhiri mmʉɛt mányìɛ̀ nɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.
Syɛptí nɔ́kɔ́ ká batɨ bǒnkwɔ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhɛka kɛbhák bɛ bákʉ̀ nɔ mǎnywinti nɔkɔ.
Yesu ákɛ́mɛ́ yí bɛ, “Ɛ̌ti ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ ngɔ wɔ anɛrɛ́nɔk fig kɛ ɔ́nókó bɛ́ nchí Mmɔ Mandɛm? Chɔŋ ɔ́ngɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛcha ɛbhɛn.”
Arɛ́, batɛmɛ́ nɛnu básɔ́t ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́nɛn mbɔ mbʉ̌nya,   báfyɛ́ ndǔ mmɛm báchyɛ́ yí ányú. Ághókótí nɔ́kɔ́ mɔ́, akɛ ka mɛ́nyú yɛ̌ ndu báyàŋ nyaka bɛ yi anyu mɔ.
Áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ɛtaŋtí Mpɛmɛ anɛ áfú ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ́ mǔbɛtok ywi Mfɔ Debhít.
Bákú bo mámpu bɛ bághok ndǔ yi árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Moses nɛ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm.
Yesu abho bɛ́gháti bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Mamɔ anɛ átɛ̀n bo ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ápú nɔ́k bɛ́twɔ. Kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛ́ncha ntá mmú anɛ ákʉ̀ mamɔ ántwɔ́ ntá bho!
Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ́, ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛkuti ntí ywi mbɔ ɛrɨŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ yí achi antɛn nnɛ́m ywi, mbɔnyunɛ bɔángɛl báyɨ̀ŋɨ.
Sɛ́nsɨ́ŋ chí ɛkáti sɛ́ngáti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ nya anɛ áfú ndǔ akap anɛ báchyɛ́ ntá mandɛm nsé, nɛ bɛ mándɔ ɛpúsí, nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ nyiɛ́ nya ɛnɛ́ manoŋ amap ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ amɨk, nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ nyiɛ manoŋ.
Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bǎchwe ɛtɔk kɛ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ kɛsyɛpti bhe nɛ maŋák, fú ka dɔk ndǔ nkɔŋɔ-mbi ɛnɛ ɛtɔk yɔ, mǎndɛm bɛ,
Mmǔ wu abhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Ɛbhɛ́n?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛbhé Mandɛm. Bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Kɛ́ kwɛn bɛrwɔp. Kɛ́ wáy mmu, Kɛ́ ghɛp aghɛ́p. Kɛ́ te ntísiɛ akwarɛ,
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ mmu wu bɛ, “Sayri sayri, máya chí agha? Nɛ ntɨkɨ bho bachi bɔ̌maya?”
Kɛ mmu anɛ ághok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌rɛ̀m yi kɛ kʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndɛ́mɛ́, achí mbɔ mmu anɛ áté ɛkɛt, yi kɛ yambɨ bɛghoko nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt sayri. Mpok nnyɛ́n nɛgboko nɛ́ghaka ndǔ ɛkɛt, tɛ́mté wu, ɛ́báy mmʉɛt amɨk juu, ɛ́chɔ́ŋɔ ɛnkɛm!”
Ngɔ́ ángɛl achak ndǔ áfú amfay ásɛ̀p amɨk. Abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhi bɛre ghɔ ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ bǎchwé arɛ́, mǎnjámbɨ mǎndɛm bɛ, ‘Kpák anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ ámbák fá amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ.’
Páílet arɛm bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɔ. Sɔt ka bhɔ́ mándɔ́k mámbábhɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ nnɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎyaŋ.”
Mbuɔt anɛ nkwaŋankɨ átíɛ́, chí Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Nɛ achyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛ́táŋ bo, mbɔnyunɛ mɛ kɛ mfú ntá Mandɛm.
Asɔt yɛ bɔ́ nɛfí abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ́, “Bɔtá, chɔŋ nkʉ yi kɛ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ mɛ?”
Sɛ́sɔ́t manɨk sɛ́gwɔ́t áchwí wu amfay anɛ sɛchi amɛm ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ápú kwáy bɛ́dákáti áyák. Bakʉ̌-bɛtɨk amɛm áchwi báré cháy bɛ chɔŋ áchwí ándɔk ampaŋ ndǔ ɛ̌siɛ́p ɛnɛ ɛ́chí ndǔ ɛbhɔ́k manyu ɛnɛ ɛtɔk Sitis. Ɛ́kʉ́ báfɛ́rɛ ndo mámɛ́sɛ anyɛ́n, bɛ́, ndǔ áchwí áyà wu, mbʉ́ɛ́p ákɛ́pɛrɛ pɔkɔ́ wu tontó. Bákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bárɔ́ mbʉ́ɛ́p árɔ́bhɛ wu pɔkɔ́ áchwí.
Babhabhɛri ɛkɛrákap bákɛ́mɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ re rɛm mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmǔ wu árɛ̀m!”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yí áchwɔ́bhɛ́ ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk, nɛ yɛ̌ chi amɛm bɛtɔk bɛgho nɛ amɛm bakɨ, báré pɔkɔ́ bǒmame ndǔ mbaŋ ɛnɛ bo báchɛ̀m mbɔ nɛfísiɛ, mánɨk nɔkɔ mʉɛt bɛ yi andɔ bǒmame mantɔk yɛ̌ chi nkokoŋ ndɛn yi. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánú átɔ́kɔ́ nkokoŋ ndɛn Yesu, ataŋ.
bo abhɛn báká nɛwú ɛ̌ti Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo.
Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ, bapú pɛrɛ bhɛ́p mɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mbák mǎmbɛp Ɛtaya yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, ǎchyɛ bhe.
Nɛ wɔ ɛrɨ́tí ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk wa, nchí yáŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ ɔ́nkwák mɛ́nyúrɛ́ bághɔrɛ́ abhɛn bati apay bɛ́ mámbák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt. Bákʉ́ bɛyǎ bɛtɨk nɛ mɛ ndu mɛ́nu bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Bákʉ́ bɛtɨk nɛ Klɛ́mɛn, nɛ batɨ̌ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abha báchák. Bɔ́ mankɛm báchí bo Mandɛm ásɨ́ŋɨ́ manyɛ́n ayap amɛm ɛkáti manyɛ́n bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ chɔŋ ɛkwak bɛbhak nɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm yɛ̌ chi ndǔ nywɔp nɛmɔt kɛ be kɛbhɔŋ mbi.
Nchí yaŋ chi bɛ ndǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó nɛ́nɛ, mǎnkwak bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ, bɛ mpok bɔ nkwɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́, mánkwak be ndǔ mpok anɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ be mankɛm bǎbhak sayri ɛnyumɔt.
Ngɔ́ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛrat. Bɛ́bhak mbɔ mánsáŋ. Ɛmɔt ɛfu anyǔ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ, ɛchak ɛ́fú anyǔ nnya mbémbé nɛ ɛnɛ́fú anyǔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé.
Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ, Yesu atɛmɛri bhɔ, arɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm ámbák nɛ bhe!” Bárɔ́k bákwɛ́n amɨk bɛsí bhi bábhó bɛkɛm bɛkak ɛbhi mánchyɛ nɔkɔ yi kɛnókó.
“Bo Israɛl mankɛm bábhɔŋ bɛ́rɨŋɨ yɛ sayri bɛ, Yesu mmu be bǎgo ndǔ ɛkotákátí kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi áchi Acha nɛ Mpɛmɛ yi áyábhɛ́.”
Sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛkakánɛkɔ mbɔ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ nywɔp ámfay. Sɛ́kɛ́ chwe ndǔ bɛpǎ ɛbhɛn bo mányù mmɛ́m mánkwɛn, nɛ mámbo barak ɛ́púsí. Nɛ sɛ́kɛ́ fyɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ nɛ barak ɛ́pusi achak. Sɛ́kɛ́ chwe ndǔ bɛ́táŋá, nɛ mpabhamɨ́k.
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe ɛchɔŋ bɛ́ mbák mmu ywɛka amɔt arɔp ansɛm anɛ́m ɛbhɨ amɔ aya apu arɛ.
Abhak arɛ́ ndǔ manywɔp árát, yi kɛkwáy bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Mpok yɔ nkɛm yi kɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́, yɛ̌nyɨŋ yi kɛ nyu.
Kɛ abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎcháy yi? Yi mǎmàkati amɛm batɨ yɛka?
Bákɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ Píta, arɛm báfyɛ́ yi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Bakwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ábhak anwi ndu bɛbhabhɛri yi mkpák nɛ mkpák. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkwɔ́ wap ábhɔ́ŋ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu manwi. Hɛ́rɔd abhɔ́ŋ nkaysi bɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛ́mfʉ́ɛ́t, mámfɛrɛ yi mántáŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bho.
Nɛ nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bo mámpu mandɔk ntá yi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ndu bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nkárɛ́nká nɛ́nɛnamɔt beti bhɔ, afa arɔk nɛfísiɛ, aghɔ́ bǒfu tété abhɛn babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ.
Básɔ́t mɛnyǔ batay ŋáŋaŋ byo nɛ apay bághóko nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk bɛ andɨ amɨ́k. Ɛnyǔ ntay nɛmɔt nɛ́bhák Jáspa, ɛnɛn nɛjwi apay nɛ́bhák sáfaya, ɛnɛn nɛjwi arat nɛ́bhák agate, nɛ ɛnɛn nɛjwi anwi nɛ́bhák ɛ́meral.
María, mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala nɛ María achák, bábhák kɛ́kwɔ́t chɔ́kɔ́ mánjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ nnɛm. 
Nkwɔ́ wap abhɛn mánóko bárɛm bɛ Pɔ̌l ántát nɛ bhɔ kɛ yi kɛka.
Yesu are sɛmti bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok nɛ yís bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ anɛ Hɛ́rɔd.”
Kristo aku bhɛsɛ afɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛyak ɛnɛ ɛchi nɛ bo abhɛn bápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm. Akʉ nɔ ndu ásɔ́rɛ́ ntɛmsi bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ. Ɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɛyak ɛchi nɛ mmu anɛ ágú ndǔ ɛkotákátí.”
Arɛm yɛ ntá bǒbati ɛtɔk bɛ, “Bo Israɛl, sɔt ka mpok ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎkáysi bɛkʉ nɛ bǒbhɛn.
Tɛ̌ndu bɔ̌ abhɛn yi arɛmɛ nɔ ɛ̌ti yap báchí bakwǎŋwaŋ, mbɔŋ Yesu ayíbhírí nyaka arɔp nkwǎ. Akʉ nɔ́ bɛ́ ámfʉɛ́t ndǔ nɛwú anchɔŋti bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋá nɛwú, nɔ chi Satan.
Bɔ̌ma, bɛrɔŋ ndǔ ngwɛnti, ghók ká maníɛ́ ma, mǎnchɔkɔ sayri. Nyurɛ́ ká ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛka, mǎmbak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ batɨ. Bák ká sayri nɛ bo báchák. Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ, chɔŋ Mandɛm mmu ákɔŋ bhɛsɛ nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ kpák, ambak nɛ bhɛsɛ, ambak nɛ bhe.
Nɛ́nɛ bárɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́, ɛ́fú chí ntá yɛ.
Báká nɔ́kɔ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔ́t, básɔt nkáp wu bárɔ́k bákú nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk ntá ngoko bɛte ndu bɛ́bhɛ́mɛ nɔkɔ mankɔ.
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ nɛsɨkɨ ntɨ ɛnɛka. Nɛ́twɔ nɛ bɛyǎ nsáy.
Kɛ mpú sɔt nɛpɛ́m ɛna mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ. Nchí yáŋ chí bɛ njɛt tɛndǔ ngwɛnti, nnáŋá bɛtɨk abhɛn Yesu Acha áchyɛ́ mɛ́ nkʉ. Bɛtɨk ɛbhɔ chí bɛ́gháti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bo.
Mpok Sakaría ághɔ́ yi achayti, bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m yi tontó.
Bǎbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛrɨ ntá yɛka bɛ mmu amɔt ángú ɛ̌ti bo mankɛm ɛcha bɛ ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛnɛm?”
Bo bárɔ́k yɛ bɛghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari. Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ntá Yesu, bághɔ́ mmu anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́fú yi amʉɛt. Abhak sayri ndǔ nkaysi yi. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛm bɔ́ mankɛm tontó.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́cha nkwǎŋwaŋ, ɛ́pú cha Mandɛm.”
nɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ árɔ́ nnɛ́m abháy achak, akwɛ̌n bɛrwɔp.” 
Bábhák maknkay tontó, bábho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Pú bǒbhɛn mankɛm chi bo Galili?
Nɛ nchí nɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛ ɔ́nchɛ́m mmʉɛt nɛ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ ɔ́ndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chi ambɨ, nɛ bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak wɔ ɔ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ ndu sɛbharɛ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo.
Nɛ mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ nɛbháŋ ndu nɛbho bɛkwɛn, bǎrɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛnɛm ɛ́twɔ̀’; nɛ ɛ́mbak ɛnyu yɔ.
Nɛ mbák bo Israɛl mángúpsí batɨ yap mánoko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu, Mandɛm ǎsɔ̀t bhɔ ankʉ bɛ mámpɛt mambak batábhɛ́nɔk ɛnɛ bapɨ. Yi abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ nɔ.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, be bho bǎpú bo Israɛl bǎtàŋ nyaka ntí nɛ Mandɛm, kɛ nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm ághɔ̀ bhe ntínso ɛ̌ti nɛtaŋántɨ bo Israɛl.
Ɔchá ɛtayɛsɛ Jekɔ́p mmu átɛ́mɛ́ nyaka mbokó manyiɛp anɛ arɔ ntá yɛsɛ? Ná ɔ́kway bɛchyɛ mmu manyiɛp amɛn áchá amɛn yímbɔŋ ányu nyaka, nɛ bɔ̌bhi mányú, mpɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́nyú?”
Bɔ́ mankɛm bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Dɔ manoŋ ami ámbák bhɛsɛ́ antí, nɛ bɔ̌ bhɛsɛ́!”
Yesu arɔk aghaka atú mmɨk bǒ Gɛrása ɛbhě manyu ɛchak. Bǒ bati apay abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ, báfú ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ manɛm anɛ́ bɔ́ báchɔ̀kɔ arɛ, bátɛ́mɛri yi. Bághɔ̀ nyaka bo, mántoko bhɔ anɛt. Ɛ́kʉ́ bo kɛpɛrɛ fʉɛ́t atú wu.
Mpok bǎpày ɛkáti ɛnɛ, chɔŋ mǎnkwáy bɛghɔ bɛ njwímɛm sayri ndǔ nkaysi Mandɛm anɛ achi nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo.
Baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bákòŋo nyaka Yesu mánchyɛ nɔkɔ yi nɛkwak bɛbhó mpok anɛ yi áchi atú Gálili. Bɛyǎ baghɔrɛ́ báchak abhɛn bákóŋó nyaka Yesu Yerúsalɛm bábhak arɛ́ nkwɔ́. 
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm nɛ Ngɔrɛ́ anɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn bárɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Twɔ́!” Bě bo bǎghòk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ, Dɛm ka nkwɔ́ bɛ́, “Twɔ́!” Bě bo manyiɛp ákwàk be, twɔ́ ká. Twɔ́ ká mǎnyú manyiɛbhɛ́ nɛpɛ́m. Bɛyɔŋɔ́ ngwɛnti
Mbɔk bho báchi mbɔ mbwɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mɔ́mbi anɛ achi amɛm nkɨ. Nɛghok anɛ bághókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, Satan antɨŋ antwɔ́ amfɛrɛ yɔ́ amɛm batɨ̌ yap.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, nkwɔ Fárisi bo bákɔ́ŋɔ́ nkáp tontó báre way yi.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk chí ɛnɛ? Bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhɛ,’ kɛ chi bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Faté kɔ?’
Bɔ́ŋ ká maŋák ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbháká ntɨ arɛ́ bɛ Mandɛm ankʉ ntá yɛka. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ ndǔ mpok ɛsɔŋɔri. Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt mpoknkɛm.
Babhabhɛri abhɛn ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bápɛ́t yɛ nsɛm ntá bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi. Bǒbati bábhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ nɛ yi?”
Fílip abhɔ́ŋ bɔ̌baghɔsɔ́ŋ batí ánwi. Bɔ́ kɛbháy manɛm. Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nyaka bhɔ akap bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n yí afyɛ́ bɔ́ antɨ.
Yesu akokosi mmʉɛt nɛ bhɔ́, aghati bhɔ bɛsí nɛ bɛsí bɛ, “Ɛtaya achyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm amfǎy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu awu amfay nɛ fá amɨk.
Sɛ́kɛ́ fɛrɛ ntí ndu bɛchɛm nɛ batɨ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk bo bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛpɨŋ bɛkʉ. Ɛnyɨŋ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chi bɛ sɛ́mfyɛ́ nɔkɔ batɨ ntɨ, sayri sayri, nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu átwɔ̀ nɛchi kɛkwɔt.
Bábhó bɛrɔŋ ntá yi máŋɔkɔ nɔkɔ yi bɛ, “Acha mfɔ bo Israɛl, kɛnókó kɛ́chí ɛkɛ ɛta!” Ndu bárɛ̀m nɔ, manchyɛ nɔkɔ yi nsáp bɛsí.
Kɛ bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ yi ákɔ̀ amfǎnyɛ́n átwɔ̀, bɛ́cháy bɛ́kɛ́m bhɔ tontó. Bábho bɛbɨk, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Chí ɛfóŋó-ngu! Chí ɛfóŋó-ngu!”
Yesu achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ bɔ́ mankɛm mánchɔ́kɔ́ amɨk. Asɔt yɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bhɔ tándrámɔt. Áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛbɔkɔti bhɔ anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ mánchyɛ́ ntá bo bhɔ. Báré sɔt mánkɔrɛ nɔkɔ.
Mandɛm kɛ ághókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi ntá yi. Ndu áyàŋ nyaka bɛ bɛyǎ bho mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhak bɔ̌bhi nɛ mámbɔŋ kɛnɛ́m, ɛrɨ nyaka bɛ yi mmu ánɛ́nɛ́ bhɔ mbǐ wu ámfʉɛ́t ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri bɛ ankwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ákʉ̀ bɔ mámbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Mbák mǎngɔ́ yɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ndu nchí pɛtnsɛm amfay ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mfú, bǎrɛm bɛ́ yi?
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ be mankɛm. Mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntɨ bɛrɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, apú kway bɛbhak nkoŋo wa.”
