Arɔk ambɨ bɛ́kʉ ɛnyuyɔ ndǔ mamiɛ́ ápay. Ɛ́kʉ bo mankɛm abhɛn báchí atú Esia, bághók Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha, nɔ chi bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. 
Ɛrɛmɛ nkwɔ́ bakók ányìɛ nyaka kɛkwɔt nɛ nɛbhʉɛ́t wu.
Mpok ákwáy anɛ Josɛ́f nɛ María barɔŋ bɛkʉ mbɔnyu ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mánkʉ ndu bɛbhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm mpok ngɔrɛ́ abhé, bápɔ́kɔ Yesu bárɔk Yerúsalɛm ndu bɛtɔŋ yi ntá Mandɛm Acha,
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ chi-bɛtɨk apú nɔ́k bɛrɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyi awɔ́ mmɔ̌bɛtok wu.
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chí ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌yáŋ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́. Kristo achí mǔnti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbakanɛm, mbakanɛm achí mǔnti ngɔrɛ́ aywi, nɛ Mandɛm achí mǔnti Kristo.
Yɛ̌ mmu achi chi mmu Israɛl, yɛ apú mmu Israɛl, ɛwupsi ɛ́pú arɛ́. Nkúbhɛ́ Acha árɛ amɔt kɛ achi Acha bǒ mankɛm. Nɛ yi ǎchyɛ̀ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá yi.
Ngók yɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ndǔ ɛ́ghàti bɔángɛl tándrámɔt bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká to bɛběntɨ Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm bɛkwɔbhɛ́ bɛběntɨ ɛbhi tándrámɔt ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm.”
Bɔ̌ma, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɛ́mɛ́rí mmu ywɛka ámbɔ́ŋ chi maŋák,
Bǒnto Yesu barɔ yɛ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif bápɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm, nɛkɔ ɛnɛ́n nɛchi mbɔ kilómɛta amɔt.
Agú ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛ bo abhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛn yi áchyɛ̀ nɛ maŋák bákɛ́ pɛrɛ bhak chi ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyap. Bapɛ́m ayap ándɔp chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ mbɔnyunɛ ɛ̌ti yap kɛ yi ágú nɛ ɛ̌ti yap kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Ngufú chɔŋ ntat nɛ be mandú, nɛ ɛ́kway bɛbhak ndǔ ɛso ɛnkɛm. Mpok ánkwáy yɛ anɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ ɛbhak ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɔ́ŋ, mǎnkwak mɛ ndɔ́k arɛ́.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yaŋ nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm, nnɨ́k nɔkɔ mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bo ɛtɔk Israɛl chi bɛ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
“Bɛ́rɔŋ ndǔ ngwɛ́nti, Stífin arɛm bɛ, ‘Bě bo nɛtaŋántɨ, bě bo bǎpu noko Mandɛm nɛ bǎpú ghok ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Bǎchɛt Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mbi mbɔ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka.
Chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ámbák ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛkwɛt nɛ angók bɛyǎ bɛbe. Ákʉ̀ nɔ bɛbho nɛ bo Israɛl nɛ bɛghaka amʉɛt bo abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Yesu apɛt abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Nɛ mpok nkɔ́rɛ́ anɛ bɛkpɔk tándrámɔt nká bho ɛnwi ɛ́nyiɛ́, anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ mǎnyokoti, abhak bɛkay mɛ́ni?” Bákɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Tándrámɔt.”
Bo Israɛl bhɔ kɛ báwáy nyaka Yesu Acha nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm nɛ bɔ́ kɛ báboko bhɛsɛ ɛtɔk. Bákʉ̀ ntɨ nɛ́mbé Mandɛm. Bachi bǒmpap ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Máyi aghati bo abhɛn bákɔ̀rɛ mmɛm bɛ, “Kʉ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí ághàti bhe.”
Mbák sɛ́nchók batú, sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́náŋ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm, sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ akap achak apu anɛ ákway bɛkʉti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛpɛt ɛtwɔ ntá yí ndɔŋ anɛ ájwí ɛpay bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm akʉ bɛ ɛmbak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí bhi, yɛ̌ mmu akɛ rɛm bɛ ɛ́pú pɛ́pɛ́p.”
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sayri nɛ ɛbyɔk ti.
Kwáy nɔ́kɔ́ ka mɛnyǔ bakwáy Nku Nsɨ́, nɛ bakwáy Mandɛm, nɛ bakwáy anɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀ ndu bɛ́fyɛ́ batɨ ntɨ. Kwáy nɔ́kɔ́ ka bakway ndu bɛbɨti Acha nɛ batɨ yɛka ankɛm.
Sɛ́ká yɛ nɛwú, bɛ́ mǎnkwáy bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛ́bhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛ́nti.
Bákɔ̀ chi bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Kristo. Ɛ̌ti yɔ bápú sɔt yɛ̌ nɛkwak ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
Jɔ̌n arɔk yɛ ndǔ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi atú Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan, angati nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm bɛ bo mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap mánjwítí bhɔ́ bɛ Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mbɔk mǎnchyɛ́ ntá mǔnti ɛpǎ nɛbhay”. Bákʉ́ nɔ́.
Mmɛ Jɔ̌n nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá bɛka bǒnkwɔ tándrámɔt abhɛn báchí atú Esia. Mandɛm mmu achi nɛ́nɛ, abhak tɛ̌ nyaka, nɛ ǎtwɔ̀ ántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, anchyɛ bhe kpák. Bɛfóŋó tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛchi bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm mɛ́ntɔ́ŋ nkwɔ bhe bɛrɨ̌ndu, mɛ́nchyɛ be kpák.
Chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe kɛnɛ́m ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛ mǎnkwáy bɛchyɛ tontó nɛ awɔ́ fúú. Nɛ akap aywɛka wu ámfʉɛt ntá yɛsɛ angaka ntá bo abhɛn bǎtò wu ntá yap, nɛ ánkʉ bɔ́ mánchyɛ́ Mandɛm bakak.
Ɛ́rɨ sayri bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ mfɔ arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛpɨŋɨ́ bo Israɛl mɛnkɛm nɛ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ bhɔ nɛ ákɔ́rɛ́. Nchí nɨk yɛ wɔ mmʉɛt bɛ́ ɔ́nkɛ́pntɨ ɔ́ngɔ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m.
Sɛ́nchíɛ yɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm. Yi ǎkway bɛkɛm be bɛ bǎkɛ́ kwɛ́n ansɛm. Chɔŋ yi ankʉ bǎkɛ nyɔ́p mmʉɛt, antwɔ́ nɛ bhe bɛsí bhi. Arɛ́, bǎghɔ́ kɛnókó ɛki, mǎmbak maŋák mpoknkɛm.
Ná mbɔk yɛká bátɔ̀ŋ mmʉɛt bɛ́ bárɨŋɨ? Mbák bo báchí ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛká abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛboŋ, bárɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí chak nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú chak, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ámbɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ nɛ nɛsɛptímʉɛt ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ mmu achí ndɨŋɨndak tɛtɛp.
Sɛ́kɛ́ bhʉrɛ yɛ kɛnɔ́ mbɔ mbɔk bho. Sɛ́mbák chí pě, sɛ́nkɛm nɔkɔ mmʉɛt.
Ɛchí chak bɛ ɔ́kɛ́ nyiɛ nnya, nɛ bɛ ɔ́ndɔ́ mɛnyu mmɛ́m, nɛ bɛ ɔ́ndɔ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛkʉ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ánkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
nɛ Satan abhɨ́kɨ́ rwɔ nyaka Adam. Ifa kɛ ákóŋó nsé Satan akwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Gɔ́bhanɔ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛpɨŋ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́, ndǔ mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, ǎfɛrɛ mǔkɛnɔŋ amɔt anɛ bo báyàŋ yí ámfɛ́rɛ́.
Amɛm ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs, Apólos abho bɛ́gháti bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy. Prisíla nɛ Akwíla bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ yi ághàti bho ɛ̌ti Yesu, básɔ́t yí ɛkɛt ɛyap, mánáŋa batɔŋ yi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ mbi Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛchi.
Nywɔp ɛpǎ bo Israɛl ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ *Pɛ́ntɛkɔs ɛghaka nɔkɔ, bakoŋo Yesu mankɛm bábhák nɛbhʉɛt amɔt.
Sɛ́bhɔŋ ntɨ nɛ ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ndɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ sɛndɔk sɛmbak anywɔ́p nɛ Acha.
Ghɔ́ ká, Mandɛm achɨk achá! Nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛni nɛyǎ nɛ́chá, nɛ arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ nkaysi ayi áchí Yɛ̌ mmu apu rɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ yi ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ́ yɛ́ bɛ́ mmu ántáŋ ntɨ ɛnɛ́ mpok ábhɨ́kɨ́ re kwáy. Nywɔp Yesu ápɛ̀tnsɛm, chɔŋ ankʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí amɛm ɛjuri nɛ́nɛ ɛ́mfú kpoŋoroŋ. Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ ankʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkaysi anɛ áchí mmu antɨ amfú kpoŋoroŋ. Mpok ɛyɔ chɔŋ Mandɛm ambɨti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhi bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́.
Mandɛm ywɛsɛ ǎkʉ̀ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ǎghɔ̀ bhɛsɛ ntínso tontó. Chí ntínso kɛ nɛ́kʉ yi áto chɔŋ Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ́, yí amfú amfay antwɔ mbɔ nyiɛnyíɛ́mok běti.
Mpok Yesu áchí ɛtɔk Bɛ́tani, abhak amɛm ɛkɛt Símun. Símun wu anáŋ ame nyaka ɛbhaŋákwa.
Bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bati byo nɛ amɔt bárɔ́ yɛ bárɔ́k atú Gálili ndǔ njiɛ anɛ Yesu ághátí nyaka bɔ́ mándɔ́k arɛ́.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi bɛ mántwɔ́ ntá yi. Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ayap bhɔ́ batí byo nɛ apay, áchyɛ́ bhɔ́ nnyɛ́n bɛ bǒnto.
Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ ákʉ̀ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyu Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bo mambak chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yàŋ chi bɛ bo mámbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, mándɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti. Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, Mandɛm ákʉ̀ yi ambak chak bɛsí bhi nɛ chɔŋ ambɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m.” 
Yesu afa, abho bɛrɔŋ nɛ yi. Bɛyǎ bo bákáp yi bɛbhe bɛpay.
Dɨŋɨ́ nkwɔ bɛ, ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛpi nɛ́kɔrɛ bhɛsɛ ɛnyunɛ́, yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛfu fá ampe antwɔ ntá yɛka; nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛrɔ ɛbhě yɛká, ampé ántwɔ́ fá ntá yɛsɛ.’
Ayibhiri yɛ mmʉɛt arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi ansɛm ansɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛka ɛcha bɛ́ bǎghɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ bǎghɔ̀!
Bɔangɛl bha báfɛ̀rɛ bhɔ mámɛsɛ amɛm nɛpǐngo. Arɛ́, bábhàk ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ́ ámɛ́n.
Mǔngo amɔt anɛ áchí ndǔ ɛkpɔk ɛbhɨ ɛyɔ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Pɔbliɔs. Abhɔ́ŋ bakɨ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ngɔkɔnyɛ́n. Asɔt bhɛsɛ sayri. Ane bhɛsɛ ndǔ manywɔp arat.
Chɔŋ bo mankɛm mámpap be ɛ̌ti bǎchí bakoŋo bha.
Yi kɛ bhɛsɛ bhɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ yi kɛ rɔ bɛkɛmɛ bhɔ. Arɛm bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ mɛ kɛ nchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.”
Ɛ́kʉ́ Hɛ́rɔd abhɛ́p Yesu bɛyǎ bɛbhɛp kɛ yɛ ɛ́mɔt Yesu ábhɨ́kɨ́ kɛmɛ.
Chɔŋ ɛmbɛp ɛncha ntá mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɔ́wa amɔt anɛ abhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ ánkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Ɛchi sayri ntá mmu wu, bɛ mánsɔt ntay nɛgho mánsɛt ɛmɨ ɛyi, mámɛsɛ yi amɛm manyu.
Mpok nchí awu nɛ bhe nkʉ mɛnyɨŋ bɛtɔŋ be bɛ nchí mǔnto tɛtɛp. Mbɔ́ŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ nkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Ɛta, kʉ bo mánchyɛ́ nnyɛ́n ɛna kɛnókó.” Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú amfay ɛrɛm bɛ, “Nnáŋ nkʉ nnyɛ́n ɛna nɛ́mbɔ́ŋ kɛnókó nɛ chɔŋ mpɛt nkʉ nɔ.”
mbɔnyunɛ mmok ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ ghɔɔ. Nɛ ɛkát ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛ́ghárɛ ndǔ bɛbhɔk bɛpay gbee.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk bɛ ngátí nyaka bhé mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n mpok nchí nɛ bhe?
Kɛ mbák chí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛtaŋántɨ, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ átɨ́knsɛm ntá Yesu, nɛ mmu ɛpúsí, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngwayti bho, nɛ mmǔ ɛpusi, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔnjɔ, nɛ bǒ babú, nɛ mmu anɛ áchyɛ̀ kɛnókó ntá mandɛm achak, nɛ basénsi mankɛm. Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ntɛ́msí yap ambak amɛm nɛpǐngó anɛ ádù nɛ sɔ́lfɔ. Ntɛ́msí yɔ, chi nɛwú ɛnɛn nɛjwi apay.” 
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛsɛ bo Israɛl sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ puyɛ̌ bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl kɛ ákʉ mmu ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, chi bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Kristo. Yɛ̌ chi bɛsɛ sɛ́nókó Yesu Kristo bɛ Mandɛm ansɔt bɛsɛ mbɔ bo abhɛn bachi chak ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛsɛ nɛ Kristo, puyɛ̌ chi ɛ̌ti sɛ́bhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé. Ɛchi ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ, bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé apú kʉ yɛ̌ mmu ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bǒfú bábhak abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔ́ŋ ámɔ́t nɛ bakoŋo Ɛpikurɔs nɛ bɔ Stɔik,   Bɔ́ nkwɔ́ bákɛ̀m nyaka ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ yi. Pɔ̌l ǎghàti nyaka bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́ chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛ́kʉ́ mbɔk ɛyap báré way Pɔ̌l mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́, “Ɛchɨŋtǐ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nkwɔ́ ǎrɛ̀m nɔ́ mbɔŋ yi?” Báchák bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ bɛ yi ǎghàti bho chí ɛ̌ti bɔmandɛm abhɛn sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ fá ɛtɔk ɛnɛ.”
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ, Mfɔ Agripa nɛ mɔ́mayi Bɛnis bárɔk amɛm áchá-ɛtɔk nɛ bɛyǎ kɛnókó, báchwé nɛ bǒbati batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ manɛm bǒ ɛtɔk. Fɛstɔs achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mánsɔ́t Pɔ̌l mántwɔ́ nɛ yí.
Kɛ báchák báré rɛm chi bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri yi akwáy bɛrɛm nɛ. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́kwày bɛ́kʉ nnɛ́mámɨ́k ángɔ́ mbaŋ-á?” 
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mpok yi ákó tɛ amfay, ásɔ́t ngɛ́mtáy bo abhɛn yi ákɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ mankoŋo yi, akɔrɛ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ntá bho.”
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, Jɔ̌n apɛt abhak téé nɛ bakoŋo bhi bati apay.
Achwe, arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Chí yí nɛ bɛyǎ ɛbyɔk nɛ kɛbhɔ? Mɔ́nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ gu. Ǎbhʉrɛ chí kɛnɔ́.”
Ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn bǒnto bákʉ̀, bo báré pɔkɔ́ bǒmame mámbʉrɛ nɔkɔ nɛpaká mbi, mbɔk ndu bɛkɔ́k, bachak ndu bɛ̌sak, bɛ́ Píta apɛrɛ́ fʉɛt ndɨkandi ywi ánkwɛ́n mbɔk ayap amʉɛt.
Nɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ntwɔ bɛ́yáŋ nɛ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ chi bo abhɛn manɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ.” 
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báré way nkwɔ yi, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Bachǐmbɨ bhɛka mányìɛ nyaka mana amɛm baso, yɛ̌ nɔ, bɔ mankɛm bágú.
Bɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ ká chi maŋák tɛ̌ndu bábhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ Kristo ndǔ bǎchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ yi, bɛ́ be nkwɔ mǎnjwi nɛ maŋák mpok yi átwɔ nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛki.
Yesu arɔk achwe ɛkɛt Píta, aghɔ́ nnɔ ngɔrɛ́ ywi bhʉ́rɛ́ nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p amʉɛt.
Ná nɛ áchwɨ̌nyɛn nkwɔ? Yɛ̌ndu áré chɨk, nɛ yɛ̌ mbʉ́ɛ́p anɛ́ ádɛ̀p wu ántaŋ ná, nsɔm achí anɛt áchwi babhát anɛ mbák mmu ánjá anjɛp, áchwi árɔ̀ŋ chí ɛbhak ɛnɛ yí áyàŋ wu andɔk.
Bɛsɛ bo sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk nɛ Mandɛm, sɛ́nɨ̀k be mmʉɛt bɛ bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn yi atɔŋɔ bhe mɛ́mbák ndɛ́ndɛm.
Yesu ayoŋ amɨ́k arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mma, bɔ́ báchí fá? Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ mángwáy wɔ?”
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ngátí bhé bɛ mmu apú kway bɛ́twɔ ntá ya mbák Ɛta abhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ yi mbi.”
Ɛkʉ Yesu kɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay arɛ́, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chí nɛnyaŋa anɛ yi ányáŋá amɔ amʉɛt mpǎy bǒmame, abú bhɔ́.
Ntí achi bɛ mpok ɛyɔ, bo bákɔŋ mmʉɛt ɛyap máncha, mánkɔŋ nkáp máncha, mámpányu, mámbɔŋ nɛyoŋómʉɛt, mámbak basɔkɔtɨ̌ bho, bɔ́ kɛka bɛghok bachi nɛ manɔ bhap. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmú ankʉ bhɔ́ bɛrɨ ná bákɛ sɔt mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ. Mpok ɛyɔ, bo bákaysi bɛ́ ntí apú anɛ bɔ́ mánɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ndu bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mmǔ anɛ apɨ́ mbwɔt anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ya, ǎghɛm mbwɔt anɛ abhɨkɨ ya. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ ápɨ́ bɛyǎ, ǎghɛm bɛyǎ.
Kɛ wɔ Tímɔti, yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak ná, kɛ́rɔ bɛbhak nɛ ntɨ amɛm kpák. Yɛ̌ ɔ̌ghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ná, kɛ́p ntɨ. Kʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn ngati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ wɔ ɔ́nkʉ.
Ansɛm mpǎy manywɔp, anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn anyokoti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi apɔkɔ arɔk ɛtɔk ɛ́chák nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ. Arɛ́ achɔŋti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛnkɛm ndu mɛ́nyiɛ ɛpɔ̌ nɛpɛm.
Kɛ mbák bo mankɛm bárɛ̀m chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm, nɛ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Yesu Kristo, nɛ yɛ̌ chí anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn antwɔ́ anchwe, ǎghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎrɛm anjwimɛm anka bɛ yi achi mmǔ bɛbʉ́, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághókó mɛ́mbo bɛtaŋ yi.
Mányiɛ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛnyíɛ́, Yesu arɛm ntá Símun Píta bɛ, “Símun, mmɔ̌ Jɔ̌n, ɔkɔŋ mɛ ɔchá mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn-ɛ?” Símun akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛɛ, Acha, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nkɔŋ wɔ.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ne bɔ̌bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ayá.”
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, nkʉbɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛ mǔnto Yesu Kristo kɛ nchi nsɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Bɛtɨk ɛbha chí bɛ́kwak bo abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ́ mámbák abhi bɛ mánsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu sayri, nɛ bɛ́kʉ bɔ́ mándɨŋɨ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ Yesu átɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka. Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mámbʉrɛ bapɛ́m ayap mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ.
Mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, yɛ basyɛp yi syɛp, yɛ bábhɨkɨ syɛp, ɛyɔ ɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chí bɛ mmu ántɔ́ŋ bɛ yi asɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Kristo ndu yi ákɔŋ bo.
Bǒbhɔ nka bɛsa tándrámɔt nsɛm nka ɛnwi báre kway nɛkwáy nɛkɔ bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ bɛsí mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m nɛ bɛsí bǒbati. Yɛ̌ mmu kɛka bɛghɔk nɛkwáy nɔ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chi bǒ nka bɛsa tándrámɔt nsɛm nka ɛnwi abhɛn Mandɛm ápɛ́mɛ́, afɛrɛ amɨk.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánókó Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, ǎbhɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm apú bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m. Kɛ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm bɛ́tɨŋɨ nɛ yi.”
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp báchɛ̀m nyaka amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm amɛm Yerúsalɛm ndu mɛ́nɨ́kmʉɛt. Báchɛ̀m nyaka nkwɔ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap ndǔ Nɛnyiɛ Acha nɛ ndǔ mɛnyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt,
“Mmɨk Sɛ́bulɔn nɛ Náftali, mmɨk anɛ bo báfʉɛ̀t arɛ bɛrɔŋ ndǔ ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛn ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Manyu Gálili, mmɨk anɛ áchí ɛbhěnyɛn nɛgho Jɔ́dan, atú Gálili anɛ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bachi arɛ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, ayoŋ amɨ́k ayɨŋɨ mfay, arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, mpok akway. Chiɛ́ Mɔ́ywɛ kɛnɛ́m bɛ ɛ̌ti ya bo mángɔ́ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛ.
“Ghɔ́k ká ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛnɔkárɛm ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́, fig ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ. Ɛ́náŋ ɛ́mbó bɛtɛm bɛtɔ́, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ́ ɛso ɛ́rɔp chi kɛ́kwɔ́t.
Kɛ mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m, pɛt dɔ́k ghɔ́ yi nɛ manɔ achak amɔt, yɛ̌ bati apay, yɛ̌ arat, bɛ́ bɔ́ mámbák batísiɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛkoŋo chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m, bǎkɛ́ kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bákʉ̀. Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ babhɔŋ bápú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bághàti bho wáwák.
Kɛ ɛnɛ́ Josɛ́f ákàysi ndak anɛ, Mandɛm ató ángɛl ywi amɔt ntá Josɛ́f ndǔ kɛnɔ́. Ángɛl wu aghati yi bɛ, “Josɛ́f, ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Debhít, kɛ́chay bɛsɔt María ndǔ nɛbhay, apɔ́kɔ́ mɛniɛ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ǎchyɛ̀ baghɔkɔ́ bhi maniɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, mmu amɔt amɛm ngɛ́mtáy bho arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ghatí mɔ́maya ánkɔ́rɛ́ nɛwú ɛtayɛsɛ ánchyɛ́ ɛbha mɛnyɨŋ!”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ánókó Yesu, Mandɛm ǎsɔ̀t bɛ yi achi chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛbhé Moses ɛ́pú kwáy bɛ́kʉ nɔ ntá mmu.
Ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu arɔk ntá nnɔ, abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Mma, ndɛ́m mfɔ ánchyɛ mɛ yi?” Nnɔ yi bɛ, “Ntí Jɔ̌n Njwiti.”
Kɛ mmǔ anɛ átè kákátí tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi.
Ató yi ntá ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ María. Abhɨ́kɨ́ re rɨŋɨ nyaka mbakanɛm. Mmu anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Josɛ́f anɛ áfú ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Mfɔ Debhít atɨ nyaka bɛbhay María.
Ɛ́gháka nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ́ntɨ́ bɛ̌ti, ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn nɛ́kú manywɔp byó nɛ ánwi, ndǔ mbʉ́ɛ́p ápɔ̀kɔ bhɛsɛ́ bɛkɨŋɨ manyu Adriya bɛti bhɔ, bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm áchwí bákáysi bɛ nɛ́kú nnyɛ́n nɛ́náŋ nɛ́chí kɛ́kwɔ́t.
“Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka, ndɨŋɨ ɛkɔŋ ɛyɛka nɛ ɛnyǔ bǎsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ mɛ. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ bǎkwàk batɨ nɛ ndǔ bǎté nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ. Nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n bǎkʉ̀ nɛ́nɛ bɛ́chá ɛbhɛ́n mbɨ.
Nɛ ɛnɛ́ Píta abhʉɛ́t bɛkáysi kɛnɔ́ ɛkɔ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ arɛm ntá yí bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, bǒ batí árát báyàŋ wɔ.
Ɛ́chi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmǔ ywɛka amɔt árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ, ‘Nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ́ nɛ́fù chi ntá yi, nɛ yí kɛ áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ bɛtaŋ sɛ́kɔ̀, nɛ yí kɛ ákʉ́ bɛ sɛmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.’ Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk batɛmɛ́ bakay bhɛka bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Bɛsɛ́ nkwɔ́ sɛ́chí bɔ̌ abhɛn Mandɛm.’
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyǔ nɛka ɛnɛ́n bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ yi, aghati mbɛ́ntí wu bɛ, “Nkwánɛ, mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhɛ.”
Mbɛ́ntí wu afate kpɛrɛp, agurɛ.
Nɛ mɛ́máka ndǔ ɛbhɔ̌ mɛnkɛm, Hɛ́rɔd arɛm báfé Jɔ̌n amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. 
Bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛkʉ bo mámbɔ́ŋ kpák nɛ batɨ.”
Nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk, bákɛ́ noko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ, mbɔnyunɛ mmɨkɨ nɛ ǎfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛnkɛm.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkáysí bɛ bo Galili bhɔ bákʉ́ nyaka bɛbʉ́ bacha bǒ ɛtɔk Gálili bachak kɛ?
Mpok apɛ́rɛ́ ghaka anɛ bákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Kristo kɛ ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, sɛchi nyaka antɛnɛ́ bɛbhé, sɛ́bhak mbɔ bo abhɛn báfyɛ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
“Pɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p ghati bo ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ ntá yɛ.” Arɔk yɛ ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ɛnkɛm angati nɔkɔ bo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu akʉ ntá yi. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ bhe mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌ chi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛtaŋ Mandɛm.
Nchí ghati bhe tɛtɛp bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ ámfʉɛt.
Kɛ ángɛl Mandɛm atwɔ́ nɛ bɛti, anɛnɛ babhǐnywɔp ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, asɔt bɔ́ báfú, arɛm bɛ
Yɛ̌ nɔ bǎkɛ́ ŋák chi bɛ, bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɛ́pti mmʉɛt ntá yɛka. Ŋák ka chi bɛ Mandɛm asɨŋ manyɛ́n yɛka amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ amfay.” 
Sɛptí ká mmʉɛt ntá bǒ mbɔ abhɔ nɛ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak anɛ áchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ bhɔ ndǔ bɛtɨk.
Mɛ Jɔ̌n ngɔ nɛ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí, nɛ nchí rɛm mbɔ ntísiɛ bɛ tɛtɛp mmǔ-nɛ chi Mmɔ Mandɛm.” 
Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ wati mɛ ntí nɛ bawɛt kɛ yí ǎwati mɛ bɛkak nɛ bawɛrɛ́riɛp.
Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ chí ndǔ mandú mpok yɛ̌ ndǔ ɛrɔ́rí mpok, nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛna ntá Mandɛm chí bɛ ɛ́kɛ́bhak chi ndiɛrɛ wɔ, kɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achák anɛ áchí fá ɛchɔŋ ághòk mɛ, ámbák mbɔ mɛ ɛbhɨkɨfʉɛt chi bɛbhak nɛ ngɛm amɔ́ mbɔ mɛ.”
Bǒnto abhɛn Yerúsalɛm bághoko nɔkɔ bɛ bǒ-Samaria mánoko Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, bátó Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n arɛ́.
Ɛ́chí mbʉ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ bɛ sɛnkɛm ɛpa ɛ́nɛ, sɛ́nkʉ́ maŋák, mbɔnyunɛ mɔmáyɛ nɛ agǔ nyaka kɛ nɛ́nɛ achi nɛpɛ́m. Anɛm nyaka kɛ sɛ́pɛt sɛghɔ yi.’”
Kɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ghok wáwák. Akʉ bákɛ́m mmʉɛrɛ ywi wu, bárɔk, bafyɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bɛ mbák abhɨkɨ kwɔ barɛm ami ánáŋá, apú fú arɛ́.
Abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ mpok yi ábhó bɛ́chɔkɔ sayri?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́yu ndu nkárɛ́nká amɔt nɛ ngósí.”
Ǎkʉ mángɔ́ bɛ chɔŋ mántáŋ bǒ bɛbʉ́ ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm átáŋ mfɔ mmɨk, afɛrɛ yi ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛki.
Aghɔ́ bachwi apay angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Bawǎnsi abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bachwi yɔ, báfù amɛm mánchaka nɔkɔ basɨ yap.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ɛncha ntá baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn báchi nɛ mɛniɛ nɛ abhɛn báchí nɛ bɔ amɔ mpok yɔ!
Bárɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi nɛfí, mmɔ́ Mfɔ Íjip anɛ ngɔrɛ́, asɔt yi mbɔ mɔ́ywi, ane yi.
Báchyɛ yi mmɛ̌m amɛn báchɔ́bhɛ́ nɛ babhé amɛn bábhɨŋɨ bɛ myrrh. Kɛ Yesu kɛnyu mɔ́.
Kɛ ndǔ bo abhɛn yi ánáká mankɛm, yɛ̌ mmu amɔt abhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ ntí. Mánkʉ nɔkɔ chi ɛbhap mɛnyɨŋ. Amɔt arɔk ɛbhɨ ɛyi, achák arɔk chí ɛkɛrɛ́siɛ ɛyi,
Bě babhɔŋ mǎngati mɛ ndak anɛ: ɛ́chí sayri bɛ ngɔrɛ́ ánɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛntɨ bǒnkwɔ kɛkuti ntí?
Bɔ̌bɛtok bhɔ bárɔ́k bakʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ághátí bhɔ. Bábhɨ́ŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu. Mmǔ mbʉ́mbʉ mǎmbɨŋɨ bhɨ́ŋɨ, mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́ mǎmbɨŋɨ bhɨŋɨ. Ɛ́kʉ́ ɛkɛt ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛ́jwí nɛ bo.
Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ mǎmbɛp Ɛtaya mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna. Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ chɔŋ nɨkmʉɛt ntá yi bɛ ánchyɛ́ bhe ɛnyɨŋ.
Mának nyaka Yesu nkwɔ́ nɛ bakoŋo bhi ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛyɔ.
Mpók yɔ, chɔŋ bo mámbak abhɛn bághàti bhe bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká yi awu!’ Báchák mandɛm bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká yi fá!’ Mbák mǎngók nɔ, bǎkɛ́ rɔŋ, bǎkɛ́ bho bɛ́koŋo bhɔ.
Chiɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn ɛchɔŋ;
Nɛ be bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn ɛtɔk Fílipi, be babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ sayri bɛ mpok njámbɨ ntwɔ́ awu nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ndɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɛka atú Masidónia ndɔk atú ɛtɔk ɛchak, ndiɛrɛ be kɛ̌ bǎtó nyaka mɛ nkáp ndu bɛ́chyɛ mɛ nɛkwak. Yɛ̌ bǒnkwɔ báchák bábhɨ́kɨ́ chɛm amɔ nɛ mɛ ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mɛ́kʉ̀.
Kɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk abhɛsɛ bákɛ́m yi bachyɛ mangway, nɛ bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Yi, Yesu, kɛ Mandɛm arɔ bɛ angu ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ, akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndu bɛkʉ bɛsɛ sɛ́mbak chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ nɛtwɔ́ wa, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm. Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ ngátí bhe bɛ́fàkari, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mpok nɛtwɔ wa arɔp kɛkwɔt.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ amfay. Ɛ́re rɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm aywɛsɛ apɛ́mɛ́ bǒbhi. Chɔŋ ambak Mfɔ bǒbhi, ankɛm bɔ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi. Nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ambɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy mmɨk nkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ mánaŋ basɔt mmu anɛ ábharɛ nɔkɔ bɔ̌mayɛsɛ barak amʉɛt bɛsí Mandɛm bɛti nɛ ngósí, báfɛmɛri fá amɨk.
Nɛ bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛnyu ɛyɔ bátɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ báyàŋ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bɔ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ ɛyap.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, kɛ mbák chi bhe, bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛkwak batɨ, bɛ mǎngó ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnókó, ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fú ntá mbɔŋ Mandɛm. Mpok mǎnɨkmʉɛt dɔ̌ ká Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ankwak bhe.
Bo Israɛl bachi bǒmpap Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo. Ɛ́fakari nɔ ɛ̌ti yɛka bo bǎpú bo Israɛl bɛ mbi ámbák Mandɛm ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhe. Kɛ bo Israɛl báchí mamʉɛrɛ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ yi anáŋ ayap nyaka bhɔ ɛ̌ti bachǐmbɨ bhap.
Yesu apɛt aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Mbák bǎkɔŋ mɛ, bʉrɛ́ ká ɛyɔŋ ɛbha.
Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ, chɔŋ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ́ nchí babhat nɛ Ɛtaya, nɛ bǎchi babhat nɛ mɛ, nɛ nchí babhat nɛ bhe.
Ɛrɛmɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n bátɔ̀ŋ bɛběntɨ ɛbhap nɛ́ghaka. Agha ákway bɛte?”
Bɛsɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm bɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ chi mɛnyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ nɛ ɛbhɛn mɛnyu, nɛ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chák ɛbhɛn bo básɔ̀t mánso mmʉɛt bɛ bákɛ bhɔŋ bakwap bɛsí Mandɛm. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ chi bɛbhé ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ́may mpok Mandɛm átwɔ nɛ ɛnyu ɛkɔ.
Júdas ásɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt ɛyɔ, afú nɛfí tɛ́mté. Nɛ bɛti bɛ́gʉ́. 
Mpok yɔ, Jɔ̌n Njwiti abho bɛ́gháti bho amɛm baso atú Judɛ́ya bɛ,
Ásɨ ájwí nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ nsi, báya bákó ɛbhɨ, bachɔkɔ amɨk bayap nsi ɛnɛ ɛrɨ, báfyɛ́ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ. Báto ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ.
Bě nkwɔ bǎchi nɛpɛ́m. Bák yɛ ka mbɔ batay anɛ básɔ̀t bɛte ɛkɛt ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ábhàk arɛ́. Bǎchi bo abhɛn yi ábhʉ́rɛ́ nyáŋá bɛ mǎmbák nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ́ bachiǎkap, ndu bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka nkɛm ntá yi ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ Mandɛm maŋák ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo.
Abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ndak bǎkɔ̀ mǎndɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛnyunɛ?” Báté nsónso.
yɛ̌ mmu apu yaŋ bɛrɨŋɨ Mandɛm, yɛ̌ mmu apu yaŋ mbi Mandɛm.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ ntɨ nɛ́bé mɛ nɛ mkpáká bobhɔ, ndɛm bɛ, ‘Batɨ̌ yap ápɔ̀kɔ bhɔ ɛbhɨ mpoknkɛm, nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbi wa.’
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mǎnókó nɛ́nɛ?
Píta aghɔ nɔkɔ ndǔ bǒbhɔ bákàp bhɔ, arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, bo Israɛl, ndaká yi bǎchí maknkay, mǎmkpɔkɔ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ? Bǎkaysi bɛ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛsɛ́ kɛ̌ yí ákɔ̀ nɛ́nɛ kɛ? Nɛ puyɛ̌ chi bɛ sɛ́chày Mandɛm tontó.
Kɛ ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp arat nɛ ɛbhɔk Mandɛm ákʉ́ ɛ̌yu ɛyi ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛ́chwé bhɔ amʉɛt. Bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, báteté. Bɛyǎ bɛcháy bɛ́kɛm bo mankɛm abhɛn bághɔ́ bhɔ.
Bakoŋo bhi bárɛm bɛ, “Acha, mbák ǎbhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́, chɔŋ aŋɛmɛ, ambak sayri.”
Mbák chi bɛsɛ, sɛ́bhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bɛsɛ sɛmbak chak bɛsí bhi ɛ̌ti sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Kristo. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ kɛ sɛ́nòŋ ndu bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ bɛ́ ntíánwɔ́p ánkɛ́m bé. Yɛ̌ ndɨŋɨndak apú ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛká anɛ ákwày mɛ́nyúrɛ bo nkwɔ́ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkpɨ́kɨ́ri nɛ batɨ kɛ?
Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm. Yi aywǐnti kɛ áchí Acha. Yí kɛ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ ntá Yesu Kristo bɛ́pɛ́mɛ́ bɛsɛ. Yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛnókó, nɛ kɛnɛ́m, nɛ bɛtaŋ, nɛ kɛfɔ kɛnkɛm, mpoknkɛm anɛ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, nɛ nɛ́nɛ, ngwɛnti ti. Amen.
Nɛka ɛnɛn bǒ bho bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka nɛ Mandɛm kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ mbɔk ayap mánú nɛ bɛtɔk bɛchak básɔt awɔ́nɛm. Báchák bákɛ́m ɛtɔk ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak, nɛ bábhɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ. Nɛka ɛnɛ́n abhɛ́nɛ́fú nɛ́kʉ́ manyǔ anɛ́ nkʉ áchók.
Áchúɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ Yesu achi, arɔk akaka yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ!” Abhɛnɛ yi.
Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛjwi ɛpay, aghɔ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi ndǔ bábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́. Bápú kwáy nyaka bɛ́chɔ́kɔ pě ndǔ kɛnɔ́ kɛ́jwí bɔ amɨ́k.
Are kʉ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn nnya anɛ mbɨ mɛnkɛm bɛsí bhi. Akʉ mmɨk nɛ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ mánchyɛ nnya mbɨ mmǔ ɛfʉɛt ɛyi ɛ́gú kɛnókó.
Nɛ bɛyǎ bo, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm, báré noko, manchɛm nɔkɔ mmʉɛt nɛ nkwɔ́ Yesu.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí ndǔ ndak anɛ, ándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛsɛ́ bǒnto Yesu nɛ batɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm bachak, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́chák bɛrɛm. 
Ɛ́fákári bɛ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi amɔt abhɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu bɛ ányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛkɛt yi. Yesu aka, arɔk, achɔkɔ are nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ yi.
Sɛpɛmɛ mɔ́nɔk mɔ́stat sɛ́chí nɨ́ŋɨ́nɨ́ŋɨ́ tontó, kɛ mbák sɛ́nchák, sɛngo, sɛ́bhak nnɛt mɔ́nɔk anɛ áchɨk. Kɛnɛn kɛ́ntwɔ kɛnte manyay ndǔ batabhɛ yi.” 
Ɛ́chí yɛ bɛ Mandɛm apu yap mmu chi bɛkoŋo nkaysi bakwǎŋwaŋ, nɛ puyɛ̌ chi bɛkoŋo bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn mmu afyɛ́ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk. Ǎyap mmu chi ndu ághɔ̀ yi ntínso.
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ̌ nkʉ ntɨ bɛ mpú pɛrɛ twɔ awu ntá yɛka ndɔŋ achák ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛchɔŋti batɨ ayɛka amɛm.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ ngɔrɛ́ ántɔ́ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ ámbɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay babhakanɛm. Abhɔŋ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ chí kpák.
Chɔŋ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm, nɛ manɛrɛ́kɛt ankɛm, nɛ bǒ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk mɛnkɛm, nɛ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm mántwɔ mámkpɔk bɛrɛnɛ́ bawú bhɔ ndǔ manywɔp arat nɛ ɛbhɔk, kɛka mámbɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ.
Nchí fyɛ nyaka bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nkáysí bɛ Mandɛm kɛ áyàŋ nkʉ bhɔ kpát, nchyɛ́ nɔkɔ Nkwɔ Kristo bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri. Nɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ kɛbhak nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ nchí bhʉɛrɛ nyaka bɛbhé bo Israɛl mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́yàŋ.
kɛ bɔ́ kɛtɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀. Mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ chi ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm mmu achi amfay mbɔnyunɛ bɛfʉɛt ɛbhap nɛ bɛbe bɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka bɔ bachi ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.
ná bǎkway bɛrɛm bɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m bɛ nchí Mandɛm ndǔ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ nchí Mmɔ Mandɛm, mmu yi áyábhɛ́ átó fá amɨk?
María abhɛ́p ángɛl wu bɛ, “Chɔŋ anɛ́ ndak ámbak ná, ɛnɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbakanɛm?”
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ básɨŋ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm kɛ̌ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mmɨk, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí arɛ́.”
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mǎnɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe, nokó ká bɛ mǎnaŋ bǎbhɔŋ yɔ́ nɛ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ yɔ tɛtɛp.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m chi bɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkway bɛrɨŋɨ. Chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mǎnáŋ bǎrɛ́mɛ́ nɛ ɛchi amɛm batɨ yɛka. Bǎkway mɛnoko yɔ ndu yɔ́ ɛchí amɛm manyu yɛka nɛ chi nkúbhɛ́ Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́rɛ kɛ sɛ́ghàti bho.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ kɛfɔ Satan. Mbák Satan ǎbók Satan, ná kɛfɔ ɛki kɛ́tee?
Bǎyáŋ bɛ́bhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ kɛ bǎpú bhɔ́ŋ bɔ́. Ɛ́kʉ bǎyàŋ bɛ́way bho. Nɛ bǎfyɛ̀ ámɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo báchák kɛ bǎpú kwáy bɛ́bhɔŋ bɔ́. Ɛ́kʉ bǎtàŋ nɛ batɨ, mǎnu nɔkɔ. Ntí anɛ bǎpú bhɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chí bɛ́ bǎpú nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ bhé bɔ́.
Mpok yɔ, ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́bhó ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs ɛ̌ti Mbi Yesu Acha.
“Mpú nɨkmʉɛt chi ɛ̌ti bakoŋo abhɛn bɔ́bhɔ, kɛ ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bághòk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ, mánsɨkɨntɨ nɛ mɛ nkwɔ.
Ndǔ bárɔ̀ŋ, bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ́ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ábhó mɛnu, mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛbho bɛdɛp áchwí, manyiɛp anchwe nɔkɔ amɛm. Yesu abhak ndǔ kɛnɔ́.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎkáysí bɛ́ bo bákwày bɛchɔkɔ nsónso ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛnɛ́ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ abhʉɛ́t nɛ bhɔ? Nsé! Kɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ báfɛrɛ chɔŋ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ ntá yap. Nɛ chɔŋ mǎntarɛ nsay mpok yɔ.”
Ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas báfù ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl, bo báre nɨk bɔ́ mmʉɛt bɛ́ mámpɛ́tnsɛm mandɔk ambɨ bɛghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndu nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɛ́n nɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ.
Kɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́chi, Mandɛm aghókó bɛ́pókómʉɛt mɛnkɛm, akʉ bɛ bɔ mɛ́mbak mmu amʉɛt mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyáŋá nyaka bɛ mɛ́mbak.
Kɛ nkoŋo anɛfú wu anɛ ayambɨ áchwɔ́bhɛ́ ndǔ nnɛm achwe amɛm nkwɔ, aghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k, anoko.
Nɛ Símun, mfyɛ̌-bɛtaŋ ndǔ barakátɔk, nɛ Júdas Iskariɔt mmu átí nyaka Yesu. 
Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi mbʉ́mbʉ yap. Arɛm bɛ, “Bě bho bɛtábhá, ndaká yí mǎmɔ̀ mɛ?”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, ngɔrɛ́ ywi Ɛlísabɛt apɔkɔ mɛniɛ. Yí kɛfú nɛfí ndǔ bataŋ átáy andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ,
nɛ Mátio, nɛ Tɔmás, nɛ Jems mmɔ̌ Alfeyɔs, nɛ Símun mfyɛ̌-bɛtaŋ ndǔ baraká ɛtɔk,
Nɛ nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtɔŋ batɨ chi bɛkɔŋ bhɔ. Ɛkɔŋ ɛ́gwɔ̀t mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ndǔ nsoŋ amɔt.
Ghatí yɛ bhɛsɛ, ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛka bɛ sɛ́nchíɛ nkábhɛ́nti ntá Mfɔ Rom kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka?”
Ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ɛ́chí tɛtɛp, kɛ mpok mmu ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, apú káŋ mmú bɛ ɛ́kɛ́ nyiɛ bɛchɔkɔtí ɛbhɛn bákwɛ̀nti amɨk.”
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu andwɔ bhe ndu yɛ̌ mbi, mbɔnyunɛ nywɔp ɛnɔ nɛ́pɛrɛ́ twɔ, bɛyǎ bo báte nɛsaŋ nɛ Mandɛm Acha mámbyaka nɔkɔ bɛbhé bhi kɛ mbʉ́mbʉ ambesi. Ngwɛnti yi chi mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́.
“Ɔ̌yáŋ mɛ̌nkʉ́ wɔ yi?” Akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Acha, nchí yaŋ mpɛt ngɔ mbaŋ.”
Nkaysi mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ áchí mmu antɨ kɛ áyà mmu ankwɛ́n ndǔ nta anɛ nɛmɔ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́.
Kɛ mbák chi bɛsɛ, sɛ́pú bo abhɛn báyà mmʉɛt ansɛm mangu manɛm. Sɛ́chí chí bo abhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ yi ǎpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ.”
Sɛ́nkɛ́m sayri nɛbhakántɨ ɛnɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ ɛbhɛn sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ sɛbhaka ntɨ arɛ́. Sɛ́kɛ́ makati mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm mmu afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ǎbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami.
Bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay áyàŋ bɔ́ mánkʉ kɛ báchí máya nɛ bɔ̌maya.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ, bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛchi mbɔ bɛ sɛ́pɔ́kɔ́ nɛwú Yesu amʉɛt sɛ́kɔ̀ nɛ nɔ. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, bo bághɔ̀ nɛpɛ́m Yesu ndu nɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk amʉɛt yɛsɛ.
Batɨ̌ Bǒ nkwɔ́ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, básɔt yi barɔk Seséria, bátó yí ándɔ́k Tásɔs.
Nywɔp nɛ́mɔ́t, Yesu abhɨŋɨ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay, achyɛ bhɔ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛ́bók mɛnyǔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ mɛnkɛm nɛ ndu bɛ́bu mame.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm mmu árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ kwɛn bɛrwɔp”. Nkúbhɛ́ yí kɛ árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ wáy”. Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ yɛ bɛ́ mbák ɔ́ngwáy mmu, nɔ́ ɔ́kwɛ̌n ɛbhé Mandɛm yɛ̌ndu ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kwɛ́n bɛrwɔp.
Afate abho bɛpɛtnsɛm ntá ɛtayi. Kɛ ɛnɛ́ yi abhʉɛt nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, chi aghɔ́ yi ndu átwɔ̀. Ntínso nɛ́kɛ́m yi, afate, ajɛt arɔk akɛ́m yi abhɛnɛ.
Bákɔt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́pú nyu bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm, mámkpɔti, mansɔŋ ango.
Amɨ́k ayi ághɔ̀ mbɔ nɛrɨ́-ngo. Bɛyǎ ntǎ-kɛfɔ ɛchi yi anti. Básɨŋ nnyɛ́n yi amʉɛt ɛnɛ́n yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chi yímbɔŋ.
Báre rɛm ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ bo Atɛns nɛ mankɔ mankɛm abhɛn báchí arɛ́ bákɔŋ nyaka bɛ́chɔ́kɔ bɛghok nɛ bɛ́fyɛ mbok ɛ̌ti barak akɔ.
Bɛyǎ bo bákóŋo yi arɛ́. Yesu arɔ bho tété, arɔk achwe, achɔkɔ amɛm áchwí ɛnɛ́ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ báté angɔkɔnyɛ́n.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mpok bábhɛ́bhɛ́ yɛ Samuɛl bɛ ánchyɛ bhɔ mfɔ, Mandɛm ayap Sɔ̌l, mmɔ̌ Kish. Kish afú ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Bɛnjamin. Sɔ̌l abhak mfɔ wap ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛ́pay. Kish afú nyaka ndu nnɛrɛ́kɛt Bɛnjamin.
“Yesu, Mmu Násárɛt, ɔbhɔŋ yí bɛkʉ nɛ bhɛsɛ! Ɔtwɔ fá bɛway bhɛsɛ? Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mmǔ wɔ ɔ́chí. Ɔ́chí Mmu Nyáŋá anɛ Mandɛm átó!”
Kɛ mbák chí nkwɛ̌ndɔŋ mǔbɛtɨk nɛ, bwɔ́p ká yi mǎmɛsɛ nɛfí ndǔ ɛjuri, bɛ́ ámbák awu ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ́ ámɛ́n.” 
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmɛ Yesu nto ángɛl wa ntá yɛka beka bǒnkwɔ bha bɛ ángátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Nchí nkaŋánɔk nɛ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít, nchí nɛmbě ŋaŋaŋ ɛnɛn nɛyǐnywɔp.”
“Chɔŋ bafɔ̌ mmɨk abhɛn mányíɛ́ ɛpɔ̌ nɛpɛ́m, mánkʉ nɔkɔ barak ɛ́pusi nɛ yi mándi, mámfyɛ nɛkwɛsɛ́ ɛni mpok bághɔ̀ mɔ́ngo anɛ áfù anko nɔkɔ amfǎy ndǔ yi ásɔ̀ŋɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chí ɛ̌ti bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbɔ bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́n nɛ́chí yɛ̌ chi nɨ́ŋɨ́nɨ́ŋɨ́ mbɔ mɔ́sɛpɛmɛ́nɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ *mɔ́stat,   bǎkwáy bɛghati njiɛ bɛ́ ámfá fá andɔk nɛbhʉɛt áchák, ɛ́mfakari ɛnyu yɔ, nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛkwɛ́y bɛcha bhe. [Bo bákwày bɛ́bók ɛnyǔ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ chí mbák báchí ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay nɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt]”   
“Bɔ̌ma, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti Júdas mmu ákwáká bo mankɛm Yesu bɛbhɔŋ nyaka bɛfu tɛtɛp. Nɔ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ nyaka Mfɔ Debhít ándɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛ arɛm bɛ bɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari.
Mandɛm achyɛ́ nyaka Yesu mbɔ akap, bɛ ɛ̌ti manoŋ mi amɛn árɔ́ŋɔ́ amɨk, Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bo abhɛn mánóko Yesu. Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ nɔ bɛtɔŋ bɛ yi achi chak. Ɛ̌ti ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ ɛyi, asó nyaka bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ́. Ǎghɔ̀ nyaka bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ́ ndu mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm mbɔ bɛ apu ghɔ.
Sɛ́nók sɛ́pé manyu ndǔ ɛbhe ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ atú Silísha nɛ Pamfília sɛ́tɛ́mɛ ɛtɔk Míra ndǔ atú Lúcia.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mmǔ ywɛka amɔt anɛ ásɛbhɛ awɔ ywi amɛm ɛkpʉrɛ́ nɛnyiɛ nɛ mɛ ǎti chɔŋ mɛ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mmá, nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ. Mandɛm achi nɛ wɔ, dɔ́k sayri.”
Kɛ ɛnyǔ mú wu kɛbhɔ́ŋ bakaŋ amɨk. Ante kákáti ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok. Kɛ mpok ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́twɔ́, bo mámbo mɛnyok yi ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ yi ánókó, amfɛrɛ amɔ́ tɛ́mté.
Páílet akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ nnáŋ nsɨŋ.”
Mbák yɛ bapú kway bɛkʉ mandú ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛyɔ, ndaká yi bǎbhɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak?
Mmǔ anɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni, ǎnɛm nɔ́, kɛ mmu anɛ ápú re fyɛ ntí ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛnɛn fá amɨk apu nɛ́m nɔ́, ǎbhɔŋ nɔ́ kpát anchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Nkúbhɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ, Yesu afú amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ yi achi arɛ, arɔk achɔkɔ nɛku manyu.
Banábas are yáŋ bɛ́ mánsɔ́t Jɔ̌n Mák yí ándɔ́k nɛ bhɔ.
Ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ́, nɛrɨŋɨ́kɛpɨ ɛnɛn barɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ́chí fá? Batɔŋɔ́ bɛbhé Moses bárɨ́ŋɨ́ yi? Bǒ mmɨk abhɛn bákɔ́ŋ bɛ́kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí báchí kpɨ́k bɔ agha? Mandɛm atɔŋ bɛ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk nɛ́chí ndɛ́ndɛmɛ́ ndak.
Mbák ɔ́mbɛ́p, chɔŋ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ ɛbhɨ́kɨ́ cha manywɔp byo nɛ apay ɛnɛ́ ndɔ́ŋɔ́ Yerúsalɛm ndu bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ápɨ́, puyɛ̌ chi nnɛrɛ́ nchwi nɛ puyɛ̌ nnɛrɛ́ mbwɔt achak, chi mɔ́nyɛsɛ nchwi, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, mɔ́nyɛsɛ mbwɔt achák.
Ngɔ́ yɛ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ bafɔ̌ mmɨk nɛ bakwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhap ndu báchɛ̀m nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bɛ manu nɛ mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ mpɔŋɔndɨ́k nɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi.
Chwe ká ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ yi áchwe mǎngati mbɔŋɔ́kɛt bɛ, ‘Ɛtayɛsɛ́ ato bhɛsɛ́ sɛ́mbɛp wɔ bɛ, ɛkɛrɛ́ mankɔ ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi arɛ́ ɛ́chi fá?’
Mpok sɛ́chí nyaka nɛ bhe, sɛ́ghàti nyaka be ambɨ ambɨ bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ bɛsɔŋɔri, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́fákárí, nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyu ɛyɔ.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ Ɛta yɛka mmu achi amfay bɛ apú yaŋ yɛ̌ mandú mɔ́ywi amɔt ánɛ́m ɛbhɨ.”   
Yesu achɔkɔ amɨk, abhɨŋɨ bhɔ bati byo nɛ apay, abho bɛghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mmǔ ywɛka anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak mǔngo, abhɔŋ bɛsɔt mmʉɛt yi mbɔ bɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ ambak mǔbɛtok ntá bo bachak mankɛm.”
Yesu akʉ nyaka ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ amɛm ɛtɔk Kána, atú Gálili. Ɛ́bhák ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ yi akʉ́ ndu bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́. Ɛ́kʉ́, bakoŋo bhi mánóko bɛ yi achi Mmɔ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɔ́ nkwɔ́ kɛbhák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bo Israɛl bhɔ bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Akɔŋ nyaka Lásárɔs achá! Ghɔ ndu áré di.”
Baghɔkɔ́ bhi barɛm bɛ, “Acha, ghɔ́ bɔakparɛnja bapay fá.” Aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká nɔ.” 
Nkáp anɛ báchyɛ̀ mmu ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhɔŋ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɔ. Nkáp wu puyɛ̌ akap.
Ngɔ́ bɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ wu anáŋ anyǔ nyaka manoŋ bo Mandɛm abhɛn baway ɛ̌ti bakoŋo Yesu nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt. Manoŋ bo Mandɛm akɛ́m yi mbɔ mmɛ́m. Mpok ngɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ wu mbak maknkay.
Bábháyti ngó nɛntɨ sɛnta. Bo báchɔ́kɔ nɛpaká ngó mángwaka nɔkɔ ngo. Píta achɔkɔ arɛ́ nɛ bhɔ.
Mbák Mandɛm apu nyurɛ bhe mpok anɛ bǎkʉ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákʉ̀ nɛ bɔ̌bhi mankɛm, nɔ bǎpú bɔ̌bhi tɛtɛp. Nɔ nɔ bǎchi chi mbɔ bɔ̌-ɛnɔŋ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánsɔt yɛ mpok nɛ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyi. Bǎkɛ́ bhak mbɔ bɛchɨŋtǐ bho. Bák ká chi mbɔ barɨŋɨ́ndak.
Bo bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Yesu árɔ̀ŋ ndǔ ɛkɛt Sakio, báré nywinti mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Yesu ǎrɔ̀ŋ bɛbhák kɛnkɔ amɛm ɛkɛt nkʉ bɛbʉ́.”
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bákɛ́mɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Arwɔ̌ be nkwɔ bǎgúrɛ́ ɛbhɨ?
Chiɛ̌ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨ́k ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l ákɔ̀ nɛ yɔ́. Nɛ kʉ Pɔ̌l ánchwɔ́p dok ntá gɔ́bhanɔ Fɛ́liks ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛbhɨkɨ fakari nɛ yi.”
Bápɔbhɛ nɔkɔ bɛyɔkɔ yi, báfɛ́rɛ nkú chu yi amʉɛt, básɔ́t ayi yímbɔŋ bákɛ́mɛ yi amʉɛt. Básɔ́t yɛ yi bárɔ́k bɛgo ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Píta aghati bɔ́ mankɛm mámfu nɛfí. Atɛp mánɛ́n amɨk anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm. Ayibhiri mmʉɛt ntá ngu arɛm bɛ, “Tabíta, faté!” Tabíta anɛnɛ amɨ́k. Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Píta afate achɔkɔ chɔ́kɔ́.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ɛncha ntá baghɔrɛ́ nɛ mɛniɛ nɛ abhɛ́n bábhak nɛ bɔ amɔ mpok yɔ!
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu aya yí batú bɛ, “Dɔ́k, kɛ kɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ mmu andɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔghátí mɛ ndak anɛ.” 
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábyàk yɛ ndak anɛ apú byak chi nkwǎ, ǎbyàk chí Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ bhe Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ yi.
Yesu apɛt abhɔ bɛtɔŋ bo angɔkɔ manyu Gálili. Bɛyǎ bho bákoŋo yi arɛ́ báté angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Yesu arɔ bhɔ́ tété, arɔk achwe, achɔkɔ amɛm áchwí.
Ngɛ́p ǎtwɔ̀ chí bɛ́ghɛp aghɛ́p, bɛ́wáy, nɛ bɛ́chɔ́ŋti. Ntwɔ bɛ́ bo mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m nɛ bɛ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɔ nɛ́njwí pɔɔt nɛ áfɔ́k ankɛm.
“Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, nkwaŋankɨ amɔt arɔk bɛtak ɛnyǔ nchwifú amɛm nkɨ̌ ywi.
Mpok yɔ, Yesu anɨkmʉɛt bɛ, “Ɛta, wɔ mmu ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mfay nɛ mmɨk! Nchí chyɛ wɔ bakak ndǔ ɔ́rɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́mbák bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ntá barɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ ntá bo abhɛn bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Ɔnɛ́nɛ́ bhɔ ɔtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mbɔ mǎmbɔ. Ɛta, ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́yáŋá bɛ ɛmbak.”
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ́ ndǔ manywɔp anɛ ngwɛnti, bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri bɛ́bhak fá amɨk.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́ghati bhɛsɛ. Mbák bǎghókó ghok, nɔ bǎrwɔ chí mmʉɛt.
Mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí.
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛ́nɛ́fú ntá bakoŋo bhi ndu bɛtɔŋ bhɔ bɛ, bábhɔŋ mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mpoknkɛm, kɛfɛrɛ ntí arɛ.
mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ mɛmbɔŋ nchyɛ́ bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm, nchyɛ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak bɛ mǎnchók manyǔ bǒmpap abhɛka.
Ɛrɛmɛ́ nkwɔ́ bakók ányìɛ nyaka ambɨ njiɛ anɛ achi kɛkwɔt. Bɛfóŋó bhɔ mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt ntá Yesu bɛ́ ándɔ́ bɔ́ mándɔ́k mǎnchwe amʉɛt bakok bhɔ. Yesu achyɛ bhɔ mbi.
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mɛ, mmu nchí rɛm nɛ́ kɛpɨ nɛ wɔ, kɛ nchí Mpɛmɛ.”
Chɔŋ mángɔ bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ chɔŋ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛmbak ndǔ bafó ayap.
Nɛ bǒnkwɔ mankɛm báchí mmʉɛt Yesu. Amʉɛt bǒnkwɔ kɛ bághɔ bɛrɨ̌ Kristo mɛnkɛm nɛ mbák chi Kristo, amʉɛrɛ-yi kɛ bo bághɔ bɛrɨ Mandɛm.
Ángɛl wu aghati mɛ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ, “Kɛ́se ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p ɛyɔ nɛ ɛ́bhánɛ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́sɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm mɛ́mbák bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́.”
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ángɛl anɛ ájwí bati tándrámɔt afe aywi mmbá. Ngók bɛtaŋtí bɛyɔŋ amfay, mɛ́ndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm Acha aywɛsɛ kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm mmɨk nkɛm nɛ́nɛ mbɔ Mfɔ mpoknkɛm. Yí kɛ ákɛ̀m mmɨk nɛ́nɛ nɛ Mpɛmɛ yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.”
Mandu yís ǎkʉ fláwa anɛ bábáy ndǔ ɛte ánkó nkɛm.
Ɛkʉ́ bo bare bɨti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ya.
Nchí yaŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ Kristo ndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chí ambɨ, nɛ nchí yaŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ nyaka ákʉ́ Yesu ápɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Nchí yaŋ mbat mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu, nka ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ yi, nchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ yi ndǔ nɛwú ɛni. Nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt bɛsí Mandɛm, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka kpát aka nɛwú
Pɔ̌l nɛ mmʉɛrɛ ywi bárɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bo bhɔ mángɔ́ bɛ́ bɔ́ nkwɔ́ báchí chí bakwǎŋwaŋ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bábhɨ́kɨ́ kwáy bɛchyɛt bɔ mbi bɛ́ bɛ́kɛ́ chyɛ bhɔ́ akap anɛ́ babhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ chi ntá Mandɛm.
Sɔt nkáp aywɛ dɔ́k. Mɛmbɔŋ kɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛchyɛ mmu anɛ abho bɛtɨk ndɔbhɛnsɛm nkáp bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp nɛmɔt mbɔ ɛnyǔ nchyɛ́ wɔ.
Kɛ Píta ataŋa bɛsí bǒ abhɛn bachi arɛ mankɛm bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m nɔ.”
Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nyaka chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ yímbɔŋ maŋák. Kɛ ɛ́fákári nɛ yi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Nsɔk ɛnɛ bo abhɛn básɔ̀kɔti nyaka wɔ ɛ́kwɛn mɛ amʉɛt.”
Nchí rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́pú amɛm batɨ yɛka.
bǒbati ɛsa nsɛm manwi báré kwɛn bɛsí mmu anɛ achí ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ mánchyɛ nɔkɔ yi mmu achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm kɛnókó, nɛ mángʉɛbhɛ nɔkɔ ntǎ-kɛfɔ ɛyap amɨk bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ mánkway nɔkɔ bɛ,
Káyfas abhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm nyaka nɔ chi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú ndǔ nkaysi yi. Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ nyaka bɛ yi andɛm nɔ mbɔ mǔngo bachiǎkap ndǔ mmíɛ́ ɛnɔ. Arɛm bɛ́ chɔŋ Yesu ángú ɛ̌ti bo Israɛl mankɛm.
Tímɔti, nchí kaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛ. Nchí nɨkmʉɛt ntá yi nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛchí amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p mbɔ bachǐmbɨ bha bákʉ̀ nyaka. Nchí nɨkmʉɛt ndu bɛ́káka Mandɛm bɛti nɛ ngósí, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok, anɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛ́kwɛ́n wɔ amʉɛt.
Bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɛta, ghati bhɛsɛ, chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari nɔ ntɨkɨ mpok, nɛ ntɨkɨ ɛrɨŋ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bo mándɨŋɨ bɛ mpok anɛ ɔ́twɔ̀ arɔp kɛ́kwɔ́t.”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛ́wákári bɛta batú ndu bɛ́ghok mɛnyɨŋ, kɛ ákɛ́ wakari bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ ákɛ́ wakari bɛ́bentɨ.
Yesu abók ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ. Ɛ́rɔ́ mmu wu, abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ tɛ́mté. Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́, babhak maknkay, bábhó bɛrɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛnyu fá amɛm ɛtɔk Israɛl.”
Mbák tɛtɛ̌tɛp bǎbhʉɛrɛ nnɛ́m ɛbhé Mandɛm Mfɔ ywɛsɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́chí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Kɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ”, nɔ́ bǎkʉ̀ sayri.
Pú mmɔ̌ nchwɛ̌ mɛnɔk nɛ? Pú mmɔ̌ María nɛ? Pú yi achí manɔ́ Jems, nɛ Júdas nɛ Símun? Pú bɔ̌máyi abhɛn baghɔrɛ́ bachí fá nɛ bhɛsɛ́?” Ɛkʉ́ bare byak yi byak.
Amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ bhɔ tɛ́mté, bapɛt babho bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Yesu asɛmti bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari.”
Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ kɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ tɛ mpok Yesu ábhɨ́kɨ́re two fá amɨk. Afʉɛ́t ntá barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi bɛkʉ nɔ, nɛ bɔ básɨ́ŋ ɛ̌ti bariɛp amɔ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm.
Páílet arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka sayri bɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap bákɛm Yesu bátwɔ ntá yi nɛ yi chi ɛ̌ti mpabhamɨ́k.
Ghók ká, mɛ Pɔ̌l nchí ghati bhe bɛ mbák mǎnka bɛ mansyɛp bhe nɛ nkaysi bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ mǎmbak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Kristo ákʉ́ ntá yɛka ɛpu yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mbɔk bo Yerusalɛm báré rɛm yɛ bɛ, “Pú mmǔ rɛ́ báyàŋ bɛway nɛ?
Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Mandú mpok, mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ, ǎtwɔ, nɛ apú chɔŋti mpok.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Yesu Acha antɔ́ŋ be ɛnyǔ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhe nɛ ɛnyu bɛkɛpntɨ mbɔ Kristo. 
Nsɨŋ bɛkʉ mǎntɨk nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm bárɛ́mɛ́ tɛ́ntɛp bɛ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛfakari, nɛ bɛ mǎntɨk nkwɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Acha mmu achi Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ afʉɛrɛ ntá bǒnto aghati bhe bɛ mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ.
Báré cháy bɛ chɔŋ mbʉ́ɛ́p ámpɔkɔ áchwí wu ándɔk ántɛm ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́, nɛ́kú nnyɛ́n. Báfɛ́rɛ yɛ baro ánwi ansɛm áchwí mámɛ́sɛ anyɛ́n bɛ́ andɔ́p téé, báré nɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ nywɔp nɛ́njí nɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ bhɔ.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, apɛt abhɨŋɨ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́ arɛm bɛ, “Bě mankɛm, tá ká batú mǎngok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm, mǎnjwimɛm!
Bɛyǎ bɛcháy bɛkɛm bǒnkwɔ Yesu mankɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak anɛ aghoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari. 
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chi ɛ̌ti Mfɔ Debhít mbɔnyunɛ Debhít ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɨk Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yi ánkʉ́ fá amɨk ndu ayi mpok, agú akoŋo bachǐmbɨ bhi. Apɔɔ ndǔ nnɛm.
Ákʉ́ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ ɛnyu yɔ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ndu bɛkwak bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ntɔ́ŋ bo abhɛn mpok anɛ átwɔ̀ ansɛm ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi bɛyǎ tontó ɛnyu ɛnɛ sɛ́pú kway bɛyɛnti bhɔ.
Nɛ mpok mbʉ́ɛ́p ǎdɛp áchwí, sɛ́kɛpɛrɛ kway mɛ́nok bɛrɔŋ tɛbhɛ tɛbhɛ nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p. Sɛ́kpɨ́k sɛ́rɔ́ bɛ wu ámpɔ́kɔ́ áchwí.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu afa abho bɛpɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm. Nsay akɛ́m yi.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ bághàti nyaka Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ yɛ̌ chí ntá bawú bɛ́ yɛ̌ndu bágú mbɔ ɛnyǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu, mánkwáy bɛbhak nɛpɛ́m ndu ɛfóŋó mbɔ Mandɛm. 
Yɨŋɨ́ ká bɔchuchu abhɛn bágò. Bápú kʉ bɛtɨk, nɛ bapu ghoko ndɛn. Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, yɛ̌ chí Mfɔ Sólomon mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛyǎ kɛnɛ́m, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka ndɛn ɛnɛ ɛrɨ mbɔ yɛ̌ chuchu amɔt.
Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ́ ndǔ mpok anɛ bɔ babhɨkɨrɛ rɨŋɨ nkaysi yi. Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ághàti bo mankɛm mbankɛm bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu antɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi,
Kɛ mbɔk yap bábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ báfyɛ nyaka bariɛp nɛ Mandɛm bɛ babhɔŋ bɛkʉ chi bɛ Mandɛm apu pɛrɛ bhʉrɛ bariɛp ami kɛ?
Ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛbhák nɛ nnɛ́m aywi tɛ ndiɛrɛ nɛwú. Kɛ mbák nnɛ́m agu, abhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛ́bháy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achák anɛ yí ákɔ́ŋɔ́. Kɛ mmu wu abhɔŋ bɛbhak chí mmu anɛ áchí nkoŋo Yesu Acha.
Mpok nchí ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bo abhɛn báchí arɛ. Ntɨkɨ nsáy mɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nɛnu ɛnɛ́n mɛ́nù ɛnɛ́n nnú nɛ nnyǎbhɨ ɛyɔ mbák bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m? Mbák bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, “Sɛ́nyíɛ́, sɛ́nyú, mbɔnyunɛ mandú mpok sɛ́gu.”
Ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́káysí bɛ ɛrɨ ɛ́ndɔ́p chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bo básɔ̀t bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛ.
Arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, atɔ́ŋ bɔ́ amɔ yi nɛ bɛkak.
Ɛrɛm ɛtɔk ɛ́kɔ́rɛ ndǔ bɛbhɔk bɛrat. Bɛtɔk bɛgho nɛ bɛtɔk mmɨk bɛchak bɛ́kwɛ́n. Mandɛm akɛ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛrɛm ɛtɔk Bábilɔn ndǔ bɛkʉ yɔ ɛnyu mmɛ́m bɛběntɨ bhi.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mányùrɛ mmu ɛ́bhak ntá yi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhɨkɨ rɨ, puyɛ̌ mbɔ ɛnɛ ɛrɨ. Kɛ ansɛm mpok, bo abhɛn bághɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛkɔ mpok anɛ mányùrɛ bhɔ, bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ kpák ǎbhak amɛm batɨ yap. 
Bágháti yɛ mɛ bɛ, “Ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́pɛ́t bɛrɛm nkaysi Mandɛm anɛ áyɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛyǎ bho, nɛ bɛyǎ bɛtɔk, nɛ bɛyǎ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk, nɛ bɛyǎ bafɔ.”
Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bárɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́yàŋ bɛ ɔ́nkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́nɨkmʉɛt bɛ ɔ́nkʉ ntá yɛsɛ.”
Ntɔŋ ɛbhé Moses amɔt achi nyaka arɛ. Aghók ndu Yesu árɛmɛ nɛ bǒ nkwɔ Sádusi. Nɛ ághókó nɔkɔ ndu Yesu ákɛ́mɛ́ bɛbhɛp ɛbhap nɛ bɛyǎ kɛboŋ abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chá bɛchak mɛnkɛm chi ɛnɛ́?”
Kɛ yi kɛ rɨŋɨ mmu wu. Yesu ábú nyaka yi anɔnɛ arɔk mbɔnyunɛ bɛyǎ bo báchí nyaka arɛ́.
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ mbák chí nkaysi Mandɛm, yi ánkwak mɛ mbɔ̌ŋ mbi bɛ́twɔ awu nɛ́nɛ ndu bɛghɔ bhe. Nnáŋ njambɨ nnu bɛ́twɔ awu ndɔŋ ɛchak.
Básɔ́t mmǔ amɔt bárɔ́k ntá yi nɛ yi. Mbaŋ yi kɛ ghók, kɛpɨ yi kɛrɛm kɔkɔ kɔkɔ. Mánɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ́ ányáŋá yi amɔ anti.
Nɛ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛsɔt mpok bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti nɛjwiti, nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛpɨŋ mɛ́nyáŋa bho amɔ́ anti, nɛ ɛnyǔ mbúrɛ́ Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ ɛ̌ti nɛtáŋ anɛ mbúrɛ́ bátàŋ bo mámkpɔt manyé yap ndɔŋ amɔt ndak amay.
Ɛ́chí bɛ́ sɛ́bhɔŋ nkaysi amɔt nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ bɛ sɛ́kɛ́ chyɛ bhe batu áchák anɛ acha bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhʉrɛ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛghati Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ tó ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Sádis. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ bɔ mandɨŋɨ bɛ bɛyɔŋɔ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfóŋó Mandɛm tándrámɔt nɛ mambe tándrámɔt. ‘Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka. Bǎbhɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí nnyɛ́n bɛsí bho bɛ bǎchí nɛpɛ́m, ɛnɛ́ bǎchi bawú.
Mmu akɛ́ rwɔ mmʉɛt, yɛ̌ mmu ápú kwáy bɛrwɔ Mandɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mmu ápɨ́, yɔ́ kɛ yi aghɛm.
“Ghók ká, Nchí to bhe ntá bǒ mmɨk mbɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n nɛntɨ nkwɔ. Bák yɛ́ ka bǒ kɛ́ŋwáŋ mbɔ nnyɔ́, mǎmbɔ́ŋ batɨ pɛ́pɛ́p mbɔ bɛbhóŋó.
Bariɛp amɛn ayɨ́ŋɨ́ be nɛ bɔ̌bhɛka, nɛ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ. Ayɨ́ŋɨ́ nkwɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ Mandɛm Acha yɛsɛ ábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ antwɔ ntá yi.”
Mfɔ arɛm ntá nkʉbɛtɨk wu bɛ, ‘Mɛ̌chyɛ̀ wɔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kɛ́m bɛtɔk bɛgho bɛtay.’
Báchɛ́m bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́náŋ ɔ́bhʉ́rɛ́ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari.
Bo báyàp yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔngo bachiǎkap ndǔ nkwɔ wap, mámbʉrɛ, yi ankʉ nɔkɔ bɛtɨk Mandɛm ndǔ ntí wap. Yi kɛ ásɔ̀t yɛ akap anɛ bho nɛ akabhɛ́nya nkwɔ ánchyɛ̀ nɔkɔ ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bho.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhák ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí bɛpay ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ mpok yi áfú atú Judɛ́ya arɔŋɔ atú Gálili.
Chɔŋ nsay apú pɛrɛ nu bhɔ, manyiɛp kɛpɛrɛ kwak bhɔ, mmok kɛpɛrɛ kway bɛsɔŋ bɔ amʉɛt, nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛchak kɛpɛrɛ kway bɛsɔŋ bɔ amʉɛt,
Mpú yaŋ mǎndɔ abhɔt ánkɛ́m be. Nchí yaŋ chi bɛ mǎnkoŋo ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ bo abhɛn mánókó, nɛ bábhɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ bághaka ndǔ nté anɛ bábhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ. 
“Nɛ ndaká yí bǎbhɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti ndɛn ɛnɛ bɛ́fyɛ́ amʉɛt? Yɨŋɨ́ ká ɛnyǔ bɔchuchu abhɛn bachi ɛbhɨ bágò. Bápú kʉ bɛtɨk nɛ bapu ghoko ndɛn.
Mbɔ ɛnyǔ miámiaŋ ákɔ̀t angɔɔ, bɛfu ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nɛbu ɛ́mɔt bɛghaka ɛ́chák, nɔ́ kɛ̌ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak mpok Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ.
Mpu sɔt bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mbɔ bɛ bɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, mbɔnyunɛ mbák mmu ǎbhák chak bɛsí Mandɛm chi ndu yi ákoŋo bɛbhé, nɔ nɛwú Kristo agu nɛ́chí ndɛ́ndɛm!
Ɛchi yɛ mbɔ bɛ manaŋ babhɛmɛ nyaka bhɛsɛ nɛ yi mpok bajwiti bhɛsɛ, bɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ ákʉ́ nyaka Kristo apɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m ndu bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bɛcha, bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛ́nkwáy bɛbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ.
Bátó mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ mbɔk bo Israɛl abhɛn báté ansɛm Hɛ́rɔd ntá Yesu ndu bɛbhɛp yi mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ntá ndu bɛkʉ yi ankwɛn anyu.
Kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu yɔ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka. Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak mǔngo ywɛka, abhɔŋ bɛbhak mǔbɛtok ywɛka,
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt arɔk ntá Yesu nɛ bɛti arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ̌ átó wɔ bɛ ɔ́ntwɔ́ ɔ́ntɔ́ŋ bo mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ̀ mbák Mandɛm apu nɛ yi.”
Mandɛm anáŋ atɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ndu átó Yesu Kristo mmu átwɔ́. Yí achi Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ. Awǎy bɛtaŋá nɛwú nɛ achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Yɔ́ achí mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ mbi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɔ bǎchí amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ mbʉ́ bɛbʉ́ bɛ́pú nɛ bhe. Kɛ tɛ̌ndu bǎrɛ̀m bɛ bǎghɔ̀ mbaŋ, bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka bɛrɔp nɛ bhe.”
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bǎchí mbɔ manɛm anɛ mmu ákɔ̀ amfay kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi manɛm.”
Arɛm ntá Ábraham bɛ, ‘Ǎe Ɛta Ábraham, ɛyɔ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kway. Mbák mmu amɔt anɛ ánáŋá ágú ámpɛ́tnsɛm angati bhɔ, chɔŋ mántɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap.’
Kɛ be babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ Tímɔti átɔ́ŋ bɛ achi ɛrɨ́tí nkʉbɛtɨk Yesu Kristo Acha nɛ mǔbɛtok bo bachak nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm. Akwak mɛ bɛ́gháti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu mbɔ mmɔ́ anɛ ákòŋo ɛ́táyi ansɛm bɛkʉ bɛtɨk.
Mbák nkʉ́ batɨ ánchɔ́ŋɔ́ be amɛm, agha achák áchi awu anɛ ákway bɛkʉ mɛ mbɔ́ŋ maŋák? Pú nkúbhɛ́ be mbák nkʉ batɨ áchɔ́ŋɔ́ be amɛm?
Mbɔŋ Yesu Kristo Acha nɛ Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ mmu akɔŋ bhɛsɛ mántɔ́ŋ bɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ mpoknkɛm nɛ nɛbhakántɨ ndǔ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari.
Nɛ mbák básɔt bhe nɛ ɛkɔŋ, nɨk ka mmʉɛt bɛ áfɔ́k Mandɛm ámbák nɛ bhɔ. Kɛ mbák bábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt bhe nɛ ɛkɔŋ, nɨk ka mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánkɛ́m áfɔ́k ywi, kɛchyɛ bhɔ.
Báchák bɛ, “Ɛláija kɛ ábhésí.” Nɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ, “Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt anɛ tɛ nyaka kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi basɛm bábhɔŋ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó ntá bachi bhap bɛ bo bákɛ́ rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti nnyɛ́n Mandɛm nɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ.
arɛm bɛ, “Kʉ ká mɛnkwɔ́ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ yɛ̌ agha anɛ nyáŋá yi amɔ́ anti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ántwɔ́ ntá yi.”
Bo básɔ́kɔ́ti mbɔk yap, nɛ bádákáti nsɛm ɛyap nɛ bɛkpa. Báfyɛ́ báchák ngɛm amɔ́ nɛ mamɛsɛ bhɔ amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, dɔ̌ ká baraká nse. Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́ndɛm nɔkɔ chi tɛtɛp nɛ batɨ, mbɔnyunɛ sɛchi mbɔ bɛpókómʉɛt nyáŋá nyáŋá ndǔ mmʉɛt amɔt.
Mbuɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mɔ́mbi chi bo abhɛn bághókó Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Kɛ Satan antwɔ́ amfɛrɛ yɔ́ ndǔ batɨ yap bɛ bákɛ́ noko Mandɛm yi ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí ghati bhe chi bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɔ̀ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay ɛnɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ ábhɨ́kɨ́ kwɛn bɛrwɔp, akʉ ngɔrɛ́ akwɛn bɛrwɔp, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbakanɛm anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ápɛ́t apu ɛkɛrɛ́nɛbhay, akwɛn nkwɔ bɛrwɔp.” 
Yesu aghɔ́ yi ntínso. Anyabhɛ awɔ, atɔk yi, arɛm bɛ, “Nkɔŋ, ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛ́may!”
Bághókó manyǔbha byo nɛ apay nɛ batay bɛyǎ nkáp anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ pɛ́l. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nyǔbha abhak ntay pɛ́l nɛmɔt. Nkɔngɔ abhak pú pú, aŋaŋari nɔkɔ mbɔ ɛ́kírísú.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bábhɨ́ŋɨ bo ndǔ ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒbati Israɛl. Báchɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bárɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ sɛ́nkʉ ná? Mmǔ-nɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛyǎ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay.
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Acha mɛ́mbák nɛ bo Mandɛm mankɛm. Amen!Nsáy ya achí yɛ́ bɛ́ yi ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn? Nsáy ya achí chí maŋák amɛn mbɔŋɔ bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ndɛ́ndɛm, nkɛ yáŋ nsáy anɛ ngati Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhɔŋ.
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi abhɛn bachi arɛ́, bábháka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ mámbɔŋ mbi ndu bɛrɛm bɛ yi akʉ ɛbɛ́ptí ndak. Bátɛ́p yɛ yi amɨ́k amʉɛt ndu bɛghɔ mbák chɔŋ Yesu ambú mmǔ wu ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Ɛfóŋó yi ɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm, afate tɛ́mté. Yesu achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ manchyɛ yi nɛnyíɛ́ ányiɛ.
Sɔt mpok nɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ. Kɛ́m bɔ́ nɛ bɛtaŋ mbɔnyunɛ mbák ɔ́nkʉ ɛnyu yɔ, chɔŋ ɔ́mpɛmɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ nɛ bo abhɛn ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chɔŋ mángwɔp yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ, mámfɛrɛ.
Yesu ayɨŋɨ bhɔ diíí, arɛm bɛ, “Ntá nkwǎŋwaŋ, mbi ápú, kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú cha Mandɛm.”
Abho yɛ bɛ́bɨ́k bɛ, “Yesu! Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít! Ghɔ́ mɛ́ ntínso!”
Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ Mandɛm nɛ amɨ́k. Kɛ mbák sɛ́nkɔŋ batɨ, Mandɛm ǎbhak nɛ bhɛsɛ nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛyi ɛnjwi bhɛsɛ antɨ pɔɔt.
Mfɔ akɛmɛ yɛ bhɔ bɛ ‘Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mǎnísí nyaka bɛkʉ bɛrɨ ntá yɛ̌ chí mmu amɔt anɛ ápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bɛ mɛ kɛ̌ mǎnisi nyaka bɛkwak.’
Yesu asɛmti bhɔ bɛ́ bákɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu bɛ yi achi Mpɛmɛ.
Ná ɔ́ghàti ntɨ bɛ, ‘Manɔ́, dɔ̌ mfɛ́rɛ́ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨ́ŋɨ́ anɛ achi wɔ anyɛ́sɛ́,’ ɛnɛ́ wɔmbɔŋ ɔpú ghɔ́ nkɔkɔ́nɔk anɛ achi amɛm ɛnɛ nyɛ́sɛ́? Wɔ mmǔ bɛtábhá! Fɛrɛ́ kpɨ́k nkɔkɔ́nɔk anɛ achi wɔmbɔ̌ŋ anyɛsɛ, kɛ ɔ́ngɔ yɛ mbaŋ sayri ndu bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨ́ŋɨ́ anɛ achi amɛm nyɛ́sɛ́ manɔ́ywɛ.” 
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchí arɛ bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri wɔ! Agha áyàŋ bɛway wɔ?”
Nɛtɛ́m anɛ bɔ́ bɛ́bho bɛ́tɛm bɛtɔ́, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛso ɛ́rɔp chi kɛ́kwɔ́t.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ báre fʉɛt atú Gálili mándɔk nɔkɔ. Akɛyáŋ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi achi,
Nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́ghɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chi bɛbhɛrí bɛ́bhɛ́rí mbɔ bɛ sɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ chí ɛ́kírísú ɛnɛ ɛchí bɛbhɛrí bɛ́bhɛ́rí. Kɛ mpok yɔ ánkwáy, chɔŋ sɛ́ngɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sayri nɛ amɨ́k. Nɛ́nɛ, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ chí mbɔk mbɔk, kɛ mpok yɔ ánkwáy, chɔŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sayri nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm árɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ sayri.
Sɛ́nchíɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm Mmu achi Chi ntá Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo! Ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ ntínso ɛni, achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ndu ákʉ́ Yesu Kristo áfú ndʉ́ nɛwú apɛtnsɛm ndʉ́ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ sɛ́bhaka ntɨ nɛ́nɛ bɛ chɔŋ sɛmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m nɛ yi.
Nɛ mpok nchí Yerúsalɛm, bǒ batí bachiǎkap nɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk báré bhat yí barak amʉɛt nɛ báré yáŋ bɛ mɛnchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ mángwáy yi.
Kɛ Mandɛm anáŋ ayap nyaka mɛ tɛ ndǔ mpok anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re bhe mɛ. Ayap mɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi, abhɨŋɨ mɛ bɛ mbak mmɔ̌bɛtok ayi.
Baghɔ́ ayap arɛ tiɛ bho mbɔ ngá-nɛghay. Nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yɔ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bǒ mangok bɛbe ndǔ bataŋ atay bɛre fu ndǔ baghɔ yap.
Mbák mmu abhɔŋ chi akap bɛfyɛ bo ntɨ, ɛrɨ yi ankʉ nɔ. Mbák mmu ábhɔ́ŋ akap bɛchyɛ bo mɛnyɨŋ, ánkʉ nɔ nɛ awɔ́ fúú. Nɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap bɛbhak mǔnti, ánkɛ́m bo abhɛn bachi antɛn yi sayri. Nɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap bɛtɔŋ bo bɛrɨ̌ntɨ, ánkʉ́ nɔ nɛ maŋák.
Nɛ mánaŋ batɔŋ be mɛnyɨŋɨ́ tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm afaté bɛsí bo ɛchɛmɛ ɛyɔ abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkɛmɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒ bhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ ɔkʉ?”
Mandɛm ápɛ́rɛ́ ghoko mmɨk, anáŋ ayap nyaka bhɛsɛ ndu áchɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo, bɛ sɛ́mbák nyáŋá, kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛsí bhi.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́chí yɛ́ bɔ̌ Mandɛm, sɛ́kɛ́ kaysi bɛ́ Mandɛm achí mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mmu ákwày bɛ́sɔt gol nɛ yɛ̌ chí silbha nɛ yɛ̌ chí ntáy angoko nɛ kɛboŋ ɛki nɛ ɛka ɛyi nkwɔ.
Bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti nywɔp ɛnɛn mbúrɛ́. Chɔŋ mbúrɛ́ antwɔ nɛ ayi barak anɛ mmu afyɛ́ ntí arɛ. Bǎkɛ́ sɔt bɛsɔŋɔri bɛchak mǎmáká ndǔ ɛbhɛn ɛchɔŋ.”
“Mandɛm akʉ bɔ́ mámbák amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́, agwɔ́t batɨ ayap, báchí mbɔ bo abhɛn bákútí amɨ́k bɛ bákɛ́ ghɔ́ mbaŋ, nɛ bɛ́ batu yap ákɛ́ ghók yɛ̌nyɨŋ, nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ jwimɛm, mantwɔ ntá ya, mbú bhɔ.”
Bɔ̌ma, mbák chi mɛ, mbɔ mbʉɛ́t bɛghati bho bɛ babhɔŋ bɛsyɛp mmu kɛ yi ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, mbʉ bo Israɛl báchyɛ̀ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ndaká yi? Mbʉ́ mbok nɛwú Yesu ndu ɛkotákátí apu chyɛ bo Israɛl ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ɛ́chí mbɔ bɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛsɛ́ bǒnto Yesu sɛ́mbák bǒ abhɛn báchókó nnɛt nɛntɨ bǒnkwɔ mankɛm. Sɛ́chí mbɔ bǒ abhɛn báré kʉ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ndak, manyé ákwɛ́n bhɔ́, bápɔ́kɔ yɛ bhɔ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ bɛ́wáy bɛsí bo mankɛm, bɛsí bǒ mmɨk nɛ bɛsí bɔángɛl.
Nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́msi mbɔ ɛkáti nɛnɛp ɛnɛ bápɛ́t báfɛ́rɛ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ njiɛ afa ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yɔ achi, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmɨk anɛ achi nɛntɨ nnyɛ́n afa ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yɔ achi.
Bǒnto Yesu báre kʉ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bɛchak bɛsí bo ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. Báre chɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt amɛm nɛbhʉɛt ɛkɛrákap anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka bɛ Acha Sólomon.
Bǒbhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bárɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bábhɔŋ bɛgu. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ nɛ bárɔ̀ŋ tɛ ambɨ bɛka nɛ bo bachak abhɛn bákʉ̀ bhɔ bɛ ɛrɨ bɛkʉ bhɔ.
Nɛ mbák nchí bók bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Bɛlsɛbul, bǒ bhɛka básɔ̀t bɛtaŋ ághá bɛ́bók bhɔ mɛ́ndɔ́ bhó? Ɛ̌ti yɔ chɔŋ bɔ́ mántaŋ be.
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ bɛsí Yesu, akwɛ́n yi bɛkak ankaka nɔkɔ yi. Ɛ́fákárí bɛ mmǔ wu achí chi mmu Samária.
Wáwák! Bɛsɛ bho sɛrɔbhɛ chi mbɔ bawú ndǔ nté yɛsɛ nɛ bɛbʉ́, sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́?
Bǒnto Yesu bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm, bágháti Yesu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bákʉ́. Asɔt yɛ bhɔ ansɛm, bárɔ́k ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Bɛtsáida.
Yesu kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ abhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ kɛnókó ancha Moses, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmu anɛ áté ɛkɛt ábhɔ́ŋ kɛnókó acha ɛkɛt ɛnɛ yi ate.
Mɛ mmǔ Yesu Kristo Acha, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák bɛ yɛ̌ndu ɛ́náŋ ɛ́tárɛ́, bǎpɛt bǎtɔ̀ŋ ndǔ akap anɛ bǎtó mɛ bɛ bǎbhɨkɨ ghɔkɔntɨk mɛ. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎkaysi mɛ mpoknkɛm, kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka chi mbi bɛkwak mɛ.
Josɛ́f arɔk aku ɛ́síɛndɛn. Afɛrɛ yi asɛbhɛ amɨk. Anɛ́p nɛ ɛ́síɛndɛn ɛyɔ, arɔk afyɛ́ yi amɛm nnɛm ɛnɛ́n bátɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́. Afú abɨŋɨri yɛ ɛrɛmɛ́ ntay akuti nyǔnɛm.
Mfɔ Agripa akɛmɛ bɛ, “Pɔ̌l, ɔkáysí bɛ́ ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok anɛ kɛ̌ ɔ́kwày bɛkʉ mɛ mbak mǔnkwɔ Kristo?”
Kɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ɛtaya ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨk mpoknkɛm, nɛ mɛnkwɔ́ mbɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk.”
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ nyaka bɔángɛl mándɔ́k ndɛ́ndɛm mpok bákʉ́ bɛbʉ́, kɛ amɛsɛ bhɔ amɛm nɛpi, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ágiri pyɔ́ɔ́, afe bɔ arɛ́ nɛ ngɛm bɛ mámbák arɛ tɛ mpok manyé ankway.
Sɔt ka bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́re sɛnɛ ndǔ baraká Mandɛm amʉɛt. Kɛ bǎkɛ́ kɛ́m ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ ɛ̌ti ayap nkaysi.
Chí amɛm ntɨ mmu kɛ̌ nkaysi mbʉ́mbʉ áfù, antɛ́n yi ndǔ ɛpúsí, nɛ bɛway mmu, nɛ bɛkwɛn bɛrwɔp, nɛ
Kɛ bápú foŋori yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Ɛ́yɔ̌ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ bɛ́tɨŋɨ mmu anti, ngwɛnti ti.”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp árát, bǒ bɛtɨk babho bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ áchwí mbɔ manɨk nɛ bɛchak mánto nɔkɔ anyɛ́n.
Bɛ̌ bǎbhɔŋ kɛ bachí ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ. Básɨŋ ɛkáti ɛyɔ chi amɛm batɨ ayɛsɛ,   bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ampay andɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bo sɛ́chi.
Kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp árát, Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m, atɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt kpoŋoroŋ ntá bo.
Ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ maŋák ama ámbák nɛ bhe, nɛ bɛ maŋák amɛka anjwi pɔɔt.
Mpok ngátí bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Mandɛm, mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɛp be nkáp. Nsɛ́ptímʉɛ́t ntá yɛka ndu bɛkwak mǎmbak manɛ́m bo. Nkʉ̌ nyaka nɔ chi bɛbʉ́ kɛ?
Ɔ́bhɔ̌ŋ yɛ bɛkʉ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́ghàti wɔ. Bǒ bati anwi mányiɛ mgbá nɛ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bɔ́ kɛrɨŋɨ batɨ kpátɛ María abhe Mɔ́ywi. Ábhé nɔ́kɔ́, Josɛ́f arɛm bɛ nnyɛ́n mmɔ́ chi Yesu.
Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp atandat, Yesu afa arɔk Bɛ́tani. Bɛ́tani abhak ɛtɔk Lásárɔs anɛ Yesu akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Yɛ̌ chí nɛchǐ-nkɔk kɛ̌ mmɔ́ abhɛp wɔ, ɔ̌chyɛ yi ngá-nɛghay?
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mamiɛ́ arat, ndɔk Yerúsalɛm bɛghɔ Píta. Mbak nɛ yí ndu manywɔp nɛkú.
Nnáŋ nkʉ bɛtɨk, nsɔŋɔri mmʉɛt bɛyǎ mpok nkɛ kway bɛbhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́, nɛ nchɔ́kɔ́ nsay nkɛ kwáy bɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ manyiɛp mɛnyu nɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́kwáy mɛ, nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p ákɔ́k mɛ ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ndɛn bɛkuti mmʉɛt.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ bo Israɛl bábhó bɛ́chyɛ Yesu nɛnyok, bɛ yi akʉ mmu ataŋ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ngú mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m. Kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛ́ncha ntá mmu anɛ áti mɛ. Ɛ́rɨ nyaka bɛ́ bákɛ́ bhe yi wáwák.” 
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́rɛ́m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, mmu amɔt anɛ áchí ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ yi, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɛ́ndɨ ntá yɛ̌ agha anɛ ányíɛ ɛpǎ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhak ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt Kɛfɔ Mandɛm awu amfay!”
Mpok yɔ, bǒ abhɛn báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛbhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl babhak Yerúsalɛm. Báfú ndǔ bɛyǎ bɛtɔk.
Kɛ Acha aghati mɛ bɛ, ‘Fǎ Yerúsalɛm dɔ́k mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngátí wɔ. Dɔ́k mbɔnyunɛ nchí tó wɔ nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl.’”
Nɛ mmǔ anɛ ághɔ́ mɛ, ághɔ̌ mmu anɛ átó mɛ nkwɔ.
Mpok yɔ, Hɛ́rɔd abhak mmu anɛ ákɛ̀m atú Gálili. Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ̀,
arɛm ntá Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndak nɛ wɔ mǎnáŋ mántwɔ́, chɔŋ ngók nnyé ɛnɛ.” Achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mámfyɛ́ yi anywɔ́p amɛm áchá anɛ gɔ́bhanɔ, mámbahɛri nɔkɔ yi. Áchá wu chi anɛ Hɛ́rɔd áté nyaka.
Matá ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu ǎtwɔ̀, afú, arɔk atɛmɛri yi ɛnɛ́ María árɔ́bhɛ́ anywɔ́p.
Mpok sɛ́bhʉɛ́t nyaka bǒmpap Mandɛm, yi akʉ sɛ́mpɛtnsɛm ntá yi, bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛwú Mɔ́ywi. Ná nɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm ntá Mandɛm? Ɛchi mbɔ̌ŋ tɛtɛp ɛcha bɛ Mɔ́ywi apu nɔ́k bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ, tɛ̌ndu yi achi nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ ndu bǎchi bo Kristo, bǎchí yɛ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, nɛ chɔŋ mǎnyíɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ́chyɛ́ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham.
Ndu ákɔ̀ árɔ̀ŋ, aghɔ́ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti amɔt chɔkɔ amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́bɛtɨk ɛyi. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Lɛ́vi. Abhak mmɔ̌ Álfeɔs. Abhɨŋɨ yi, arɛm bɛ, “Twɔ́ bhák nkoŋo wa.” Lɛ́vi afaté, abho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Ɛ́re rɛm bɛ, “Sɔt ɛkáti sɨŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́ghɔ̀, ɔ́nto yɔ ntá bakwɔ́ bo Yesu tándrámɔt awu ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs, nɛ ɛtɔk Smína, nɛ ɛtɔk Pɛ́gamɔm, nɛ ɛtɔk Tiatíra, nɛ ɛtɔk Sádis, nɛ ɛtɔk Filadɛ́lfia, nɛ ɛtɔk Laodísia.”
“Puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɨ̀ŋɨ mɛ bɛ, ‘Acha, Acha’ kɛ̌ áchwè ndǔ Kɛfɔ̌ mfáy. Mǔnɛ ákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay áyaŋ kɛ áchwe arɛ.
Kɛ mbák chi Yesu, yi ǎrɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhi mbɔ nchiakap mpoknkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ yi apu gu wáwák.
Mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko basɨŋ ami, ná bǎkway mɛ́nóko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m?”
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ mbɨ ɛnɛn Ɛpǎ Brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔ́ŋ yis, nɔ chi nywɔp ɛnɛn bɛway mɔ́nkwɔmɛn ndu bɛkʉ nɛnyíɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, baghɔk Yesu bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌yaŋ sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́nkʉ nɛnyíɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ntá yɛ fá?”
Bághòk nyaka ghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ya bɛ, “Mmǔ nyaka áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, arɔbhɛ ghati chí bo bɛ mbák mmu ásɨ́kɨ́ntɨ nɛ Yesu Kristo, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi, ɛnɛ́ nkúbhɛ́ nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ nɛ Kristo kɛ yi ánù nyaka bɛ́chɔ́ŋti.”
Yɛ̌ndu bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí mbɔ mmu anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ, Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndu sɛ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ yi. Kɛ ndu sɛ́tòk bhe, chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m nɛ Kristo ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm.
Mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́náŋ sɛ́gháti bhe, mpɛt nchí ghati bhe bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághàti bhe mbok anɛ achí kɛkúrí nɛ anɛ sɛ́ghàti nyaka bhe, mǎnókó, ɛyak ɛmbak nɛ yi.
Nɨk ka mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ankʉ bǒ Judeya abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko yi bákɛ́ kʉ mɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛbʉ́bʉ. Nɨk ka mmʉɛt bɛ bǒ Mandɛm abhɛn Yerúsalɛm mánsɔ́t nɛkɛp ɛnɛ́n mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ ntá yap nɛ nɔ nɛ maŋák.
Bǒmpap báfù chi ɛkɛt mbɔ̌ŋ mmu.
Bɔ̌ma, bɔ́ŋ yɛ ka bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ bhe akap bɛghati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm, nɛ bǎkɛ́ káŋ bo bɛ bákɛ́ rɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
Kɛ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́jwí pɔɔt bɛ́twɔ́, chɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí mbɔk nɛ́nɛ mɛ́may.
Arɛ́, amfǎy ɛkotákátí, Yesu anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, foŋorí bhɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákʉ̀.” Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bágʉɛp ɛbháŋá ndu bɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛnyu bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kɔ́rɛ ndɛn Yesu.
Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ nyaka batap ɛnɔk mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo. Mbák chí be bho bǎpu bo Israɛl, bǎchi batábhɛ́nɔk chi ɛ̌ti bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo. Bǎkɛ́ yoŋ yɛ mmʉɛ́t. Cháy ká Mandɛm.
Banábas achí nyaka ɛrɨ́tí mmu anɛ asɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu sayri. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ yí tontó. Akwak bɛyǎ bo mánoko mbok Yesu, báchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bakoŋo bhi.
Tɛ̌ndu mǔnti bo Mandɛm chí mmu anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhi nta yi, bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́bhak nɛ yi, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́bhak mmǔ mpányu, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́bhak mmu ɛchókóntɨ, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́bhak nnyǔmɛ́m, abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛ́bhak mmu anɛ átɔ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ, abhɔŋ bɛ́bhak chí sayri nɛ bho. Abhɔŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ́bhak mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ngoŋó nkáp nɛ apú kʉ bapu ɛ̌ti nkáp.
Foŋorí bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ́, mbɔ ɛnyu sɛ́fòŋori yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ́ bhɛsɛ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ kɛ́ka sɛ́nchwe ndǔ nɛmɔ ɛnɛn nɛ́kʉ sɛ́nkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́.’”
ɛbhɛn yi áre tɔŋ bhɛsɛ, akʉ nkwɔ bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak nɛnkɛm nɛ nɛjwǐmɛm nɛnkɛm.
Nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchí ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ babhɔŋ bɛbhák mbɔ bǒ abhɛn bápú ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ maŋák áchí nɛ yí, ámbák mbɔ mmu anɛ maŋák ápú nɛ yí. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákù mɛnyɨŋ, ámbák mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ.
Asɔt yɛ nkɔ́bhɛ́mɛ́m, áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛchyɛ ntá yap. Básɔ́t. Ntɨ anyǔ anchyɛ ntɨ.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi? Bɛ́ Mandɛm apu chak ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀ kɛ? Wáwák!
Kɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ mmǔ-nɛ áfú. Mpok Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò átwɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu apú rɨŋɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi áfú.”
Píta apɛt ataŋa, kpát, ayɨkɨ bɛ, “Mandɛm arɨŋɨ, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɔ́nkwǎ wu.”
Ayámbɨ aghókó nyaka mmǔ amɔt nɛ amʉɛt mmu wu kɛ̌ manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ́ bho ankɛm fá amɨk áfú. Ápɛ́rɛ ghoko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnɛrɛ́kɛt, ayambɨ abhʉrɛ nɛbhʉɛ́t anɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt wu bábhàk nɛ mpok anɛ bɔ́ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak arɛ́.
Ɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n ndɛ́mɛ́, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm chí ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbha. Ɛtaya mmu átó mɛ kɛ ághátí mɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɛm.
Mbɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛchǎy mbɔnyunɛ ɔchí mmu mbeápak. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́pú ɛyɛ, ɔ̌sɔrɛsɔt. Nɛ ɔ̌ghɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ.’
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌rɛ̀m nɛ́, ɛ́chi tɛtɛp: Mbák mmu ámfyɛ̌ ntí bɛ́bhak mǔnti Nkwɔ Kristo, nɔ ǎyaŋ bɛkʉ ɛrítí bɛtɨk.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛrɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm ntínso kɛ áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn-nɛ sɛ́kʉ̀, sɛpú fɛrɛ amɔ́.
Básɔt Pɔ̌l barɔk Ariyopagɔs, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bǒbatí báchɛ̀m nɔkɔ nyaka, bárɛ́m ntá yi bɛ, “Sɛ́kɔŋ bɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ bɛkɔ ɛbhɛ́n ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Ansɛm mpok, nchɛ́bhɛ́mú wu agú, bɔángɛl Mandɛm basɔt yi barɔk amfay, bákʉ yi achɔkɔ kɛkwɔt nɛ Ábraham. Mǔnkáp agú nkwɔ, bábhɛ́mɛ yi.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbák mǎmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, kɛmakati bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, bǎkwáy bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nkʉ ɛnɔk fig ɛnɛ. Nɛ bǎkwáy bɛ́gháti yɛ̌ chí njiɛ nɛ bɛ ‘Fǎ fá kwɛ́n awu amɛm manyu,’ ɛ́mfakari ɛnyu yɔ.
Nɛ́nɛ, nchí fyɛ́ ɛbhé ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛbhay, nɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́fú chí ntá mbɔŋ Yesu Acha. Ngɔrɛ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́rɔ́ nnɛ́m ndǔ nɛbhay.
Nkʉ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ́, nɛ chɔŋ ndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ, bɛ bɔ mankɔŋ batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋ mɛ, nɛ bɛ mɛ́mbák amɛm batɨ ayap.”
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi nyaka mpok ɛyɔ, mmɔ̌ anɛ bábhé mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak ǎchyɛ̀ nyaka mmɔ́ anɛ bábhé ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ɛsɔŋɔri. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ́nɛ.
Nchí ghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔnyunɛ mpok yɔ, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎrɛ̀m bɛ́pú fu be antɨ. Ɛfóŋó mmu Mandɛm ɛtayɛka átò kɛ̌ ághàti bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm.
Mǔntí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu wu aka bɛ́ anáŋ agu. Páílet aghati yɛ Josɛ́f bɛ́ ǎkway bɛ́rɔŋ bɛfɛrɛ ɛrɛnɛ Yesu.
Kɛ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ́ nyɛ́sɛ́ mbwɔt ɛnɛn bápɨ́ aywi mmʉɛt anɛ nɔ nɛ́chak, nɛ́ngo, nɛmbɔŋ mbɔ ɛnyu yi átɨ́ bɛ́ ɛ́mbák. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mbwɔt ǎfu amik ambɔ́ŋ chí ayi ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt.
“Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha mbɔnyunɛ bǎsɔ̀t mpok bɛ́tyɛt nsɛm-ámok nɛ nsɛmɛ́ nchán, kɛ batɨ yɛka ájwí nɛ bɛpɔ̌ nkaysi ndǔ bǎsɔt mɛnyɨŋ bho nɛ bɛtaŋ, nɛ ndǔ bǎchi bo batɨ rakáraka.
Bǒbha, mpɛt nchí mbɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ánòŋsi, nɛ mpu rɔ bɛghok bɛbe kpátɛ mǎmbɔŋ ɛpɨŋɨ́ Kristo.
Mambe áre fú amfay ánkwɛnti nɔkɔ amɨk mbɔ kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk ɛkɛn kɛ́kwɛ̀nti amɨk mpok mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ áfòk nɛ ɛnɛm.
Kɛ wɔ Tímɔti, mmǔ Mandɛm, kɛ́fyɛ́ amɔ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ. Kʉ ntɨ ɛnɛ bɛ́ ɔ́mbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ búrɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ mbɔnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ. Bɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, kɔŋ bo, bɔ́ŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ, nɛ bák ndu kpák nɛ bo báchák.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛ́ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ batɨ ɛ́ngó ɛ́ndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chí ambɨ. Nɛ bɛ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mǎndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chí ambɨ, mǎndɨŋɨ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Nɛ mbák ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu anyɛ́rɛ́ wɔ́ bɛ ɔmpɔkɔ ntu ywi ɔndɔk nɛ yi nɛkɔ̌ ntay   nɛmɔt, dɔ́k nɛ yi nɛkɔ̌ batay apay.
Asɔt nnɨk aghoko ɛ́kpá, abho bɛ́bok bho nɛ yɔ, bɛ mámfú amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Akʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n, nɛ mpɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí arɛ́. Atakati bɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ ɛsiɛ́ bakáp bɛwupsi, nɛ atakati bakáp ayap.
Chɔŋ bo mankɛm abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛbhé Moses mánɛ́m yɛ̌ndu bátàŋ bhɔ kɛkoŋo bɛbhé Mandɛm. Nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm amkpɔ́t manyé bo mankɛm abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ mpok bárɨŋɨ bɛbhé Moses bɛkoŋo bɛbhé Moses.
Nchí ghati be tɛtɛp bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ amfʉɛ́t.
Arɔ bhɔ atɛ́n mmʉɛt ambɨ mandú. Akwɛn nɛ bɛsí amɨk, abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ, “Ɛtaya! Kʉ nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ámfʉɛ́t mɛ ansɛm ntí, mbák mbi achi bɛkʉ nɔ. Kɛ ɛ́kɛ́ bhák mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌yáŋ, ɛ́mbák chi mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́yàŋ.”
Kɛ nká ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔ́t bɛsí bhɛ kpoŋoroŋ. Nchí koŋo Mbi anɛ́ bo Israɛl bárɛ̀m bɛ abhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ndu nchí nɨkmʉɛt nchyɛ́ nɔkɔ kɛnókó ntá Mandɛm bachǐmbɨ abhɛsɛ. Nɛ nnókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɛbhé Moses bɛ́yàŋ sɛnkʉ nɛ yɛ̌ chí ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm basɨŋɨ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ.
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bachi nɛ yi bábhàbhɛri Yesu bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ mmɨk ányɨ́kɨ́sí, bághɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chák ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí. Bɛchay bɛ́kɛ́m bhɔ tontó. Bábhó bɛrɛm bɛ, “Achí mbʉ Mmɔ Mandɛm tɛtɛp!”
Mpok báchɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ, Yesu afaté, afɛrɛ ɛ́wɛt ɛyi amʉɛt, asɔt táwáy atɛ́m ɛbho.
“Nɛnɛ́ ká batú sayri mǎngok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí ghati bhe. Chɔŋ mánti Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, mámfyɛ yi amɔ bǒ mmɨk.”
Kristo akʉ nɔ́ bɛ ankway bɛkʉ nkwɔ Kristo mantwɔ ntá yi nɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ, kɛbhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ chi bo mánji bhɔ.
Nɛwú ɛnɛn yi agu, agú bɛchɔŋti bɛtaŋ nɛwú. Agú ndɔŋ amɔt ndak amay. Kɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛchi chi ndu bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ mmu amɔt kɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ kpóŋóróŋ ɛ̌ti yi, mbɔnyunɛ báchày nyaka bǒbati bhap.
Mfɔ wap chí ángɛl anɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ nɛpi ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Nnyɛ́n ɛni ndǔ ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl chí Abádɔn, nɛ ndǔ ɛyɔŋ Grik chi Apóliɔn, nɔ chi “Nchɔ́ŋtí mɛnyɨŋ.”
Nnɛ́m achi mǔnti ntá ngɔrɛ́ ywi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kristo achi mǔnti ntá bǒnkwɔ. Bǒnkwɔ chi mmʉɛt yi nɛ yímbɔŋ kɛ ápɛ̀mɛ bhɔ.
Bɔ̌bha, ntí anɛ mɛ́sɨ̀ŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chi bɛ mɛ́nkwák bhe bǎkɛ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ mbák mmu akʉ bɛbʉ́, sɛ́bhɔ̌ŋ mmu amɔt anɛ áté bɛsí Ɛtayɛsɛ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ nɛ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi amfoŋori bhɛsɛ. Mmǔ wu chi Yesu Kristo mmu achi chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mpǎy manywɔp, Mfɔ Agripa nɛ mɔ́mayi anɛ ngɔrɛ́ Bɛnis bárɔ́k Seséria ndu bɛ́káka Fɛstɔs.
Yesu abhɛ́p baghɔkɔ́ bhi mbák bájwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághátí bhɔ mɛnkɛm. Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ bajwimɛm. 
Yesu apɛt abho bɛ́gháti bho mɛnyɨŋ. Arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ, ǎbhɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bo mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ apú kɔ amɛm ɛjuri.”
Nkúbhɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bɛbhɛp yi ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛkʉ yi ánkwɛ́n anyu. Bǒnkwɔ Sádusi babhɨkɨ noko nyaka bɛ ɛwak ɛ́mɔt bawú bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Acha, agha ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛ́chay wɔ? Agha ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛchyɛ wɔ kɛnókó? Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí nyáŋá. Wɔ kɛ̌ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ bɛsí ɛbhɛ manchyɛ kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ mankɛm mánaŋ bághɔ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ́ mɛnkɛm bɛchi chak”.
Bǒnkwɔ abhɛn atú Masidónia nɛ abhɛn atú Akáiya bábhɔŋ maŋák bɛchyɛ mbɔk nkáp awap ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho ndǔ nkwɔ bo Mandɛm abhɛn Yerúsalɛm.
Mandɛm atɔ̌ŋ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ átó Njaŋa Mɔ́ywi fá amɨk bɛ sɛ́mfʉ́ɛ́t ntá yi sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́nɛ ndu bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re fakari, bɛ́ mɛ́náŋ mɛ́mfákárí, mǎnókó bɛ, ‘Nchí mmu nchí’ mpoknkɛm.”
“Mmɔ anɛ bábhé bɛ́ ámbák Mfɔ bo Israɛl achí fá? Sɛ́bhɛ̀p mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ nɛmbe ɛnɛ́n nɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti nɛbhe ɛni awu atú mmok áfù, nɛ sɛ́twɔ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó.”
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, mmu ɛbhaŋákwa amɔt arɔk akwɛ́n yi bɛkak abho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, mbák ɔkɔŋ, ɔ̌kway bɛkʉ mɛ ntáŋ.”
Yesu abhɛ́p yɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkpkɔkɔ́ brɛt afɔ mɛ́ní? Dɔ́k ká byo.” Bábyó nɔ́kɔ́, bárɛm bɛ, “Bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bɛ́tay nɛ nsi ɛ́pay.”
Abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmǔ anɛ bǒ nɛfí nkwɔ báchyɛ̀ kɛnókó. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, bákwày bɛ́chyɛ yi ntíánwɔ́p ankwɛ́n ndǔ ntá Satan.
Ɔ́kɛ́ ji nsénsí nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ. Chiɛ̌ yi chi maniɛ́ mbɔ bɛ achi chi ɛtayɛ. Sɔt babhakanɛm abhɛn bábhíkí ghaka ɛkaká nɛbhe ɛyɛ mbɔ bɔ̌máyɛ.
Mbák ndɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛm ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ́, nchí rɛm ngaka fá? Mpok apu bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti Gidiɔn, nɛ Bárak, nɛ Samsɨn, nɛ Jɛ́fta, nɛ Debhít, nɛ Samuɛl nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mankɛm bachak mankɛm nkwɔ.
Bárɛ́m bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak, mánso nɔkɔ yi nɛ nsɔk. 
Báre bhɛsɛ arɛ́ mámbɨŋɨ nɔkɔ njiɛ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ bɛ, “Kwɛ́n ká kuti bɛsɛ bɛ́ sɛ́kɛ ghɔ bɛsí mmu anɛ achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ bɛ ntɛmsi Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n akɛ́ bhak nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ afʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, bǎchi nyaka mbɔ bawú bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ bǎpú bhʉɛrɛ nyaka bɛbhé Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka.
Nɛka kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bo Israɛl bákɔ́ bápé manyu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Manyu Chu mpok ákɔ́rɛ́ mbɨŋ ɛpay, ɛ́rɔp mbɔ bɛ bákɔ̀ chi ndǔ mmɨk anɛ nnyɛ́n nɛ́pú fʉɛt arɛ. Kɛ mpok bo Íjip mámɔ́ bɛkʉ ɛnyumɔt, nnyɛ́n nɛ́gbókó nɛ́pɔ́kɔ bhɔ mankɛm.
Yi arɛm ntá Mandɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ ndɛm ɛ̌ti yɛ ntá bɔ̌maya mpok bǒbhɛ báchɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, nte bɛsí bhap nchyɛ́ wɔ bakak.”
Tɛ̌ndu bǒbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛkaysi ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti Mandɛm, Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ amɔ nɛ bhɔ. Arɔ́ bhɔ́ ndǔ bɛpɔ̌ nkaysi yap, nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɨkɨ kway bɛ bɔ mankʉ.
Bɔ̌bha, bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu ándwɔ́ bhe. Mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak achi chak mbɔ Yesu.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Chiɛ́ yɛ́ ka Mfɔ Rom yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛyi, mǎnchyɛ Mandɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛnɛ Mandɛm.” Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu arɛmɛ, bápɔ́p! 
Yɛ̌ndu ɛ́chí nɔ́, mbɔŋ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm. Nchí kɔ ɛchɔŋ nɛ mbúrɛ́ nɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn nɛjwi arat ńgaka arɛ́. Amɛm Yerúsalɛm kɛ báway nɔkɔ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.’
Yesu afate nɛ bakoŋo bhi bábho bɛrɔŋ nɛ mǔnti wu.
Pɔ̌l ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́rɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m, bɔ́ mankɛm bátɛp mánɛ́n amɨk, babho mɛnɨkmʉɛt.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɔ̀ŋ Yerúsalɛm, are te ndǔ bɛtɔk bɛgho nɛ bɔ̌bɛtɔk antɔŋ nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mǔnkwɔ Fárisi wu abhak maknkay bɛ́ghɔ bɛ Yesu abhɨkɨ so amɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛyap ɛ́tɔ́ŋ kɛ anyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́.
Nɛrɛm anɛ Píta árɛ́mɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ, nɛbháŋ nɛ́sɛp tɛ́mté, nɛbho bɛ́kúti bhɔ. Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú amɛm nɛbháŋ ɛ́ndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ yí tontó. Ghók ká yi!”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔ́bhɛ̀p mɛ ɛ̌ti ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ? Mmǔ amɔt aywǐntí kɛ árɨ́. Mbák ɔ̌yáŋ yi anchyɛ wɔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉ́rɛ́ bɛbhé Mandɛm.”
Kɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ ɛchi ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́twɔ̀ nyaka mɛ chi nɛ nɛwú kɛ? Wáwák! Bɛbʉ́ kɛ bɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ́ mɛ nɛ nɛwú. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, sɛ́ghɔ̀ yɛ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ bɛbʉ́ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bɛ́bhɛ́ ɛ́chá. Bɛ́fʉɛ̀t ndu ɛrɨ́tí ɛbhé Mandɛm, bɛbʉ́ bɛ́twɔ̀ bho nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bɛ́bhɛ́ bɛcha. 
Bɔ báchi mbɔ bɛtaŋtí mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn amɛm manyu ngo ɛnɛ́ ɛ́gbògho ɛ́mbay nɔkɔ gboo, gboo. Mɛnyɨŋ ntianywɔp ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀ bɛchi mbɔ ɛfɛn ɛnɛ́ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́gbogho ɛmbay nɔkɔ angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Báchí mbɔ mambě mfay anɛ ábóŋoboŋ. Mandɛm abhʉ́rɛ́ ɛbhak ntá yap, ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɛ́giri pyɔɔ. Arɛ́ kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak ngwɛnti ti.
Ndǔ manywɔp ayɔ, bǎbhɔŋ nyaka bɛyǎ maŋák. Yi ɛ́fákárí nɛ maŋák amɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka? Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ yɛ̌ ngati nyaka bhe chi bɛ mǎmpóŋórí amɨ́k ayɛka mǎnchyɛ mɛ bǎkʉ nɔ.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ɛtayi nɛ máyi nɛ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi nɛ mpok anɛ bábhé yi. Nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Achí nchiakap Mandɛm ngwɛnti ti mbɔ Mmɔ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ndu yi achí nyaka ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt mbɔ mbɔŋ Ɛta Mandɛm ndǔ babhi ankɛm, abhɨ́kɨ́ kɛ́m kɨ́kɨ́rɨ́k bɛ́ yi achi Mandɛm.
Báyát kɛpɛm ɛkɔ amɛm nɛyarɛ́ grep antí ɛtɔk. Manoŋ afú wu arɛ. Manoŋ mɔ ajwi amɨk mbɔ mɛta amɔt nɛ ɛbhɔk, nɛ aghoŋo kpát bɛsap ɛbhi bɛghaka mbɔ bɔkilomɛta bɛsa byo ().
Batísyɛ bhɔ batí árát chi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ manyiɛp, nɛ manoŋ, nɛ bárɛ̀m chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt.
Kɛ Mandɛm ánáŋ ánkʉ́ mpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, chɔŋ njambɨ atú Gálili, mǎntɛmɛri mɛ arɛ́.’”
Dɔ̌ ká bɛ́rwɔ́ mmʉɛt yɛka! Mbák yɛ mmǔ ywɛka akáysí bɛ́ achí ndɨŋɨndak bɛ́kóŋo nkaysi bǒ mmɨk, ɛ́rɨ́ yí ánjíbhírí ámbák mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá bǒ mmɨk. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak yí ambak ndɨŋɨndak, bɛ́kóŋo nkaysi Mandɛm.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bápɛt bábhɛ́p nnɛ́mámɨk anɛ Yesu ákʉ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ bɛ, “Wɔ bɛ́ mmu wu kɛ ákʉ́ ɔ́ghɔ̀ mbaŋ, ɔkáysí bɛ yi achi agha?” Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi wɨkɨrɨk bɛrɛm ntá mbɛ́ntí-nɛ chí ɛnɛ́? Bɛrɛm bɛ ‘Mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhɛ’, kɛ chi, ‘Faté pɔkɔ́ bɛkpaka ɛbhɛ kɔ?’
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ bǎfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhi, mɛ nkwɔ nchí foŋori yi. Nɛ mɛ̌foŋori mbák ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi mbɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yàŋ bɛ mámfoŋori yi. Nchí foŋori yi ɛ̌ti yɛka ndu nnyɛ́n Kristo mmu átó mɛ.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ nnáŋ ntóŋtí bɛ́twɔ bɛghɔ bhe ndu ndɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́jwí ɛ́rát. Mpú bhak chɔŋ ntu ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ be kɛ mɛ̌yaŋ, puyɛ̌ bakap ayɛka. Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ puyɛ̌ mǎmbɔ kɛ babhɔŋɔ bɛbhʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ntá bachi nɛ manɔ bhap, chi bachi nɛ manɔ kɛ bábhɔŋɔ bɛbhʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ntá bɔ̌bhap.
Bo abhɛ́nɛ́fú báchí mbɔ mmɨk anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ tákɔ nsěnse. Bághòk nkwɔ́ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm,
Puyɛ̌ chi bɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́té mɛ ntísiɛ, nchí ghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti ya bɛ Mandɛm ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhe.
yí bɛ́ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndak nɛ yi mántwɔ́ ntá yɛ.] Mbák wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́ndɛ́m kɛpɨ nɛ yi, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ yi ákʉ́ ɛchí tɛtɛp.”
Ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay, abhak nɛ bhɔ́ amɛm baso, abhɔ́ŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛ́rɨ yɛ bɛ sɛ́mfyɛ́ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́mbák kpák nɛ batɨ, nɛ bɛ sɛ́mfyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwàk batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ mango ndu nɛka ɛnɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Mandɛm.
Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́, bǒ mankɛm báchɔ́kɔ amɨk.
kɛ abʉɛ́ ɛbhówɔ, ndɛn ayi arɔp bɔ́ amɔ. 
Mbok Mandɛm áchí mbɔ ɛpɔ̌ndak ntá bo Israɛl ndǔ báyàŋ bɛ́ghɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fù amfay kɛ mánoko bɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achí tɛtɛp. Bǒ Grik mánoko chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔ́ŋ ámɔ́t nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnap.
Mmu achák ǎkwáy bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Mandɛm aghókó nɛnyíɛ́ chí bɛ́ mányíɛ́ mámfyɛ́ mɛniɛ, aghoko mɛniɛ bɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛmfʉɛt arɛ kɛ nɛ́nchwe mmu amʉɛt.” Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp, kɛ ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Mandɛm ǎkʉ bɛ mɛniɛ bɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ bhak, nɛnyíɛ́ nkwɔ kɛpɛrɛ bhák. Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ ghoko mmʉɛt nkwǎ chí ndǔ barak ɛpúsí. Aghókó mmʉɛt yɛsɛ́ chí bɛ́ sɛ́nkóŋó Yesu Acha nɛ yɔ́. Nɛ yí Yesu Acha kɛ̌ áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwàk mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛmbak sayri.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́fyɛ́ yɛ́ bɔ́ ntɨ, básɔ́t nɛnyíɛ́ mányíɛ́.
Akʉ nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ arɛm nyaka nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, “Mbák ntɔk yɛ̌ chi nkokoŋ ndɛn Yesu, chɔŋ ntaŋ.”
Ŋɛmɛ́ ká mǎmfyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ mandu bɛtaŋ anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ ákɛ́ kpɨkɨ ɛ́may mǎngú. Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ngɔ́ bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ jwi pɔɔt bɛsí Mandɛm mmu mɛ́tòk.
Mpok yí áyámbɨ átwɔ́, are nyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Kɛ bo abhɛn Jems átó bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, abho bɛya mmʉɛt ansɛm, akɛpɛrɛ nyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bo abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl, ndu áchay nkwɔ́ bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ babhɔŋ bɛsyɛp yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkoŋo Yesu anɛ apu mmu Israɛl.
Chɔŋ ɛ́ndɨ ntá mmɔ̌bɛtok wu ɛncha mpok chi-bɛtɨk ywi afu nɛkɔ, apɛtnsɛm, aghɔ́ bɛ́ yi ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi sayri.
Kɛ́ bhɛ́p yɛ mmʉɛt bɛ, “Chɔŋ agha ansɛp amɨk ndu ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú?” [Nɔ chi bɛ, “Mmu abhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛsɛp andɔk amɨk ndǔ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú bɛkʉ Kristo ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”]
Babhɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛnti nkwɔ bárɔ́k bɛ yi anjwiti bhɔ. Bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, yi sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ?”
Nɛ bákʉ̀ barak ɛ́pusi nɛ amɨk, nɛ ɛkwak bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ ɛpu may bɔ antɨ. Bárwɔ̀ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Yesu. Batɨ yap achi chi batɨ bǒ ngwáy. Ntɛ́msí Mandɛm anáŋ achi nɛ bhɔ.
Ndǔ mpok yɔ, Yesu ánɨkmʉɛt bɛ, “Ɛta, wɔ mmu ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mfay nɛ mmɨk! Nchí chyɛ wɔ bakak ndǔ ɔ́rɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́mbák bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ntá barɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ ntá bo abhɛn bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Ɔnɛ́nɛ́ bhɔ ɔtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mbɔ mǎmbɔ.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas báfú yɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bárɔk ɛkɛt Lídia. Bátɛ́mɛri bǒnkwɔ Yesu arɛ báchíɛ bhɔ maníɛ́ nɛ báfyɛ́ bɔ́ ntɨ. Báfá yɛ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ.
Bě nkwɔ́ bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhak maŋák. Ŋák ká nɛ mɛ. 
Kɛ nɛ́ chi nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay, bɛ́ mmǔ anɛ ányíɛ́ nɔ́ ákɛ́ gu.
Bǎkɛ́ cháy bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ be ambɨ. Ghok ka, mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ǎkʉ chɔŋ mámfyɛ mbɔk ayɛka ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ndu mɛmɔ bhe. Nɛ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ manywɔp byó. Kɛ bɔ́ŋ ka nɛka tɛ ndǔ nɛwú. Nɛ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti mbɔ nta kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ mǎnu bǎsɔt awɔ́nɛm.
