“Mɛ̌ghàti yɛ be bɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ áfɔ́k anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndǔ yí áchí nɛ bhe mbɔ Mfɔ ywɛka, anchyɛ ntá bo báchák abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ bɔ mankʉ.” [Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ akwɛnɛ ndǔ ntay ɛnɛn, ǎsìɛpti ndǔ mbɨŋ, nɛ mmu anɛ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ yi amʉɛt, nɛ́chɔ̀kɔti yi.]
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Mandɛm akɔŋ be nɛ ayap be
Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ka bɛtɨk nɛ maŋák mbɔ bɛ bǎtòk chi Acha, puyɛ̌ nkwǎ.
Ɛ́fákári ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ndu bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ nɛwú yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gu ɛmfu tɛtɛp.
Yɛ̌ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛrɛm chi bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk mɛnkɛm nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́ bɔángɛl nkwɔ, mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ bo, nɔ́ nchí chí mbɔ akánkáŋ nɛ njánɛ́ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yɔ̀ŋ.
Bú ká bǒmame, ŋɛmɛ́ ká bawú, mǎmbu bǒ ɛbhaŋákwa nkwɔ. Bók ká bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ mɛ́ndɔ́ bho. Nchyɛ́ bhe bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nkɛ sɔt nkáp. Dɔ́k yɛ́ ka kʉ bhɔ ntá bho kɛbhɛ́p bhɔ nkáp.
Yí mámfyɛ́ nkwɔbhánya kɛ bákɛ́ pɔkɔ ndɛn ɛ́chák.
Bǎrɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti Yesu mmu Násárɛt, nɛ ɛnyu Mandɛm achyɛ́ nyaka yi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ bɛtaŋ. Akɔ mbǎnkɛm ankʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɨ nɛ ambu nɔkɔ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn Satan áchyɛ̀ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achi nɛ yí.
Mmu anɛ apu nu nɛ bhɛsɛ, achí nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎrɨŋɨ ɛbhe. Bǎrɨŋɨ yɛ bɛ ɛbhé ɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mmu chi ndiɛrɛ mpok yi achi nɛpɛ́m?
Ɛkʉ mbɔk bo abhɛn bachi arɛ chɔkɔ bábéntɨ tontó, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ nɛ ǎchɔ̀ŋti bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn ndaká yí?
Bágwɔ́t nɔ́kɔ́ yí ndu bɛdɛn, Pɔ̌l abhɛ́p mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt anɛ achi arɛ tee bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛ́chyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ ɔ́ndɛ́m mándɛ́n mmu Rom ɛnɛ bábhɨkɨ re yɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ manyé ayi mángɔ́ bɛ́ akʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́?”
Nchí sɨŋ bɛkʉ ɔndɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ ayɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bághátí wɔ. 
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bakay yɔ nɔ́ Yesu átɛ́mɛ́, bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛ ǎrɛ̀m nɔ chí ɛ̌ti yap.
Kaká ká batɨ nɛ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm.
Achí mmu tɛtɛp nɛ áchyɛ̀ ntɛ́msí ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi sayri nɛ chak. Anáŋá achyɛ ntɛmsi ntá nnɛ́m ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ anɛ áchɔ̀ŋti mmɨk nkɛm nɛ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ yi. Akɛ́mɛ́ kɛ́mbé bǒ bɛtok abhi abhɛn ngɔrɛ́ wu ákʉ́ baway.”
Acha aghati mǔnkwɔ Fárisi wu bɛ, “Bě bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǎsɔ̀t mpok bɛ́tyɛ́t nsɛmɛ́ nchán kɛ mɛŋɛ́mɛ́ nɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛjwi be antɨ.
Ghok ka nɛkay nɛ́chák, “Mmǔfú abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkɨ. Apɨ mɛnɔk vain arɛ. Atɛp ɛbhá ɛnɛ ɛghabhɛri nkɨ ankɛm. Atɛ́m mbok aghoko nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báyàt kɛpɛm váin, bɛ nnok ywi amfu, mánsɔt, máná mmɛ́m. Ate mɔ́kɛrɛ́mfay amɛm nkɨ wu, bɛ́ ámbák nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mmu áchɔ̀kɔ ndu bɛ́bhábhɛ́ri nkɨ. Afyɛ́ yɛ bo arɛ́ bɛ mánkʉ bɛtɨk mánkɔrɛ nsáy nɛ yi. Arɔ, arɔk nɛkɔ ɛtɔk ɛchak.
Ndǔ bɛ́tɛm ɛbhɛn sɛchi arɛ́ nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ sɛ́chí ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tɔ́ŋ bɛ sɛ́yàŋ Mandɛm ámfɛ́rɛ́ mmʉɛt anɛ ágù. Sɛ́yàŋ chi bɛ yi anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt nkɔ, bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpu gu ɛ́mɛn ɛnɛ ɛ́gù.
Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ bɛ, “Nchí fá amɛm acha manyé Mfɔ Rom, nɛ fá kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́táŋ nyé ɛnɛn. Wɔmbɔŋ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bo Israɛl bɛbʉ́.
Kaká ká Filólogɔs nɛ Júlia nɛ Nériɔs nɛ mɔmáyi anɛ ngɔrɛ́, nɛ Olímpas nɛ bo Mandɛm abhɛn bachi nɛ bhɔ.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fákárí nyaka ntá bo Israɛl, bɛ́chí chí bɛrɨŋ ntá bo báchák. Kɛ ntá yɛsɛ, básɨŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ mɛ́nsɛ́mtí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ánsɔ́t mpok nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ ngwɛnti mmɨk arɔbhɛ kɛkwɔt.
Mbák bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, chɔŋ nnɨk Ɛtaya mmʉɛt, nɛ yi anchyɛ bhe Nkwak achak, yi ambák nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm.
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛn bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ bɛ́bhó mɛnɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ, “Mbák ɔ̌bòk bhɛsɛ, tó bhɛsɛ chi ndǔ nkwɔ bakók wu.”
Nɛ mpok anɛ bághɔ́ mɔ́ngo anɛ áfù ndǔ ngó anɛ ásɔ̀ŋ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn chɔŋ mánde rɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, ‘Tɛ̌ mmɨk abhó, yɛ̌ ɛtɔk ɛbhɨ́kɨ́re ghaka mbɔ nnɛ́m ɛtɔk ɛnɛ.’
Bǒ mmɨk mankɛm báchí mbɔ mmu anɛ Mandɛm ághókó nɛ ntɔp, nɛ bǒ mfay mankɛm báchi mbɔ mmu anɛ áfú amfay.
Dɔ̌ ká mbɛp be ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́mɔt. Mandɛm achyɛ bhe Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ chi ɛ̌ti bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé kɛ chi ndu bǎghókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo nɛ mǎnókó?
Mmyamyaŋ are fú ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Nɛbu nkwɔ́ nɛ́re rɛmti, nɛfaŋ ansay nɔkɔ. Bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ tándrámɔt bɛbhak ambɨ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ mɛ́ndu nɔkɔ mbɔ *sɛsay. Bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɔ chí bɛfóŋó Mandɛm tándrámɔt.
Bɔ Píta bátɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bachwi yap angɔkɔnyɛ́n, bárɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bakoŋo Yesu. 
Mmu wap amɔt áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Ágábɔs. Ndu bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ afate arɛm bɛ chɔŋ ɛrɛmɛ nsay ɛ́nkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí antɛn Mfɔ Rom. [Nsay yɔ akwɛ́n mpok Klaodiɔs áchí Mfɔ Rom].
Bakoŋo Yesu bághɔ́kɔntɨk bɛ́pɔ́kɔ brɛt. Babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka chí mɔ́kpɔkɔ́ brɛt amɔt amɛm áchwí.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu apé, arɔk ɛbhě Manyu Gálili. Nkúbhɛ́ Manyu wu kɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Manyu Tibérias.
Bɔ̌ma, puyɛ̌ be mankɛm kɛ̌ babhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak batɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bo, manyé ásɔ̀ŋ bɛsɛ́ bhó sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amʉɛt ɛ́ncha bo báchák.
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ nkáp anɛ bǎchwɔ̀p ndu bɛkwak bo Mandɛm, bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyu ngátí bǒnkwɔ abhɛn atú Galéshia mánkʉ.
Máyɛsɛ, nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ sɛ́nkɔŋ batɨ. Ɛnɛ ɛ́pú ɛbhé ɛkɔ. Mɛ́chyɛ̀ wɔ chi nkúbhɛ́ ɛbhé ɛnɛ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ tɛ mpok sɛbho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Nɛ akap anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bho ndɛ́ndɛm achi kɛkúrí tontó nɛ akap anɛ bɛbʉ́ mmu wu amɔt bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ wu. Bɛkoŋo bɛbʉ́ bhɔ mɛmɔt Mandɛm atǎŋ bo mankɛm nɛ bákwɛn manyé. Kɛ akap anɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ ndɛ́ndɛm bɛkoŋo bɛbʉ́ bɛyǎ bho ákʉ̀ bo mámbák chak bɛsí bhi.
Bɛyǎ bo básɔ̀t Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ bághàti bho mbɔ mbi bɛyaŋ nkáp. Bɛsɛ́ sɛ́pú nɔ, sɛ́ghàti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ chí nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt, ndǔ bɛtaŋ Kristo, nɛ sɛrɨŋɨ bɛ amík Mandɛm achi bhɛsɛ amʉɛt.
arɛm bɛ, “Ndǔ ɛpa, báyambɨ mantwɔ chi nɛ ɛrɨ́tí mmɛ́m. Nɛ bo mǎnáŋ mányú ánchwé bhɔ amʉɛt, kɛ mántwɔ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmɛ́m báchák. Kɛ ɔrɔ́ ɛrɨ́tí mmɛ́m ansɛm, nɛ nɛ́nɛ kɛ ɔ́twɔ̀ nɛ mɔ́.”
Nkoŋo ywi amɔt anɛ achí manɔ Símun Píta anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Andru arɛm ntá yi bɛ,
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɨ́ bɛsí Mandɛm chí bɛ́ yí ánkwák bɔ̌bɛrǎ nɛ mánkwɛ́sɛ́, nɛ ankɛ́m mmʉɛt bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk bɛ́kɛ́ chɔŋti yi mɛ́nkʉ́ yi ánjíbhírí ámbák mmǔ bɛbʉ́. Mmǔ Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ kɛ ábhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ndǔ nku nsɨ́, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nchiakap ǎte nyaka ndǔ bɛtɨk, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báchyɛ akap arɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp, ndu bɛ́chyɛ nkúbhɛ́ akap anɛ apu kway bɛpɔkɔ bɛbʉ́ bho wáwák.
Mpok anɛ sɛ́chí nyaka kɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkwak mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ, Kristo agǔ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm ayabhɛ, bɛ ánkwak bhɛsɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́.
Nu bɛ́ Mandɛm anjɨŋɨ wɔ ambɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ wɔ bɛ́ ɔchí nkʉbɛtɨk anɛ apú kway bɛbhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p, nɛ bɛ́ ɔ̌tɔŋ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ sayri.
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɨ bɛcháy. Ǎchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ chi nɛtaŋántɨ, nɛ ɛkɔŋ, nɛ nɛkɛ́mɛ́mʉɛt.
Nɛ mbák sɛ́ndɛ́m bɛ, ‘Bɛ́fǔ nyaka ntá nkwǎ’, nɔ́ sɛ́yàŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bǒ bhɛsɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ mankɛm mánoko sayri bɛ Jɔ̌n achi nyaka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.”
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhɔŋ bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkáp byó. Mbák ɛbhɔk ɛ́mɔt ɛ́nɛm, ǎkʉ yi? Pú ǎdurɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́, ansɔt kɛtɨ́ŋɨ́ anyɔ ɛkɛt ɛnkɛm, ambyo sayri mbǎnkɛm kpatɛ angɔ́ yɔ́?
Bɔ̌bha, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bǎrɔp chi bo abhɛn bárɨŋɨ Ɛta. Bɔtá, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bǎrɨŋɨ mmu anɛ ánáŋ achi nyaka tɛ mpok mmɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́re bho. Bɛsak, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ nɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛchi amɛm batɨ ayɛka, nɛ mǎnʉ́ nɛ mbʉ́mbʉ bǎsɔt awɔ́nɛm
Kɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ nɛchí kɛkúrí. Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ chi bɛ nɛ́pú fyɛ mmu bakwap antɨ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kòŋo chí bɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n Mandɛm áchyɛ nɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ámbák sayri nɛ batɨ, nɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ bhɔŋ ntɨ gum gum, nɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ámbɔ́ŋ ɛpɨŋ bɛghɔ bho ntínso, nɛ ɛpɨŋ bɛkʉ bɛrɨ mpoknkɛm. Mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fù ntá Mandɛm, ǎbhák mmu tɛtɛp, ápú kʉ bɛtábhá.
Bǒ abhɛn yi átó, bárɔ́k, bághɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi aghati bhɔ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ́ntɨ́bhɛti, mmǔ amɔt abho bɛbɨk andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Ghók ká, mbǎyngɔrɛ́ wu atɛwú átwɔ̀! Twɔ́ ká sɛnsyɛpti yi!’
Ɛchi yɛ chi mbɔ ɛbhé ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna bɛ mpok mɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ, ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ kɛ nchí kʉ.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bákɛ́m bɛyǎ ɛpʉ́ítí kpát akɔrɛ akwɛn nɛntɨ nap. Banábas asɔt Jɔ̌n Mák báchwe achwǐnyɛ́n, bárɔk Sáyprɔs.
Ndǔ sɛ́kɔ̀ ndu nkwɔ, ɛyɔ ɛpu chyɛ mbi bɛ mmu ánkáysí bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ batɨ apay. Sɛ́sɔ̀t mpok bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ ji bhɛsɛ bɛyɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ sɛ́kʉ̀ nɛ bɛyǎ akabhɛ́ nkáp anɛ.
Mbák mǎnkʉ́ brɛt, mǎnchyɛ́ anɛ bǎyámbɨ bǎkʉ́ ntá Mandɛm, nɔ brɛt achak nkɛm achi brɛt Mandɛm nkwɔ. Nɛ mbák bakaŋánɔk achi ntá Mandɛm, nɔ batábhɛ́nɔk ɛyɔ nkwɔ achi chi ayi.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, tá ká batú mǎngók. Mandɛm ayap bo abhɛn báchí bachɛ́bhɛ́bho bɛsí bǒ mmɨk bɛ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, mámbɔŋ kɛfɔ bɛsí Mandɛm. Akʉ nkwɔ́ bɛ́ bɔ́ mámbák bo abhɛn yí ábhàk nɛ bhɔ́ mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ yí afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛkʉ nɛ bo abhɛn bákɔ́ŋ yi.
Kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ Yesu kɛrɛm. Páílet abhak maknkay tontó. 
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mbɔk ɛyɛka bǎpànyu mbɔnyunɛ bǎkaysi bɛ mpú pɛrɛ kway bɛ́twɔ bɛghɔ bhe.
Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ́ nkaysi basɨŋ mankɛm amɛn áchí amɛm Ɛkáti yi. Basɨ̌ŋ ǎkwak ndu bɛtɔŋ bhɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp nɛ ǎji bhɛsɛ ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛpu sayri ndǔ bapɛm ayɛsɛ. Basɨ̌ŋ ǎkwak mɛnyurɛ bhɛse ndǔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɛsɛ nɛ ndu bɛtɔŋ bhɛsɛ ɛnyu bɛbhak chak ndǔ bapɛm yɛsɛ.
Atɔk yi nɛ amɔ. Tɛ́mte wu, anyabhɛ mmʉɛt téé, abho bɛbɨti Mandɛm.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Moses ásɔ́rɛ́ nyaka nnyɔ́-sɛnɔŋ abhat ndǔ ɛnɔk, ayoŋ amfay, amɛm baso, ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyoŋ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm nkwɔ amfay.
Bǎkɛ́ bhak mbɔ bafɔ amfáy bo abhɛn báfyɛ́ amɔ́ yɛka. Bák ká chɨ́ bɛrɨ́tɨ́ bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́ŋɔ́kɔ.
María wu, kɛ áwáti nyaka bɛkak Yesu Acha nɛ bawɛrɛ́riɛp, are tɛsɛ nɛ ɛmɛnɛ́ntí yi. Yi kɛ mɔ́mayi Lásárɔs akwɛnɛ nyaka nɛme.
Yesu arɔk yɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Gɛtsɛ́mani nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Arɛ́, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Chɔkɔ́ ká fá, mɛ̌tɛn mmʉɛt ambɨ ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt.”
Ǎkway bɛ́chɔ́ŋti yɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ́ ɛbhɛn mbák sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt mpok. Ǎkway bɛkʉ nkwɔ́ bɛ́ bo bákɛ́pɛrɛ sɔt ɛkɛrákap mandɛm ngɔrɛ́ Atɛ́mis, mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ. Mbák ɛ́mfákárí nɔ, Atɛ́mis mmu áchí mandɛm ngo ywɛsɛ apú pɛrɛ bhak yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Nɛ yí kɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu atú Esia nɛ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm báchyɛ̀ kɛnókó!”
Bě nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛsɔt mmʉɛt ɛyɛka mbɔ bɛ bǎgu, nɛ bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛ bǎchi nɛpɛ́m ndu bɛ́tok Mandɛm ndu yi áchɛ́mɛ́ bhe nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛjwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́. Mandɛm abhɛsɛ ntí bɛyɔŋ bhɔ ntá yap bɛ bákɛ́ rɨŋɨ ndak anɛ áchí amɛm. Nɛ báre cháy bɛbhɛp Yesu mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́. 
Yí ǎghati bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi aghɔ nɛ amɨ́k, aghók nɛ batú. Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ mmu apú noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ.
Yɛ̌ndu mpú awu, ntɨ ɛna nɛchi nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm. Nkɔŋ bɛghok bɛ bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́yàŋ nɛ bɛ bǎte kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Kristo. 
Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú amfay, ɛnɛ́ nnáŋ ngɔ́kɔ́ ɛpɛt ɛghati yɛ mɛ bɛ, “Dɔ́k sɔt mɔ́kati nɛ́nɛ́p anɛ achi fuu awɔ ángɛl anɛ achi téé nɛ ɛkak ɛ́mɔt ndǔ manyu, ɛkak ɛchak ɛbhɨ.”
Bɔ mankɛm babhak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt. Báchyɛ́ mmʉɛt ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛbhʉɛt amɔt chɛchɛm nɛ mbɔk bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn baghɔrɛ́, nɛ María nnɔ Yesu, nɛ bɔ̌máyi abhɛn babhakanɛm.
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛmɛ be bɛ bǎkʉ nyaka bɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk. Yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ pá yɛ nnyu.
Nɛ mbák Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́gháti bhe ɛ̌ti yi bɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm nɛ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ yi nɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Báfyɛ́ nyaka yi bɛko bɛkak nɛ ngɛm amɔ́. Kɛ ngɛm ɛyɔ ɛ́ré kɨti kɨ́ti nɛ bɛko mɛ́ndakati nɔkɔ. Yɛ̌ mmu kɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn ákway bɛkɛm yi.
Kɛ mpǎy mɛnyɨŋ bɛchi nɛ bhe ɛbhɛ́n mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ. Mbɔk yɛka bákòŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Bálam átɔ́ŋɔ́. Bálam ǎtɔ̀ŋ nyaka Bálak ɛnyǔ yí akway bɛkʉ bo Israɛl mánkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛ mányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn bayɛrɛ bachyɛ mbɔ akap ntá bɔmandɛm nsé, nɛ mánkʉ nɔkɔ barak ɛ́pusi.
Ndiɛrɛ ɛfóŋó mmu kɛ ɛ́kwày bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ nkaysi anɛ áchí yí antɨ, mmu achák apú kwáy bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ yɔ́. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ ɛ́chí nɛ Mandɛm, ndiɛrɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ̌ árɨ́ŋɨ́ nkaysi anɛ áchí Mandɛm antɨ.
Kɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mmɨk nkɛm achi antɛnɛ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́. Ɛchi yɛ bɛ, ndiɛrɛ bo abhɛn babhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo kɛ bákway bɛbhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ ntá bo abhɛn mánókó Yesu Kristo.
Ɔ́kɛ́ bhák maknkay ndu ngátí wɔ bɛ, ‘Bábhɔŋ bɛbhe wɔ ndɔŋ achak.’
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Tiódas árɛ̀m nyaka bɛ yi achi nnɛ́m mmu. Bǒ mbɔ batí bɛsǎ ɛsa () babhak bákoŋo bhi. Báwáy nɔ́kɔ́ yi, bakoŋo bhi bhɔ bátáka, nsóŋó ɛyi amay.
Ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt, ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm ághòko mmɨk, arɛm bɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ mɛ́ngɔ́ɔ́ ndǔ ɛjuri, nɛ ɛbhak nɔ. Nkúbhɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhi bɛ́ghɔ̀ amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ. Nɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm ndǔ bɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛsí Kristo nɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ nɛ́nɛ ɛnyǔ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm bɛchi.
Ɛ́fákari bɛ ntɔŋ ɛbhé Moses arɔk mɛmɔ Yesu. Abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, chɔŋ nkʉ yi kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?”
Báfyɛ mɛ ntɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu báfyɛ́ bhe ntɨ. Chíɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ kɛnókó.
Puyɛ̌ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe kɛ afyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ mǎnkʉ nɔ.
Ntɨ nɛ́bé Yesu tontó. Abhaŋari ayɨŋɨ bhɔ́ mankɛm nɛ bɛběntɨ bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ bátàŋ batí. Yɛ̌ nɔ, abhɔ́ŋ ntínso nɛ mmu anɛ awɔ́ ágú nɔ́ yi aghati yi bɛ, “Nyabhɛ́ awɔ́ ywɛ.” Anyabhɛ awɔ wu, apɛt ataŋ abhak mbɔ áchák.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, abhak chɔ́kɔ́ anta nɔkɔ batú ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m. Pɔ̌l ayɨŋɨ yi dǐǐ, ághɔ́ bɛ́ yí wu anókó bɛ́ Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛ́bú yi.
Yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ chyɛ yɛ ɛpókómʉɛt ɛyi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɔt bɛkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ nɛ yɔ. Kɛ chyɛ̌ ka mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mbɔ bo abhɛn mánáŋ bágú kɛ yi ákʉ́ bǎpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Nɛ chyɛ ká bɛpókómʉɛt ɛbhɛka ntá Mandɛm mbɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bǎsɔt bɛkʉ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ghatí ká mɛ, “Agha áchyɛ́ nyaka Jɔ̌n Njwiti bɛtaŋ bɛjwiti bho? Mandɛm kɛ chí bǒ mmɨk?”
mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt abhɨkɨ rɛm nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfu ndu nkaysi nkwǎŋwaŋ. Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ áchwé nyaka bho antɨ, akʉ bɔ́ mándɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfu ntá Mandɛm.
Ɛ̌ti bɔángɛl, yi ǎrɛ̀m bɛ́ ákʉ̀ bɔ mambak mbɔ mbʉ́ɛ́p, ákʉ̀ bǒ bɛtok abhi mámbák mbɔ bárɨ́-ngo.
Nɔ kɛ Mandɛm Acha mmu akʉ bo mándɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn arɛmɛ tɛsáy.’”
Bǒ bhɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nkwɔ bɛ mǎnòŋ Mmɔ Mandɛm ámfú amfay antwɔ. Nɔ chi, Yesu mmu Mandɛm ákʉ́ nyaka áfú ndǔ nɛwú apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Yí wu kɛ ápɛ̀mɛ bhɛsɛ mpok Mandɛm átàŋ bo ndu ábè ntɨ nɛ bhɔ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Mpok anɛ barak ayɔ áfákárí, baghɔk Yesu kɛjwimɛm bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti yi kɛ bɛ́fù nɔ́ tɛtɛp. Kɛ mpok Yesu apɛrɛnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ Mandɛm asɔt yi amfay achyɛ yi kɛnókó, bátɨk yɛ bɛ básɨŋ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ɛ̌ti yi. Bátɨk nkwɔ́ ɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́fákári ntá yi.
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ kɛm nyaka Mɔ́ywi bɛ akɛ bhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri. Arɔ yi bɛ ankwak bhɛsɛ mankɛm. Tɛ̌ndu yi áchyɛ́ nyaka yi ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ bɛ chɔŋ anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ?
Bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák, bábhó bɛ́chyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Nɛ abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ ngwɛnti, mánoko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari, kpátɛ mpok ɛ́ghorǐ manyiɛp ɛ́twɔ. Nɛ mpok ɛ́twɔ ɛ́pɔ́kɔ bɔ mankɛm. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ nɛtwɔ wa, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ábhák chɔŋ.
Ɛfóŋó Kristo ákʉ̀ nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mángátí bho be Kristo abhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, nɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, ambɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ kɛnókó. Bɔ́ mánù nyaka bɛrɨŋɨ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákári, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ mmu anɛ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfakari nɛ yi.
Kɛ mbɔk yap báré rɛm chi bɛ, “Bɛlsɛbul mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ kɛ áchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ bɛbok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.”
Báchyɛ yɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ɛ́wɛt ɛnɛ pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ bágháti bɔ bɛ mandɔk ambɨ bɛywemʉɛt mandú kpatɛ mpǎy batɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk nɛ batɨ̌ bǒ nkwɔ́ abhɛn bǒ mmɨk babhɔŋɔ bɛway mbɔ bhɔ ankwáy.
Nku nsɨ́ ǎtwɔ̀ nyaka nɛ ntɛ́msi. Yɛ̌ nɔ, abhak chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. Nɛ́nɛ, Nku Nkɔ, yɔ́ anɛ ákʉ̀ sɛ́mbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛ́tɔŋ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm ancha Nku Nsɨ́.
Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bo mankɛm abhɛn báchí arɛ́. Bábhó bɛbɨti Mandɛm mándɛmɛ́ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛtaŋtí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm afú fá ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛsɛ! Mandɛm atwɔ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bǒbhi!”
Mpok ɛyɔ, ngɔ́ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n téé nɛntɨ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m. Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n abhak ndǔ nkwɔ bǒbati. Ɛbhak mbɔ bɛ mánaŋ baway nyaka yi. Abhɔ́ŋ babhaŋ tándrámɔt nɛ amɨ́k tándrámɔt. Amɨ́k ayi tándrámɔt chí bɛfóŋó Mandɛm tándrámɔt ɛbhɛ́n bátó mbankɛm amɨk.
Mmǔ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Kríspɔs. Abhak mǔnti ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt. Yi anoko Yesu Acha nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm. Bɛyǎ bǒ Kɔrint bachak abhɛ́n bághòk nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m mánóko nkwɔ, nɛ bájwíti bhɔ.
Mɔ́ngo ajwi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ɛyɔ. Afú ndǔ kɛnɛ́m nɛ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ mmu kɛbhɔŋ mbi bɛchwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm. Bɛghori tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɔángɛl tándrámɔt bakɛmɛ amɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ nyaka bɛfʉɛt kpɨk.
Báre kɔ mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ. Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ manyiɛp achi, arɛm ntá Fílip bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ manyiɛp. Ntí achí anɛ bábhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́jwiti mɛ?” [Fílip akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Mbák ɔ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛnkɛm nɛ Yesu, mɛ̌kwáy bɛ́jwiti wɔ.” Mmǔ wu akɛmɛ yí bɛ́ “Nnókó bɛ Yesu Kristo chí Mmɔ Mandɛm.”]
Kɛ bachak báré way bakoŋo Yesu mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mmɛ́m akɛm bǒbhɛn!” Nɛtwɔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ 
Puyɛ̌ chi bɛ aká bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́ghátí yi. Yímbɔŋ anáŋ abhɔŋ ɛkwak bɛpɛt bɛ́twɔ awu bɛghɔ be mankɛm. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, ǎtwɔ̀ yɛ nkwɔ ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyi.
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ mmu abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛyɨkɨ wáwák. Mmu abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛyɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ mfay, mbɔnyunɛ mfay chi bɛchɔ́kɔ́ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ achák ndǔ áfù amɨk. Abhɔ́ŋ babhaŋ apay mbɔ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́bhák mbɔ ɛnɛ nnya.
Bɔtá, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bǎrɨŋɨ yi Mmu ánáŋ achi nyaka tɛ mpok bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghoko mmɨk. Bɛsak, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ mǎnu nɛ mbʉ́mbʉ, kpatɛ bǎsɔt awɔ́nɛm.
Ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ, Píta akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bě bakɛmɛ́ ɛtɔk nɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk,
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm mmu ákʉ́ Yesu Acha ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ǎkʉ chɔŋ bɛsɛ́ nkwɔ́ sɛ́mpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ yi, nɛ ansɔt bhɛsɛ nɛ bhe sɛ́mbak nɛ Yesu ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́t bɛchɔkɔ bhi.
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎyaŋ nkʉ be yi?”
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bo bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ndu ákʉ̀ mámbák chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛyɔ chi akap Mandɛm nɛ ǎfʉ̀ɛt chi ntá Yesu Kristo bɛkʉ nɔ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́ ndu bɛfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ǎghàti bhɛsɛ sayri bɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ mbɔk bho bárɔ bɛ́koŋo nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp, mándɔbhɛ koŋo chí bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́rwɔ bho nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛghati Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Tiatíra. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn chi bɛyɔŋɔ́ Mmɔ Mandɛm mmǔ amɨ́k ayi ápè chuuu mbɔ nɛ́rɨ́-ngó, bɛkak ɛbhi mɛ́ngɔɔ nɔkɔ ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ mbɔ brɔ́ns anɛ básɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ɛtaŋtí ngó báfɛ́rɛ́ mɛ́nyɨ́ŋɨ́ arɛ́.
Akɛ́m yi ndǔ awɔ arɛm bɛ, “Talíta, kum!” Nɔ chi bɛ, “Mɔ́ngɔsɔŋ, faté!”
“Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, nkwaŋankɨ amɔt arɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛtak ɛnyǔ nchwifú amɛm nkɨ ywi. Ɛnɛ́ yi átàk árɔ̀ŋ, mbɔk akwɛnti ndǔ mɔ́mbi anɛ áchí amɛm nkɨ. Bo báyáti. Kɛnɛn kɛ́twɔ́ kɛ́bwɔ́pti nchwi yɔ nkɛm.
Ndɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ndu Ábraham nɛ Áisek nɛ Jekɔ́p bárɔ mmɨkɨ nɛ, báchí nɛpɛ́m, nɛ Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɔ. Mandɛm achí Mandɛm bo abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m. Apú Mandɛm bawú. Bě bo Sádusi bǎchi ndǔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ tontó!” 
Batɔŋɔ́ nse bhɔ bágʉɛti mmʉɛt mǎnchwe ndǔ manɛrɛ́kɛt mánu nɔkɔ bɛ́ bo bákɛ́ noko tɛtɛp Mandɛm. Báchi mbɔ Jánɛs nɛ Jambrɛs bo mánú nyaka bɛ bo bákɛ́ noko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm átó Moses ángati Mfɔ Íjip. Báchí bǒ bɛbɛ́ptí nkaysi nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu tɛtɛp.
Ɛrɛmɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ mbɨ ɛ́fʉɛ́t. Ghɔ́ ká, bɛ́chák bɛ́páy bɛ́twɔ̀.
Bo abhɛn bákɛ̀m ɛkɨ́kɨ́ ndǔ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀, báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhɔ kɛnɛ́m nɛ kɛnókó nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn mmu ápú gu. Mandɛm ǎchyɛ̀ bhɔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Nchi yaŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ baghɔrɛ́ mánsɔ́bhɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt nɛ kɛnókó, mándɨŋɨ ndu báyàp ndɛn nɛ mámfyɛ yɔ sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛ́kwáy. Bákɛ́ ghoko batí ámbák yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyu nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ŋwaŋwaŋ arɛ́ kpaŋtí kpáŋtí nɛ bákɛ́ fyɛ ndɛn bɛyǎ nkáp.
Abhɨŋɨ yɛ bakoŋo bhi bati byo nɛ apay ató nɛfí, bati apay apay. Achyɛ bhɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛbok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.
mámbɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm. Bǒ mankɛm bághɔ́ ndǔ bakoŋo Yesu bákʉ̀ nɛ báre bhɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ bhɔ. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛwak Acha ankʉ nɔkɔ bo abhɛn yi ápɛ́mɛ́ mánchɛ́m nɛ bakoŋo bhi.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, bakoŋo Yesu mankɛm bati byo nɛ apay bápɛ́t nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm atú Gálili, Yesu aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bákɛ́m chɔŋ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm mámfyɛ yi amɔ bǒ mmɨk.
Mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ tɔŋ bɛ bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ndǔ baraká nkáp nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk, agha ákway bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ be amfyɛ kɛfɔ̌ bakáp ɛkɛn kɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti amɔ yɛka?
Mɛnyɨŋ bɛchi bɛrat ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhak mpoknkɛm. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛrɛ chi nɛka, nɛbhakántɨ, nɛ ɛkɔŋ. Kɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛrat, ɛnɛ ɛcha bɛchak mɛnkɛm chi ɛkɔŋ.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ángɛl achak ndu árè tɛ amfǎy nɛbu. Are twɔ́ nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm nɛ achi tɛtɛp mpoknkɛm. Are twɔ́ nɛ yɔ ntá bǒ mmɨk, nɔ chi, bɔ̌bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm, nɛ bǒ manɛrɛ́kɛt ankɛm, nɛ bǒ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk mɛnkɛm.
Mmu anɛ ánú asɔt awɔ́nɛm báfyɛ yí ɛ́wɛt pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt, nɛ mpú fɛrɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni ndǔ ɛkáti nɛpɛ́m. Chɔŋ ndɛm bɛsí Ɛtaya nɛ bɔángɛl bɛ yi achi mmu wa.
Júdas mmu átí Yesu ághók nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ bábhɔŋ bɛway Yesu nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ́jwí yi antɨ ɛ̌ti ɛpɔ̌ndak ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́. Asɔt nkáp silbha bɛbhɔ́k ɛsa nsɛm byo anɛ báchyɛ́ yí antí Yesu arɔk bɛ́kɛ́mɛ ntá bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk.
Bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ Yesu Kristo nɛ bɔángɛl Mandɛm, nchí ghati wɔ bɛ ɔ́mbʉ́rɛ́ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn sayri, ɔkɛ́ tɔ́ŋ kɛnkábhɛ́ nɛ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛta áŋɛ̀mɛ bawú anchyɛ bhɔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ́ kɛ̌ Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi nchí chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ntá yɛ̌ agha anɛ mɛ́yàŋ bɛchyɛ nɛpɛ́m.
Bo abhɛn bághɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárɨ́, báré ghati bǒ abhɛn bárɔŋ arɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí ntá mmu anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri nyaka nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí nɛ nkwɔ́ bakók.
Bakoŋo bhi bárɔ́k maŋɛmɛ yi barɛm bɛ, “Acha, pɛmɛ́ bhɛsɛ, sɛ́twɔ̀ gu anyɛ́n!”
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́fákárí bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ andɛm, ɛmfu tɛtɛp.
Sɛ́ndɔ́ yɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́, bɛ́ bɛbʉ́ bɛ́kɛ́ gó mɛ́njwí ndǔ nkwɔ́ aywɛsɛ́. Sɛ́nkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ chí bɛrɨ, sɛ́nkoŋo nɔkɔ mbi Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ nɛ́mɔ́t. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ sɛ́mbak mbɔ brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔŋ yís anɛ bo mányiɛ nyaka mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ bɛsɛ́ nkwɔ́ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ mbɔ bǒ tɛtɛp abhɛn bapu ápú nɛ bhɔ́.
Ghɔ́ ká bɛrɛmɛ́ basɨŋ amɛn nsɔ́rɛ́ bɛsɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá yɛka nɛ awɔ́ awa mɛmbɔŋ.
Ánáŋ ántwɔ́, bákʉ mkpaká bho bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm mánchɛm bɛsí bhi, ǎfap bhɔ́ ndǔ bakwɔ́ apay, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n áfàp mmɛ́nɛ́ mbɔŋ nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n,
Ndǔ bɛtaŋá Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmú achí nɛ bhɛsɛ, kɛ́m Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ báfyɛ wɔ amɔ sayri.
Jɔ̌n até ntísiɛ ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ yi arɨŋɨ. Asɨ́ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághɔ́.
ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi yɛ bɛ Kristo achyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni mbɔ akap ndɔŋ amɔt ndu bɛ́pɔkɔ bɛbʉ́ bo mankɛm, nɛ chɔŋ ampɛt antwɔ́, puyɛ̌ ndu bɛfɛrɛ bɛbʉ́, kɛ ndu bɛpɛmɛ bo abhɛn bachi nɛ amɨ́k ambi mánòŋ yi.
Nɛ sɛ́chí bo abhɛn Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́. Abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bho, puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ bo Israɛl kɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Nɛ bɛ́yɨŋɨ nɛkʉ anɛ Mandɛm akʉ Yesu ámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnyu ɛnɛ yi ápú pɛrɛ gú, Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ́: ‘Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ bhe áfɔ́k mbɔ ɛnyu mfyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp nɛ Debhít nɛ njɛt yi nɛ ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ.’
Bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Mbɔ bhɛsɛ sɛchi nyaka mpok bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ, mbʉ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka nɛ bhɔ bɛ mángwáy barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm Acha.’
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛbhʉɛrɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ayi nɛbhʉɛt, bachiǎkap báre rɔŋ ndǔ mɔ́kɛt anɛ mbɨ, mpok nɛ mpok, ndǔ bɛkʉ ɛbhap bɛtɨk.
Bákɛ́mɛ Yesu bɛ, “Mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m bɛ ɔchí Jɔ̌n Njwiti. Bachak bɛ Ɛláija, abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ́ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Jeremáya, nɛ bɛ, mbák puyɛ̌ yi, nɔ chi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ achak.”
“Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bǒ mmɨk bɛ yi achi mmu wa, chɔŋ mɛnkwɔ́ ndɛm bɛsí Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay ndǔ nywɔp manyé, bɛ mmu wu achi awa.
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛ́fú amʉɛt mmu wu bɛrɔk bɛchwe amʉɛt nkwɔ́ bakók. Bakók mankɛm bárókóri básɛp ndǔ nkokonjiɛ dúgúdúgúdúgú bágúrɛ anyɛ́n.
Bákɛ́mɛ yí bɛ, “Chí ntí Sísa, Mfɔ Rom. Nɛ nnyɛ́n, chi ɛni.” Yesu aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chiɛ́ yɛ́ ka mfɔ Rom yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛyi, mǎnchyɛ Mandɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛnɛ Mandɛm.”
Anɛ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛpay atwɔ́ nɛ mɛnwi arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta, ɔchyɛ́ nyaka mɛ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛpay. Nnu kpát bɛchak bɛpay bɛko amfay’.
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákwáy nɛkwáy báchyɛ́ Mandɛm bakak. Báfú yɛ bákó amfay Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif. 
Aka nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn yi ayambɨ ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ chɔŋ yi anchyɛ bhɔ nkáp anɛ́ ákwáy ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp nɛmɔt. Ató yɛ́ bhɔ bɛ mándɔ́k mánkʉ́ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ ywi.”
Nywɔp nɛ́mɔt, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bábhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Ntɨ́kɨ́ mpok Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bo fá amɨk mbɔ Mfɔ wap?” Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ ɛrɨŋ ɛ́pú ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm abho bɛ́kɛm bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap.
Yɛ̌ ɔchí agha, mpok ɔ́tàŋ bo nɛ ɔ́nkʉ nɔkɔ nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀, ɔpú kway bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt bɛsí Mandɛm. Bɛ́taŋ mmu kɛ ɔ́nkʉ nɔkɔ nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀ chi bɛrɛm bɛ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́kwɛ̌n manyé bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu áchí Yerúsalɛm ndǔ mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, bɛyǎ bo básɨ́kɨntɨ nɛ yi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn bághɔ́ yi ákú.
Ndu Páílet áyàŋ nyaka bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ báyàŋ, afɛrɛ Barábas ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bádɛ́n Yesu nɛ ɛ́kpá. Achyɛ yi ntá yap bɛ́ mángó ndǔ ɛkotákátí. 
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ nchí fyɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk, ndɛp nɔkɔ mmʉɛt nɛ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Kristo áchyɛ̀ mɛ.
Bɔ̌ma, nchí yaŋ bɛtɨk bhe ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ ngátí nyaka bhe, bǎbhʉ́rɛ yɔ antɨ nɛ bǎté kpɨrí ndu yɔ.
Kɛ mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu afyɛ́ ntí ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mǔngo bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk amɛm áchwí nɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋ áchwí bárɛ̀m ɛcha ɛnɛ́ Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m.
Kɛ bághɔ́ bɛ́ ɛbhɨkɨ rɨ bɛ mánkɛ́m yi mpok ɛpa. Bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ́ mbák mánkɛ́m yi mpok ɛpa, bo bágʉɛ́p ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ɛtɔk. 
Ndaká yí bǎpú rɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́ndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ bɛ Mandɛm antɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ,” mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk bo báchɔ̀ŋti manyɛ́n ayɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m ɛnyu yɔ. Chɔŋ mámbɔŋ ntɛmsi anɛ akway nɛ bhɔ. 
Aghɔ́ bɛ́ nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́nɛ. Ɛnyɨŋɨ́fú ɛ́fú arɛ ɛre sɛp amɨk. Ɛ́bhak mbɔ ntěndɛn nɛgho ɛnɛ́n bákɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ batí yi anwi básɛ̀bhɛ amɨk.
Baghɔkɔ bhi barɔk máŋɛ́mɛ́ yi barɛm bɛ, “Ɛta! Ɛta! Sɛ́twɔ gu anyɛ́n!” Yesu aŋɛmɛ asáy mbʉ́ɛ́p nɛ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn. Mbʉ́ɛ́p ágú, nɛ nnyɛ́n nɛ́kwɛ́n tɨɨ.
Ɛnɛ́ mpok áfʉ̀ɛt běku ɛbhɔ, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́k ntá yi barɛm bɛ, “Nywɔp nɛ́naŋ nɛrɔŋ nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ sɛchi-nɛ arɛ́ chi ɛbhɨ.
Ngɔ̌ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bǒbha bábhɔ̀ŋ amɛm ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ ngók nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ ɛnap, nɛ nsɛp ntwɔ bɛfɛrɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyɔ. Twɔ́ yɛ́, chɔŋ ntó wɔ Íjip.’
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Nkʉ wɔ ɔ́mbák chi ntá bo bɛyǎ bɛtɔk. Yi achi bɛsí Mandɛm mmu yi ánókó, Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Yí ǎchyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́pú ɛmbak, ɛ́mbak.”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bariɛp amɛn, sǒ ká amɔ́ fɛrɛ́ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kwày mɛnyɔp mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ nɛ batɨ̌ ywɛsɛ. Sɛ́ncháy Mandɛm, sɛ́nu bɛbhak nyáŋá bɛsí bhi ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi. 
Bě abhɛn mǎnókó yi, ntá yɛka yi arɨ acha kɛ ntá bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ noko yi basɨŋ bɛ, “Nkúbhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn batěkɛt bábyáká, nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́yíbhírí nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kɛ̀m ɛkɛt.”
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́gháti Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ tó ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Pɛ́gamɔm. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ntá mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akparɛnja nsɛm ɛpay anɛ ácháp.”
Kɛ Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ bo abhɛn batɨ apɛt apu bɔ amɛm nɛpɔptǐntɨ́, achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ ndu Táytɔs átwɔ́.
Nɛ ndu bághɔ́ mbɛ́ntí anɛ bákʉ́ yi ataŋa nɛpak Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n, manyu áchók bhɔ.
Atwɔ́ ntá bǒbhi, kɛ bǒbhi bábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt yi nɛ maŋák.
Kɛ nchí dɛn mmʉɛt nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri bɛ mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛkɛm mmʉɛt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Nchí yaŋ bɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, Mandɛm akɛ rɔ mɛ ansɛm, mɛ mmu ngati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, ansɔt bo báchák.
Yesu akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Ndak anɛ́ ɔ́bhɛ́bhɛ́ mɛ, áfu chi wɔmbɔ̌ŋ antɨ kɛ bo báchák kɛ̌ bágháti wɔ wu ɛ̌ti ya?”
Acha, ghɔ́ yɛ ndǔ bápà bhɛsɛ. Kʉ bɛ bhɛsɛ́ bǒ bɛtok abhɛ, sɛ́ngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bho Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɛ nɛ nɛtaŋántɨ nɛnkɛm.
Ndu Yesu ákɔ̀ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm, are fʉɛ́t ndǔ ndyɛrɛbhɨ Samária nɛ Gálili.
Sɛ́ghɔ̀ yɛ bɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm bɛchi nyáŋá. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛchi nyáŋá, ɛ́chí chak, nɛ ɛrɨ.
Puyɛ̌ bɛ sɛ́mɔ̀ bɛyɛnti mmʉɛt nɛ bo abhɛn bákàk mmʉɛt. Kɛ nɛyɛnti mmʉɛt ɛnap nɛ batɨ ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ bácha bhɔ, nɛ́tɔ̀ŋ chi bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mbɔ̌ŋ kɛboŋ.
Ɛ́kʉ́ ákɔ́rɛ́ nɛ bɛtaka bɛkwɛn nɛntɨ nap ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí nɔ́kɔ́, Pɔ̌l akʉ ntɨ ɛni bɛ́ yí abhɔŋ bɛ́fʉɛ́t atú Masidónia nɛ atú Akáiya ampɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm. Arɛm bɛ, “Nnáŋ ngáká arɛ́, mbɔŋ bɛrɔŋ Rom nkwɔ.”
Ábraham ánoŋ yɛ nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ kpát abhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ yi.
Báchwé achwi bárɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs. Pɔ̌l arɔ Prisíla nɛ Akwíla angɔkɔnyɛ́n arɔk achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, are kɛ́m ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bo Israɛl.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bábhɛp bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛ́pú yaŋ mankʉ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt?”
Nɛ mbák mánókó nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp, kɛboŋ ɛkap kɛ́kway bɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm nɛ mámfú ndǔ ntá anɛ Satan. Bákwɛn nyaka ndǔ ntá yi mankʉ nɔkɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyaŋ bɔ́ mánkʉ.
Kɛ aya mmʉɛt arɔk ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́fu amɛm baso anɨkmʉɛt. 
Chɔŋ mánjɔkɔ yi, mámpati batíɛ́ yi amʉɛt, mándɛn yi nɛ ɛ́kpá nɛ mángwáy yi. Kɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.” 
Mpok yɔ, bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛka bɛbhak chi ɛbhɛn bǒ mmɨk nɛ mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ chi mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ anɛ, nɛ́nɛ, abhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ bɛpɨŋɨ́ bho. Mfɔ bɛfóŋó wu ǎkɛ̀m batɨ̌ bo abhɛn bátàŋti nɛ Mandɛm.
Sɛ́ndɛ́m yɛ bɛ yi? Bɛbhʉɛrɛ ɛbhé chi bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ kɛ? Wáwák! Ɛbhé kɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mándɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛchi. Mbɔ ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ fyɛ ngoŋo ndǔ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmu” mbʉ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛchi ndu bɛfyɛ ngoŋo ndu ɛnyɨŋɨ mmu.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta abhʉɛ́t bɛ́rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ́ abhak nɛ bo mankɛm abhɛn bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ akap chi mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi akʉ ntɨ bɛchyɛ, puyɛ̌ chi nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ, nɛ ɛ́kɛ́bhak chi mbɔ bɛ bápùri yi puri, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ mmu anɛ áchyɛ̀ akap nɛ maŋák.
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt mpoknkɛm nɛ ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áyà bhe mbi. Bǎk ká pě. Kɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ ká ɛkɨ́kɨ́ ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛ̌ti bǒ Mandɛm mankɛm bɛ yi ankwak bhɔ.
Bábhɨ́kɨ́re sense wáwák mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́. 
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm anɛ ághɔ́kɔ́, árɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap, achí mbɔ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt anɛ áfɛ̀rɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛkɔ nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛsɨ amɛm mɔ́kɛt anɛ yi ábhʉ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ.” 
Bɔ́ babhɔŋ bárɛ̀m ɛnyǔ básɔ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ mpok sɛ́twɔ́ awu ntá yɛka nɛ ɛnyǔ bǎtɨknsɛm ntá bɔmandɛm nsé bǎrɔ́bhɛ chyɛ kɛnókó chi ntá Mandɛm. Yi aywǐnti kɛ achi Mandɛm anɛ tɛtɛp nɛ yi kɛ áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.
Mpok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhó bɛfakari, tě ká sɛnɛ́ nɛ nkaysi bɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm áfɛrɛ bhe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri arɔp chi kɛkwɔt.” 
Barábas chi mmu anɛ báfyɛ́ nyaka ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ndǔ barak apay, “Agʉɛbhɛ́ nyaka ɛbyɔk ɛtɔk, nɛ awáy mmu.”
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛtɔŋ. Arɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ mmǔ ywɛka amɔt abhɔŋ mǔbɛtɨk anɛ áchí ɛbhɨ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk, yɛ̌ chí ndu bɛbhábhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n, yɛ̌ chi ndu bɛ́kwáŋ mbaŋ. Mbák afǔ ɛbhɨ apɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, wɔ chi-bɛtɨk ywi ɔ̌ghati yi bɛ, ‘Twɔ́ chɔkɔ́ amɨk nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́’?
Bǎkway bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ nyaka mbɔk batábhɛ́nɔk bɛ ambat bhɛsɛ ndu ɛnɔk.”
Mɛ, mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ mmu mbɔ yi anɛ ákway bɛkwak be ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yɨ́ŋí nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka, bɛ mǎmfyɛ́ mɛ ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu Kristo.
Tɛ́mté wu, Yesu afyɛ́ bhɔ ntɨ arɛm bɛ, “Chí mɛ, bǎkɛ́ chay!”
Tɛ́mchok, Moses nɛ Ɛláija, barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm abhɛn tɛsáy, bábhési mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ kɛpɨ nɛ Yesu.
bɛ́ ambak mǔnto ndu bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn ndu bɛsɔt ɛpók Júdas mmú árɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwáy nɛ yi?
Fʉɛ́t yɛ́ ka ndǔ nyǔbhá anɛ achi mábhɛ́rí mbɔnyunɛ wú kɛ̌ mmu áfʉɛt arɛ́ anchwe ndǔ mbǐ nɛpɛ́m. Mbi wu ábè mmʉɛt bɛfʉɛt arɛ́, nɛ bǒ abhɛn báfʉɛ̀t arɛ babhɨkɨ ya.” 
nɛ akɛka bɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ámpɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ámfʉɛt amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ndu áyàŋ mbǐ mbɨŋ.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ nɛtwɔ wa, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm. Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm nɛ ngátí bhe bɛ́fàkari, dɨŋɨ́ ka bɛ mpok nɛtwɔ wa arɔp kɛkwɔt.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mpǎy manywɔp, Fɛ́liks nɛ ngɔrɛ́ aywi Drusíla batwɔ. Drusíla abhak mmu Israɛl. Báto mmu bɛ ambɨŋɨ Pɔ̌l. Atwɔ nɔkɔ, bátá batu bare ghok ndu yi árɛ̀m ɛnyǔ mmu ákway bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Kɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap nɛ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi nɛ yi, nɔ chi bǒnkwɔ Sádusi, bábhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ mpap amɨ́k.
Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhʉ̀ɛrɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛjwi yi antɨ pɔɔt. Ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ sɛbharɛ mmʉɛt nɛ yí.
Yɛ̌ndu ɛchi nɔ, bɛsɛ́ bo sɛ́bhárɛ́ mʉɛt nɛ Acha sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ apú ndǔ mʉɛt ɛyi, achí antɛnɛ́ mbakanɛm. Nɛ mbakanɛm apú ndǔ mʉɛt ɛyi, achí antɛnɛ́ ngɔrɛ́.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anyiɛ́ anɛ ákwáy yi. Bakɔŋo bhi bábwɔpti nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́. Nɛ́jwí bɛkay tándrámɔt.
Aghɔ́ nkwɔ kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ amɔt anɛ ɛyi ɛ́pú ndu afyɛ́ bɔ̌bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkap bapay.
Bě nnyɔ́ ɛnɛ! Bě bho bǎbɛbhɛ bǎchá mbɔ̌ŋ bɛfé! Bǎkáysí bɛ́ bǎkway bɛbhɔŋ mbi bɛbʉɛ bɛ Mandɛm akɛ tɛmsi bhe amɛm nɛpǐngo?
Báyá yi báfú ɛtɔk nɛ yí, bátɛ́mti yi nɛ bɛtay bawáy. Batísiɛ bɛtábhá báfɛ́rɛ nkú mfǎmʉɛt ɛyap, barɔ ntá ɛsakámu amɔt bɛ ambabhɛri nɔkɔ. Ɛsakámu wu aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Sɔ̌l.
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmǔ anɛ ápú kwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Ábraham arɔŋ nyaka ambɨ mɛnoko bariɛp Mandɛm. Are noŋ ambaka nɔkɔ ntɨ yɛ̌ndu ɛ́be nyaka mmʉɛt mɛnoko bɛ bariɛp Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛfu tɛtɛp. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, achí chi ntá bo bɛyǎ bɛtɔk bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm aghati yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhɛ mánja máncha.”
Nɛ mbák bápú makati bɛ Mandɛm ǎghok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnap, mmǔ nɛme ǎtaŋ. Mandɛm Acha ǎkʉ mmu nɛme antaŋ, amfoŋori yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́.
Básɔ́t bɔ̌batábhɛ́nɔk nsɛ̌nsé mánɨ́ mbɔ ntá kɛfɔ báfyɛ́ yí antí, básɔ́t ɛnɔkɔfú báfyɛ́ awɔ́nɛm aywi. Bábhó bɛ́tɛ́p mánɛ́n bɛsí ɛbhi máŋɔkɔ nɔkɔ yí bɛ, “Acha mfɔ bo Israɛl, kɛnókó kɛ́chí ɛkɛ ɛta!”
Bátɛ́mɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ yi, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ́chí mpǒknkɛm anɛ mɛnchí atú Esia bɛ́bhó nywɔp ɛnɛ́n mbɨ bɛ́gháka ɛchɔŋ.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas babhak Ikɔ́niɔm ndu ɛrɔri mpok mángati nɔkɔ bo mbok Acha kpoŋoroŋ kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy. Mandɛm are tɔ́ŋ bo Ikɔ́niɔm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ mbok anɛ bɔ́ Pɔ̌l bághàti bho ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi achí tɛtɛp, akʉ nɔ ndu áchyɛ́ bhɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay.
Báfʉɛt yɛ atú Pisídia, bárɔk atú Pamfília.
Bǎchi batísiɛ bhɛsɛ. Mandɛm nkwɔ achi ntísiɛ bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ́ nɛntɨ ɛnɛka bakoŋo Yesu nɛchí nyáká nyáŋá nɛ chak nɛ nɛ́kɛ bhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Tɛ mpok anɛ njámbɨ ngoko bɛ bǎsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Acha nɛ bɛ́ bǎkɔŋ bo Mandɛm mankɛm,
Kɛ árɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mmokoti bɛ̌tak ɛbha, ngoko ɛbhɛn bɛ́chɨ́kɨ́tí, mfyɛ́ mbwɔt aya nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbha arɛ.’
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎsɔ̀t mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛtɔŋ bɛsɛ bɛ mpoknkɛm anɛ mɔ́kɛt anɛ mbɨ abhʉɛt téé, mbi bɛchwe arɛ apu bhak.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm abhɛ́p Stífin bɛ “Ɛchi tɛtɛp bɛ ɔkʉ barak anɛ bárɛ̀m nɔ bɛ ɔkʉ?”
Kɛ wɔ nkwǎ, ɔchí agha bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ Mandɛm? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngoko-bɛte ásɔ́rɛ́ ntɔp ánɨ́ ɛ́kway bɛrɛm ntá ngoko bɛtě ntɔp bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔ́ghókó mɛ chi ɛnyu ɛnɛ kɛ?”
nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhak nyáŋá, mbɔnyu mɛnchí nyáŋá.”
nɛ anɛnɛ nɔkɔ nɛ antɔŋ nɔkɔ bɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ angú, kɛ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Pɔ̌l are ghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Yesu mmu nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi kɛ áchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.”
Kɛ akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Pú bǎghɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ báté bɛkɛt ɛbhɛn bɛchi ndǔ ɛkɛrákap kɛ ɛ́bhak ɛnyunɛ? Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ amɨk ɛnkɛm, yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp téé.” 
mbɔnyunɛ, mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ, mámaka yi ɛ́chák. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ, yɛ̌ chí mandú anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, chɔŋ mánsɔt mamfɛrɛ ntá yi.” 
Mmok ábhó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ́nɛ́m, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́k ntá yi barɛm bɛ, “Ghatí bǒbhɛn bɛ mándɔ́k ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá kɛkwɔt nɛ ndǔ bakɨ mánjáŋ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bɛbhak bɛbhʉrɛ. Ɛtɔk ɛ́pú fá!”
Ntɨkɨ mmu ábhák ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu kɛ kɛchyɛ yí nkáp nɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chák? Ntɨkɨ mmu ábhɔ̀ŋ nkɨ kɛ yí kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́sɔt nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn yí áfɛ́rɛ́ arɛ́ anyiɛ? Ntɨkɨ nchɨkɨ mpɔŋ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ mɛ́nyú nɛ́bhɨ̌ mpɔŋ?
Ntwɔ nyaka awu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ bɛtaŋ bɛ́pú nɛ mɛ nɛ mbɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛcháy, ngwɛt nɔkɔ gbagbǎgbak.
Ɛrɨ mbɔŋ bɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ ámbák nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛká ndu bɛkʉ mǎngɔ́ bǒ abhɛn bákòŋo Yesu nɛ ntɨ nɛ́mɔ́t.
Ɛfakari nyaka bɛ Hɛ́rɔd achyɛ ɛyɔŋ, bákɛ́m Jɔ̌n, bagwɔt, nɛ báfyɛ́ yi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti Hɛródias, ngɔrɛ́ mɔ́mayi Fílip anɛ yí áfɔ́ŋɔ́, ábháy.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́kʉ́ bo Israɛl bábho bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ná mmǔ-nɛ ǎkway bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ nyamwʉɛ́t ayi bɛ sɛnyiɛ?”
Sɛ́chɔ́kɔ́ kpát, sɛ́kɛ pɛrɛ kwáy bɛkɛpntɨ, sɛ́ka bɛrɔp ansɛm ndu ɛtɔk Atɛns,
Mmu anɛ áchá báchák abhɔŋ bɛbhak mǔbɛtok ywɛka.
Nɛ are ghati bo ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhàk nɛ mmu mbɔ Mfɔ ywi, antɔŋ nɔkɔ nkwɔ́ bo mɛnyɨŋ kpoŋoroŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo Acha, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu kɛmɔ bɛchɛt yi mbi bɛ akɛ kʉ nɔ.
“Nɛ sɛ́nsɔt bɛ mfɔ amɔt abhɔ̌ŋ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nka byo (,). Apɛrɛ́ rɔŋ mɛnu nɛ mfɔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nka ɛsa, (,) ǎkʉ yi? Pú ǎyambɨ anchɔkɔ, ankaysi sayri, mbák ǎkway mɛnu nɛ mfɔ wu?
“Bǎkɛ́ sɔt mɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm mǎnchyɛ ntá bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ yi. Báchí mbɔ mmú. Mmu ákɛ́ sɔt mɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ ntá bo abhɛn bábyak bhɔ. Báchí mbɔ bakók. Mbák mánchyɛ bakók ɛnyɨŋɨ́ nkáp, básɔ̀t mányɔp chi ndǔ ntɔp. Nɛ mbák mǎnchyɛ mmú mɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm, ǎyibhiri mmʉɛt antoko bhe anɛt.” 
Ándru, nɛ Fílip, nɛ Batolómio, nɛ Mátio, nɛ Tɔmás, nɛ Jéms mmɔ̌ Alfeyɔs, nɛ Tadiɔs, nɛ Símun, mfyɛ̌-bɛtaŋ ndǔ barakátɔk,
Yesu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ mbok nɛwú Jɔ̌n, afa, bárɔk bachwe amɛm áchwí, babho bɛrɔŋ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yɛ̌ mmu achak apu. Ǎyàŋ nyaka bɛ mámbák bɔbhɔ. Kɛ mpok bo bághókó bɛ yi asɔt áchwí ǎrɔ̀ŋ, báfá bɛtɔk ɛbhap, babho bɛkoŋo yi nɛ bɛkak.
Apɛtnsɛm, aghɔ́ bhɔ bati arat ndu bápɛt bákwɛ́nɛ́ kɛnɔ́. Bápú kwáy nyaka bɛ́chɔ́kɔ pě ndǔ kɛnɔ́ kɛ́jwí bhɔ amɨ́k. Bɔ́ kɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákway bɛghati yi.
Mmu anɛ ánù ánsɔ̀t awɔ́nɛm, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ yí bɛtaŋ bɛ anchɔkɔ nɛ mɛ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛya, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛmbɔŋ nnú, nsɔt awɔ́nɛm, nchɔkɔ nɛ ɛtayá ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi.
Jems arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Ndu nkaysi aya, sɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ sɔŋɔri bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl abhɛn bátwɔ̀ ntá Mandɛm.
Nkɛmɛ yi bɛ, ‘Acha, bɔ́ babhɔŋ bárɨ́ŋɨ sayri bɛ nchí rɔ́ŋ nyaka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl nkʉ nɔkɔ bɛ mánkɛ́mtí bo abhɛn mánóko wɔ, nɛ mandɛn, mámfyɛ nɔkɔ mbɔk yap ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ Debhít arɛmɛ nyaka bɛ áfɔ́k áchí nɛ mmǔ anɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ achi chak, yɛ̌ndu abhɨkɨ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkʉ bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ yi áfɔ́k wu.
Nɛ yí mmú átó mɛ, achi nɛ mɛ. Abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ mɛ mbak awanti mbɔnyunɛ mɛ́kʉ̀ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákɔ́ŋɔ́.”
Mbi anɛ báchwè ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt Mandɛm abhʉɛ́t yɛ fúú. Kɛ bo abhɛn baghoko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mpok ɛyɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ chwe arɛ ɛ̌ti nɛtaŋántɨ ɛnap.
Sɛ́rɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ sɛkɔŋ bɔ̌ Mandɛm tɛtɛp mbák sɛ́kɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ mbák sɛ́bhʉɛ̀rɛ bɛbhé bhi.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ nɛ bǒbati bare kway nɛkwáy nɛkɔ bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́kwáy bɛsɔt ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p ɔ́mbakari bɛ́bhánɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ báwǎy nyaka wɔ nɛ manoŋ amɛ amɛn árɔ́ŋɔ́ amɨk kɛ ɔ́kú bo nɛ mɔ bɛ mámbák bo Mandɛm. Ɔkʉ nɔ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ bho, nɛ bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk, nɛ bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkwɔ́ bho.
Bǎkɛ́ chɔkɔ mǎnkáysi bɛ bǎchí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛpu kway bɛkʉ bhe. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛsɔt batay anɛ ankʉ yɔ́ ámbak bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak bɛghati bhe, kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛfyɛ bhɔ mɛnkɛm amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Mbɔ̌ŋ nkaysi bɛ́twɔ bɛghɔ bhe bɛ sɛ́ndɛm kɛpɨ bɛsí nɛ bɛsi, bɛ́ maŋák amɛsɛ anjwi pɔɔt.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bárɔ́k ntá Yesu babhɛp yi ɛ̌ti nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko nyaka bɛ bawú bápɛ̀t chɔŋ nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Babhɛp yi bɛ,
Bo bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari, bábhak maknkay tontó, babho bɛbɨti Mandɛm mmú áchyɛ́ nkwǎ ɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ. 
Ɛnyǔ baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bábhɔŋ ɛkwak ndu bɛ́ghɔk mɛnyɨŋ bɛkɔ mpoknkɛm kɛ bápú kwáy bɛbhɔŋ nɛ́jwǐmɛm ndǔ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ábhʉɛ́t amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, bɛyǎ manɛ́mámɨk nɛ bakɛm bárɔ́k ntá yi, abú bhɔ mankɛm.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ bě bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bǎsɔt ndu bɛ́rɨ amɔt ndǔ baru byo mǎnchyɛ ntá Mandɛm, mǎnkʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ mbwɔ́t achak, kɛ bǎpú fyɛ́ ntí bɛbhak chak nɛ bo mankɛm, bǎpú fyɛ́ ntí bɛghɔ bho ntínso, nɛ bǎpú fyɛ́ ntí bɛbhak tɛtɛp nɛ bo mankɛm. Ɛ́rɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛcha bɛkɔrɛ mɛnyɨŋ baru byo, mǎnchyɛ ndu amɔt ntá Mandɛm. Ɛ́rɨ nyaka bɛ mǎnkóŋó ɛbhé ɛnɛ bɛkɔrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ baru byo mǎnchyɛ ndu amɔt ntá Mandɛm, kɛ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nyaka bɛghɔkɔntɨk bɛbhé bɛ́chák.
Akɛmɛ yi bɛ ‘Babhaŋá bawɛt bɛsa bɛtay.’ Mmǔ bɛtɨk wu aghati yi bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ɛkati barɛm ɛyɛ, sɔt, wupsi, sɨŋ babhaŋ bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo ndǔ ɛnɛ́ ɛkɔ nɛ.’
Filɛmɔn, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt nchí kaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛ,
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákway bɛkʉ bɛ ambak kpák nɛ bo mankɛm mpoknkɛm.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ mpok Kristo ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́twɔ fá amɨk, arɛm ntá Mandɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ yaŋ bɛ bo mánchyɛ́ akabhɛ́nya nɛ mɛnyǔ akap áchák. Kɛ ɔghókó chí mmʉɛt nkwǎ ɔchyɛ́ mɛ bɛ́ nchyɛ́ wɔ akap nɛ yɔ.
Pɔ̌l arɔ yɛ bɔ́ afú arɔk.
Bápɛt báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Yi bɛ́ ‘Mandu mpok’, mandú mpok, nɔ bɛ́ yi?” Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ jwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta árɛ̀m ɛnyu yɔ, nɛbháŋ nɛ́sɛp nɛkuti bhɔ. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m baghɔk Yesu bhɔ ndǔ nɛbháŋ nɛ́kùti bhɔ.
Nɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bɛsɛ nkwɔ. Mpok sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka baraka Mandɛm, sɛ́bhák basɛm antɛnɛ́ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ fá mmɨk.
Nɛ́rɨ́ nkwǎ nɛchi mbɔ nsɔm anɛ achi anɛt áchwí. Yɛ̌ndu nɛ́chí nɨ́ŋɨ́ nɨ́ŋɨ́, nɛ́pà bɛkʉ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ. Bě babhɔŋ mǎnkáysí ndǔ mɔ́nɛmbě ngó ákɛm ndǔ ɛrɛmɛ́ nchɔ́t ámbo bɛ́du gum gum gum.
Apɛt arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ pɔkɔ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnɔ, yɛ̌ ntɛm, yɛ̌ ɛbha, yɛ̌ brɛt, yɛ̌ nkáp, nɛ yɛ̌ chí ndɛn ɛ́chák.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎbhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ nɛtwɔ́ anɛ sɛ́twɔ́ awu bɛghɔ bhe ápú nyaka ndɛ́ndɛm.
Bɛ́kóŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́, bo Israɛl bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɔ́kway bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ndu bɛtɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ ɔbhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn?”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku, Yesu arɔk achɔkɔ mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay.
Apɛt abhɨŋɨ bɔ̌-bɛtok abhi báchák aghati bhɔ bɛ, ‘Dɔ́k ká ghati bo abhɛn nnáká bɛ́ ngwáy bhɔ bɛsɛnɛ́ mpɔŋ nɛ mǎnáŋ mana nɛnyíɛ́, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́náŋ ɛ́chí téé. Dɔ́k ká ghati bhɔ mántwɔ́.’
Mmɛ Jɔ̌n mɔmáyɛka, mɛ mmǔ amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu kɛ̌ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí nsoŋ amɔt nɛ be ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ̀, nɛ ndu Yesu achi Mfɔ ywɛsɛ nɛ ndǔ sɛchi kpirí ndǔ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ ɛyɛsɛ. Nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ amɛm ɛtɔk nɛntɨnyɛ́n ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Pátmɔs ndu nchi ghati bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ nte ntísiɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ bo bárɨŋɨ.
Básɔt Yesu bárɔk ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Golgóta, nɔ́ chi “Nɛbhʉɛt Ɛ̌nkɔ́nti.”
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn báchí amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm bághók ndak anɛ áfákárí. Ɛ́kʉ́ bábhó bɛ́bhɨ́ŋɨ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mɨk wu ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛyap bɛ Akɛldáma, nɔ́ chí mmɨkɨ́ manoŋ.
Kɛ ngɔrɛ́, ɛrɔ́rí ɛmɛnɛ ɛ́kwǎy nɛ yí tontó. Ɛ́kwǎy nɛ yí mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achyɛ́ yí ɛmɛnɛ́ntí bɛ ɛ́mbák mbɔ ndɛn anɛ ngɔrɛ́ ákuti ntí nɛ yɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ yɛ̌ mbʉ́ mánchɔkɔ chí kpák, batay ábɨk ambɨti Mandɛm.” 
Kɛ chi aghati bɔ̌-bɛtok bhi bɛ, ‘Twɔ́ ká ayak nɛ ɛ́wɛt ɛnɛ ɛrɨ́ ɛ́chá mǎnsɔbhɛri yi nɛ yɔ, mǎmfyɛ́ yi sɛnɔŋ ndǔ sɛnɔŋáwɔ, nɛ nkwɔbhánya bɛkak.
Nɔ chí, bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko nyaka Mandɛm mpok Nóa. Mandɛm ǎnòŋ nyaka nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ bɛ bɔ́ mángúpsí batɨ yap mpok Nóa ághòko áchwí. Bǎru bho bati anɛn abhɛn bachi amɛm áchwí kɛ bápɛ́m nyaka ndu áchwí ághɔ̀k amfǎnyɛ́n.
Anɛ ájwí bati apay atwɔ́ arɛm bɛ, ‘Acha, mbɔ̌ŋ nsay bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛtay amfay ɛbha ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ.’
Chák ká mmʉɛt bɛghɔ mbák, ndǔ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛka, bǎkòŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnókó. Yɨŋɨ́ ká mmʉɛt. Mbák ɛpu nɔ, nɔ́ bǎkwɛn nɛmɔ.
Natániɛl arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm tɛtɛp! Ɔchí Mfɔ bo Israɛl!”
Nɛ́nɛ, bɛsɛ bo sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ ndɛn anɛ ákútí batɨ yɛsɛ, sɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Acha, nɛ sɛ́yìbhiri bɛbhak mbɔ yi. Nɛ ndǔ sɛ́yìbhiri nɛŋɔ̌k nɛ nɛŋɔk, bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhi bɛ́ghɔ̀ bhɛsɛ amʉɛt mɛ́nja mɛndɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ. Acha mmu ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ ɛmbak nɔ.
Mbɔ mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́ ngátí bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ, mbʉ bákwáy bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, bápú kway bɛtaŋa bɛ babhɨkɨ kʉ bɛbʉ́.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, bakoŋo Yesu báfú ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bárɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛku nɛnyíɛ́ bápɛtnsɛm. Bábhák maknkay bɛghɔ bɛ Yesu ǎrɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ ngɔrɛ́, kɛ yɛ̌ mmǔ wap kɛbhɛ́p ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ, “Ɔ̌yàŋ yi?” Nɛ yɛ̌ amɔt kɛbhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔ́rɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ yi?”
Sɛ́chwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Rom, bárɔ́ Pɔ̌l ánchɔ́kɔ́ ndu mmʉɛt ɛyi, ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt ámbábhɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ yí.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bakoŋo bhi bárɛm bɛ, “Mbák ɛ́chí nɔ́, ntí ápú yɛ́ anɛ mmu abhay ngɔrɛ́.”
Bǎpɔkɔ nyaka ɛ́tɛm ɛnɛ́ mandɛm nsé anɛ áká nyɛ́n bɛ Mɔ́lɔk. Nɛ nɛmbe ɛnɛn mandɛm nsé Ráfan. Nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghókó ndu bɛchyɛ bhɔ kɛnókó. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, chɔŋ mfɛ́rɛ́ be ntó ɛtɔk ɛ́chák bɛfʉɛt Bábilɔn.’
Nɛ mɛ́máka ndǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ Mandɛm maŋák, bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ mbɔ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt amɔt nɛ mǎnkɔŋ bǒ mankɛm.
“Ntɔŋ, ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́chá bɛbhé Moses bɛ́chák chi ɛ́nɛ́?”
Yesu akó ambɨ njiɛ, achɔkɔ arɛ́ nɛ bakoŋo bhi.
Nɛ chɔŋ ankɛ́m bo Israɛl mbɔ Mfɔ mpoknkɛm. Kɛfɔ ɛki kɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti!”
Yesu asɛmti yí bɛ, “Kɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí, kɛ dɔ́k ntá nchiakap Mandɛm bɛ yi angɔ bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛmay. Ánáŋ ámbyó wɔ, ɔ́ndɔk, ɔnchyɛ yɛ akap ntá Mandɛm bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhé Moses. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bo bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛ́may.”
Ndǔ nkaysi mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ yi áyábhɛ́ bɛsɛ́ bɛ́ sɛ́mbák bɔ̌bhi. Afʉɛ́t ndǔ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi bɛkʉ bɛsɛ́ bɔ̌bhi. Nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mpoknkɛm. Ayap bɛsɛ́ bɛ sɛ́mbák bɔ̌bhi bɛ́ sɛ́mbák ambɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n yí ághókó. 
Anáŋ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri amɔ bɛyǎ baghaŋ nɛ achɔŋti nkáp ankɛm anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndɛ́ndɛm. Nte yi ambɛ́p andɔkɔ nɔkɔ chí ambɨ.
Sayri sayri, tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk, ‘Mandɛm ághókó nyaka bo, ngɔrɛ́ nɛ mbakanɛm.’
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Kpák ámbák nɛ bhe! Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛtaya átó mɛ, kɛ nchí tó be.”
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bábhó bɛ́bhát yí barak amʉɛt, kɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kɛmɛ yɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ.
Bǒbhɛn chi bo ɛnywíntí nɛ bákɔŋ bɛji batɨ. Bákòŋo chí bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù bɔ antɨ. Báchí bǒ mpányu nɛ básɔt sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu bɛsɔt nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ntá bho. 
Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú ndǔ nɛbháŋ ɛ́ndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Mɔ́wa anɛ njábhɛ́. Ghók ká yi!”
Ayap wɔ nɛ ntí bɛ́ chɔŋ ɔ́mbak ntísiɛ aywi ndu bɛ́gháti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n ɔ́ghɔ́ nɛ ɛbhɛn ɔghoko.
Mandɛm akʉ Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́ghɔ́ yi nɛ sɛchi batísiɛ bɛ achi nɛpɛ́m.
Nɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ nku anɛ Mandɛm anyǔ nyaka nɛ Ábraham. Mandɛm afyɛ́ Ábraham nɛ ɛbhárɛ́ mɔ́ywi bariɛp. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛpú rɛm bɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka yi nɛ bɛbhárɛ́ bɔ̌bhi bariɛp, bɛtɔŋ bɛ báya, kɛ ntá yi nɛ ɛbhárɛ́ mɔ́ywi, bɛtɔŋ bɛ chi amɔt. Ɛbhárɛ́mɔ wu chí Kristo.
Hɛ́rɔd ágú nɔ́kɔ́, ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi ntá Josɛ́f ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɛm ɛtɔk Íjip,
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bo báchák mankɛm bákàysi chi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyɨŋɨ ɛnap nɛpɛ́m, kɛfyɛ́ ntí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyɨŋɨ Yesu Kristo.
Mǔngo wu arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, twɔ́ sɛ́ndɔ́k bɛ mɔ́wa ákɛ́ sɛbhɛ.”
Mbɔ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ́ bo akap chi ɛ̌ti bábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé, mbʉ apú koŋo chi bariɛp ami ndu akap anɛ yi áchyɛ̀ bo. Kɛ chi ɛ̌ti bariɛp ami ntá Ábraham kɛ yi áchyɛ́ nyaka akap wu.
Kɛ mmǔ anɛ átwɔ́ nɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ chi mɛ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛrɛm tontó, kɛ ngɔ bɛ ákʉ́ chi be mankɛm.
Bɛbhé bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ nɛka ɛnɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Kristo. Ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ basɨŋɨ bɛ, “Mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé, ǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛ̌ti yɔ.”
Natániɛl abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ɔkʉ ná kɛ ɔ̌rɨŋɨ mɛ?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Fílip ápɛ́rɛ bhɨŋɨ wɔ ndǔ mpok anɛ ɔ́chí anɛrɛ́nɔk fig, nnáŋ ngɔ wɔ.”
Yi aghati bhɛsɛ ɛnyǔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ bɛ mǎnkɔŋ batɨ.
Abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛ́fʉɛ́t atú Samária ndu bɛrɔŋ Gálili.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛpe manyu, bákó ɛbhɨ, atú Gɛnɛ́sarɛt. Básɛt áchwí wap.
Bákɛ́mɛ Yesu chi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.” Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛnkwɔ́ mpú ghati yɛ bhe mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀.” 
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, yɛ̌ chí Mfɔ Sólomon mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛyǎ kɛnɛ́m, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka ndɛn ɛnɛ ɛrɨ mbɔ yɛ̌ chuchu amɔt.
Ɛ̌ti Acha Yesu, sɛptí ká mmʉɛt ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔnti ywɛka, nɛ yɛ̌ chi mfɔ ngo mmu bo mankɛm bachi antɛnɛ yi,
Nɛbho mpok yɔ, Yesu abho bɛ́gháti bho bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́tɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap arɔp chi kɛkwɔt.” 
Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Ɛ́be mmʉɛt tontó bɛ mǔnkáp anka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi!”
Fílip akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Nkáp nkʉbɛtɨk ndǔ manywɔp bɛsǎ byo ápú kway bɛ́ku brɛt anɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap akway bɛbhɔŋ mandú.”
Píta átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Antiɔk, nji yi bɛsí bhi mbɔnyunɛ akʉ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpu chak.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu básɔ́t Yesu báre rɔ́ŋ nɛ yi. Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, bátɛ́mɛri mmǔ ɛtɔk Sírene amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Símun. Áfǔ nyaka ɛbhɨ ǎpɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, Yerúsalɛm. Bákɛ́m yi bábáyti nɛ ɛko Yesu, bákʉ yi apɔkɔ yɔ́ ankoŋo nɔkɔ Yesu.
Ngók nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́ghàti mɛ, ndɛm bɛ, ‘Acha, ɔ̌yàŋ mɛ nkʉ yi?’ Acha arɛm ntá yá bɛ, ‘Faté dɔ́k Damáskɔs. Arɛ́, chɔŋ mángátí wɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm áyábhɛ bɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛkʉ.’
Yesu áfá nɔ́kɔ́ atú Gɛrása, arɔk, asɔt áchwí apé nnyɛ́n, apɛtnsɛm Kapɛ̌naum, ɛtɔk ɛnɛ yi áchɔ̀kɔ.
Achí nyaka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Arɨŋɨ bariɛp amɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yi, kpát anyú nku bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ ywi anyiɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi.
Manyiɛbhɛ́ mɔ até ndǔ nɛjwiti ɛnɛn nɛ́pɛ̀mɛ bhe ɛchɔŋ. Nɛjwiti puyɛ̌ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fɛ̀rɛ bo bakwap amʉɛt. Chi nku anɛ mmu ányù nɛ Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛn pɛ́pɛ́p. Nɛjwiti nɛ́pɛ̀mɛ mmu ɛ̌ti nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ɛnɛn Yesu Kristo ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Píta apɛt ataŋa. Tɛ́mté wu, nnɛ́m nkɔk akók kɔkɔrɔ́kɔ̌ɔ. 
Nnɨk Yesu Acha mmʉɛt ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ yi amfɛrɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ amʉɛt.
Ɛnɛ́ mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, chɔŋ mmu ywɛka amɔt anti mɛ”.
Mpok nchí nɛ bhɔ, nkɛ́m bɔ sayri nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ. Nkɛm bɔ́, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu wap amɔt abhɨkɨ nɛm ɛbhɨ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chí anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka mɛ́nɛm, bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp.
Ndé kʉ yi bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ mɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛnyǔ ɛrɛm áfɔ́k, bɛ́ nnɔ Acha ántwɔ́ ntá ya?
Kɛ Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt arɛm ntá baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bɛ, “Baghɔrɛ Yerúsalɛm, bǎkɛ́ di mɛ! Dí ká chí mmʉɛt ɛyɛka nɛ bɔ̌bhɛka.
Abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ ntá yɛka mpok mǎnókó Yesu?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ́ “Áe! Yɛ̌ chí bɛghok bɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achí sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghok.”
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛchi nɛ́nɛ mbɔ bɛ bágo nyaka nɛpɛ́m nɛsɨ́ ɛnɛsɛ ndu ɛkotákátí nɛ yi, bɛ Mandɛm anchɔŋti mmʉɛt bɛbʉ́ ayɛsɛ bɛ sɛkɛ pɛrɛ bhak ndu kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.
Kɛ, Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́re go ɛ́ndɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
Yesu abhɨŋɨ bǒbhɔ bati byo nɛ apay aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ̌tò bhe nɛfí ndǔ bɛtɨk. Kɛ bǎkɛ́ rɔŋ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, nɛ bǎkɛ́ chwe ndǔ yɛ̌ ɛtɔk Samária ɛ́mɔt.
Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛ́pɛ́rɛ ghaka, Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ mpok akway anɛ yi árɔ mmɨk, ampɛtnsɛm ntá ɛtayi. Ndǔ yi ákɔ́ŋ nyaka bǒbhi fá amɨk, nɛ́nɛ atɔ́ŋ bɛ́ akɔŋ bɔ acha.
bɛ́ ɔ́nkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngátí wɔ mɛnkɛm. Kɛ́ kwɛn ndu yɛ̌ ɛ́mɔt ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛ́ji wɔ. Ɛ́mbák nɔ́ kpát bɛ́gháka ɛwak ɛnɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo ábhèsi.
Sɔt yɛka mpok, mǎmbak pɛ̌ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ nywɔp ɛnɔ.
Nɛ yɛ̌ chi mpok anɛ sɛ́chí nyaka mbɔ bawú ɛ̌ti sɛpu bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm, yí akʉ sɛ́bhak nɛpɛ́m chɛ́chɛm nɛ Kristo mmu ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bɛkoŋo bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi kɛ̌ yi ápɛ́mɛ́ bhé.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɛmbak bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɨ̀ŋɨ Acha bɛ ánkwák yi, Acha ǎpɛmɛ yi.’”
Chi abhɨŋɨ yɛ yí arɛm bɛ, ‘Mɔ́wa, ɔchí fá nɛ mɛ mpǒk nkɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛya, chí ɛyɛ.
Yi kɛ ghati bhɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ tɛ́m nɛkay. Kɛ mpok anɛ yi ábhák aywǐntí nɛ bakoŋo bhi, anɛnɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kpoŋoroŋ ntá yap. 
Ɛ́kʉ Yesu atɛ́m bɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ:
Nku anɛ apú bhak mbɔ anɛ nsɨ́ nyaka nyu nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhap mpok nsɔ́rɛ́ bhɔ́ nɛ awɔ́ wa mfɛ́rɛ́ ɛtɔk Íjip. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ nyaka ambɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nku nsɨ́ áyaŋ bɔ mankʉ. Ɛ́kʉ́ Acha arɛm bɛ, ‘Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ bhɔ. Mmɛ Mandɛm Acha kɛ nchí rɛm.’
Bɛsabhɛ́ ɛtɔk nɛ bɛchɨkɨ́ ɛtɔk bɛbhak nɛjyɛ. Ángɛl ayɛnti ɛtɔk nɛ mɔ́nɔk ɛywi. Bɛsabhɛ́ mfáy bɛbhak nɛjyɛ nɛ bɛsabhɛ́ ɛtɔk nɛ bɛchɨkɨ́ ɛtɔk, nɔ chi bɔkilomɛta nka ɛpay nɛ hɔ́ndrɛt ɛnwi (,).
Apɛt achwe amɛm áchá abhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɔ́fú arɛ chi ɛnɛ́?” Kɛ Yesu abhɨkɨ kɛmɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ, bǒ mankɛm abhɛn báchí arɛ bábhák maknkay tontó ɛ̌ti ɛyi ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ yi átɔ̀ŋ.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maŋák bɛ mánkʉ nɛ mmɔ̌ ɛkáti mbɔ ɛnyu bákʉ́ nɛ ntɔŋ aywi. Nɛ ɛ́chí ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maŋák bɛ mɔ̌bɛtok ámbák mbɔ chi-bɛtok ywi. Mbák bo bákway bɛ́chɨk ntɨ kpát mámbɨŋɨ mɛ mǔnti nnɛrɛ́kɛt bɛ Bɛlsɛbul, ná nɛ be bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt? Chɔŋ mánchyɛ bhe manyɛ́n anɛ́ ábɛ́bhɛ́ áchá ɛnɔ!” 
Ndu ɛ́fákárí nɔ, bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yi bághɔ́ bɛ mbǐ wap bɛbhɔŋ nkáp áchɔŋti. Bákɛ́m Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas, báya gbaka gbaka gbaka bárɔk nɛfísiɛ, bɛsí bǒbatí ɛtɔk, amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ manyé.
Bɔ̌ma, mpú yɨŋɨ mmʉɛ́t ɛya bɛ́ nnáŋ nnu kpát nsɔt awɔ́nɛm, mbɔ̌ŋ akap. Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔ́t ɛnɛ mɛ̌kʉ̀ chí bɛ njɛt ntiɛt, mfɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfʉɛrɛ ansɛm, ndɔbhɛ jɛt ndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
Tɛ̌ndu bɔ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, yi kɛkʉ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay amɛm ɛtɔk ɛyi Násárɛt.
Bákɛ́ sɔt mɛnyɨŋɨ́ bachi bhap ansɛm ansɛm. Bábhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bachi bhap bɛ báchi bo bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ bhɔ sayri. Ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ mántɔŋ ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákʉ̀ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bátɔ́ŋ bɔ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm mmu ápɛ̀mɛ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo bachak bákway bɛbhɔŋ ɛkwak bɛ́kóŋo bhɔ.
Ɛ́kʉ bárɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛrɨŋ ɔ́kwày yɛ bɛkʉ bɛ́ sɛ́ngɔ́, sɛ́noko wɔ? Chɔŋ ɔ́nkʉ yi ntá yɛsɛ?
Bo Israɛl bábhó yɛ mɛ́nywinti ɛ̌ti Yesu, ndǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay.”
Ɛ́tat nɔkɔ, Yesu abhɛsi ɛnyu ɛchak bɛsí bakoŋo bhi bati apay abhɛn báfu ɛtɔk ɛgho bákɔ mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ ndu mɔ́tɔk ɛbhɨ.
Mpok ǎtwɔ nɛ mpok yɔ ánáŋ ánkwáy, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ báyibhiri tɛtɛp Mandɛm mándɔbhɛ rɛm chi barak anɛ ápɔ̀kɔ bho angʉrɛ ɛbhɨ kpát mánja bakoŋo Yesu bɛ mandɔbhɛ koŋo chi bhɔ.
Mbák báyàŋ tontó bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ, agha ákway mɛnɨ bhe?
Bo Israɛl abhɛn fá Yerúsalɛm bárɛm bɛ́ ɔ̌kɔ̀ ɔ́ngati nɔkɔ bo Israɛl mankɛm abhɛn báchí amɛm bɛtɔk bɛchak bɛ mámfɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndǔ bɛbhé Moses nɛ bɛ mándɔ bɛ́syɛ́p bɔ̌bhap, nɛ bɛ mándɔ́ bɛ́kóŋo bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhap.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ ndǔ bɛtɔk bɛchak ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá kɛkwɔt. Mbɔŋ bɛ́gháti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm árɛ́ nkwɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ntwɔ́.”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ bɛti, bǒnkwɔ́ bátɨ́ŋ bákʉ́ Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas bábʉ́ɛ barɔk ɛtɔk Bɛ́roa. Arɛ́, bárɔ́k báchwé ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl.
Bághɔ́ bɛ tɛtɛp, Mandɛm kɛ afyɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ amɔya bɛ ngati bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi akʉ nɛ Píta bɛ yi angati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá bo Israɛl.
Ndɛm kɛpɨ mbɔ ɛchɨŋtímu. Bě kɛ̌ bǎpúrí mɛ nkʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ, be kɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛghati bho ɛnyǔ mmu mɛ nchí. Yɛ̌ndu mpú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, bǒnto abhɛn bǎyòŋ nɔ manyɛ́n ayap amfay bábhɨkɨ cha mɛ.
Kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha ɛyɔ chi bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ maŋák ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afʉɛrɛ ntá Yesu Kristo Acha akʉ ntá yɛsɛ. Yi Kristo kɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́pɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ntá Mandɛm. 
Nɛ bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti bo ndǔ bɛchɔ́ŋti manyɛ́n ayap, nɛ bɛpap Mandɛm, nɛ nɛsaŋ, nɛ nɛyoŋómʉɛt, nɛ mpányu, nɛ bɛkaysi babhi akɔ anɛ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛtaŋ ntí nɛ bɔtáyap nɛ bɔmáyap.
Mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chí amfay, bɛ́chák bɛ́chí fá amɨk ɛbhɛ́n bo básɔ̀t mbɔ bɔmándɛ́m. Bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chí ɛnyuyɔ nɛ mbɔk bho básɔ̀t bɔ mbɔ bafɔ bhap.
Píta asá ɛyɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Ná nɛ bhɛsɛ́? Sɛ́rɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sɛ́kòŋo wɔ! Nsáy anɛ sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ chí yí?”
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎchí bǒ mmɨk. Mfu chi amfay. Bǎchí bǒ mmɨk nɛ, mpú mmǔ mmɨk nɛ.
Nɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛchyɛ bhe áfɔ́k anɛ aya acha bɛ mǎmbɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ be ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛ́ya ɛncha kpát mǎnkwáy bɛkwak bo abhɛn mɛnyɨŋ bɛchɛbhɛ bhɔ.
Báre rɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́kɛ́ kɛm yi mpok ɛpa mbɔnyunɛ bo bákway bɛ́chyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri.” 
Árɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu ǎfʉɛ̀t, abho bɛyaŋ mbi bɛ ángɔ́ ɛnyǔ mmu Yesu achi, kɛ ɛ̌ti kɛmbɨŋ ɛki nɛ bɛyǎ bo, yi kɛkwáy bɛghɔ yi.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bǒnkwɔ Yesu mankɛm abhɛn báfú atú Esia bátɨ̌knsɛm ntá ya. Fijɛ́lɔs nɛ Hɛmogɛ́nes nkwɔ́ bátɨknsɛm ntá ya.
Ntí apu bɛbhɔŋ mmok nɛ ntaŋ arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm bɛ́ghɔ̀ arɛ́ nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn achi ɛyǐ ɛrɔŋɔ.
Bǒ bhɔ bápú jwimɛm ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbɔnyunɛ Satan mmu achi mandɛm mmɨk anɛ́mɛ́ bɔ amɨk bɛ bákɛ noko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Yi apu yaŋ bɔ́ mangɔ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́ghɔ̀. Nɔ chi, bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo. Apu yaŋ bɔ mandɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ Kristo achi, Kristo mmu achi ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt nɛ Mandɛm.
“Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bo abhɛn Mandɛm áfóŋórí ɛpɨŋ ɛyap ɛnɛ bápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé, antɛsɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap nkwɔ,
Bɛ́fʉɛt ntá Mɔ́ywi wu sɛ́bhɔŋ mbi bɛ mánku bhɛsɛ mǎmfɛrɛ ndǔ kɛsɛm ɛkɛn bɛbʉ́, nɔ chi, mǎmfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ. 
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ɛrɛm ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛnɛ pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ mmu anɛ achi arɛ chɔ́kɔ́. Mfǎy nɛ mmɨk mánɛ́msi bɛsí bhi. Bákɛpɛrɛ kway bɛghɔ mfay nɛ mmɨk.
Sɛ́nsɨ́ŋ bɔ́ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bábho bɛ́pay bɛbhé Moses ɛbhɛ́n amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl tɛntɛp, ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt, nɛ bo yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk bárɨŋɨ bhɔ.” 
Yesu apɛt arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bhɔ abhɛn yi ato bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághók bé ǎghók chi mɛ. Anɛ ábyak be ǎbyak chi mɛ. Mmu nɛ ábyak mɛ, ǎbyak chi mmu anɛ átó mɛ.” 
ambe nɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ́ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛkɛt ɛya ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak chi ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt’, kɛ bǎyíbhírí yɔ́ ɛ́rɔp chi ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ baghɛ́p bábhɛ̀sɛ arɛ!”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛkáti ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Ɔ́kɛ́ mɔ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ.’”
Nɛ bo bábhɔŋ bɛghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm, bɛ́ amɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk bo mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛghok yɔ, kɛ Mandɛm ankʉ ngwɛnti mmɨk antwɔ́.” 
Afɛ́rɛ́ mpap nɛntɨ bakwɔ́ bho bhɔ apay bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛwú ɛni ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Akʉ bɛ́ bakwɔ́ bho apay mándɔp chi nkwɔ amɔt, nɛ bɛ bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl, mambak ɛrɨrɨ nɛ Mandɛm.
Nɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ apú kwáy bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ánchyɛ́ yí mbɔnyunɛ yi apu chɛ́p yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Yímbɔŋ kɛ áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m nɛ ɛ̌yú nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Mbák mmu akɔŋ bo apú yoŋ mmʉɛt, apú kʉ barak ntíánwɔ́p, apú yɨŋɨ chi ndiɛrɛ mmʉɛt yi. Apú kaysi chí ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛkwak yímbɔŋ, apú wakari bɛbent, apú fyɛ bo antɨ mbák bákʉ yi bɛbʉ́.
Chɔŋ Tíkíkɔs ángati bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ya. Achí manɔ nɛ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ anɛ nkɔ́ŋ tontó. Ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨk nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt nɛ ǎtok Acha nɛ mɛ.
Kɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀ mmu chi ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ yi ambɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ, nɛ ambɔŋ maŋák, nɛ kpák, nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ, nɛ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ, nɛ ambɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí ntɨ, nɛ ambak mmu tɛtɛp,
Be nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkwak bɛsɛ ndǔ nɛnɨkímʉɛt. Nɛ chɔŋ bɛyǎ bo mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm bakak ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ, bɛyɨŋɨ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt. 
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, yi ǎkway bɛpɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ntá yi atwɔ ntá Mandɛm ndɔŋ amɔt ndak amay, tɛ̌ndu yi achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yap.
Kɛ nchí to bɔ̌mayɛsɛ abhɛn ntá yɛka ndu bɛkʉ bɛ nɛpá anɛ sɛ́pànyu ɛ̌ti ɛyɛka ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ákɛ́ bhak ndɛ́ndɛm. Ɛnɛ, chi bɛkʉ bɛ mǎnkwáy bɛ́tóŋti mmʉɛt nɛ aywɛka akap mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngátí bhɔ bɛ chɔŋ mǎnkʉ.
Bǎbhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ mɛ́nyiɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎkɔ́ŋɔ́. Kɛ sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kʉ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re sɛnɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm ánkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mányìɛ.
Mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu wu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́ afa arɔk ntá mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu arɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́yàŋ bɛkʉ nɔ yi? Mmǔ-nɛ abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mbɔ mmu Rom. Ɔbhɛ́ mándɛ́n yí?”
Mmǔ nɛme wu akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Ɛta, mmu apú anɛ ápɔ̀kɔ mɛ nsɛp anyɛ́n ayak mpok nnyɛ́n nɛ́bòŋ. Mpɛrɛ́ nu bɛ́chwɔ́p arɛ́, mmu achák anáŋ áyámbɨ.”
Nɛ mbák bǎpwɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chí ntá bo abhɛn bǎbhaka ntɨ bɛ bakɛmɛ ntá yɛka, bakak amɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ bhe achi bɛ yi? Yɛ̌ chí bǒ bɛbʉ́ bápwɔ̀ nkwɔ mɛnyɨŋ ntá batɨ̌ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́, ndu bákɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bápwɔ́ ntá yap!
“Chɔŋ sɛ́nkʉ yi nɛ bǒbhɛ́n? Bǒ mankɛm fá ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm baghɔ ɛrɛmɛ́ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bákʉ́ nɛ sɛ́pú kway bɛtaŋa.
Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ bápú kway bɛkʉ mmu anɛ arɔ mbi Mandɛm bɛ ámpɛt antɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi. Nchí rɛm ɛ̌ti ɛnyǔ mmu anɛ mánáŋ bákʉ́ amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ́ yi, aghɔ́ akap anɛ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ̀ bǒ bhi, nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ yi nkwɔ.
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́chí mbɔ nkɔsíɛ́ anɛ áyàŋ bɛku batay bɛyǎ nkáp.
Ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, bárɔ ɛsɨ́ ɛbhé mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ nyaka bɛtaŋ, ɛ́kɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Nɛka Ábɛl kɛ nɛkʉ yi achyɛ nyaka Mandɛm akap anɛ́ ákwáy achá anɛ Ken. Nɛsɔt anɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ akap Ábɛl atɔ́ŋ bɛ aká bɛ Ábɛl achi chak bɛsí bhi. Yɛ̌ndu Ábɛl ágú, nɛka ɛni nɛ́kʉ abhʉɛt bɛrɛm kɛpɨ ntá yɛsɛ tɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ.
Kɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛyɛka ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́, mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, mbɔŋ bɛrɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ amɔt anɛ bǎyàŋ mandɔ yi andɔk. Bǎyaŋ mámfɛ́rɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl amɔ, yí ándɔ́kɔ́?”
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ɛnyǔ mmu anɛ ábhàk chak bɛsí Mandɛm ndǔ yi ásɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu chi bɛ, “Kɛ́ bhɛ́p mmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ agha ankó amfay?’” [Nɔ chi bɛ mmu abhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛko amfay, ansɔt Kristo, ansɛp fá amɨk nɛ yi.]
Nywɔp ntóŋtí bo Israɛl nɛ́kwáy. Bɛkʉ yɛ bɛ́ ɛrɛnɛ ngú ɛ́kɛ́ rɔp amfay ɛkotákátí ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, bárɔ́k babhɛp Páílet bɛ ánchyɛ́ bɛtaŋ mánsíɛ́ptí bɛkak ɛbhap, mámfɛ́rɛ́ bhɔ ndǔ bɛkotakati. Nywɔp nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɔ nɛ́bhak nywɔp nɛgho.
Mpok Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti báfú atú Masidónia báchwɔ́bhɛ́ Atɛns, Pɔ̌l arɔ bɛtɨk bɛghoko bɛ́tɛm arɔbhɛ kʉ chi bɛtɨk bɛghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ndu mpok nkɛm anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, anu nɔkɔ bɛkʉ bo Israɛl mángɔ́ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu kɛ achí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛrɨŋɨ chí bɛ mmu apú kway bɛbhák nɛpɛ́m mbák mámfɛ́rɛ́ bɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛbhɛ́n bo bákáysí bɛ́ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ mɛnwɔp yi amʉɛt.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ chi bɛ, tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm áyɨ́ŋɨ́ ághɔ́ bɛ sɛ́kwǎy bo abhɛn yi afyɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ amɔ́, nɔ kɛ sɛ́ghàti bho yɔ. Nɛ puyɛ̌ chi bɛ bo mámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ bhɛsɛ, kɛ chí bɛ́ Mandɛm mmu áyɨ̀ŋɨ bɛghɔ ɛnyǔ bati ayɛsɛ achi amɛm, ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Nɛ mpok báwày Stífin ntísiɛ aywɛ, mbak arɛ́ nkwɔ téé, mbabhɛri nɔkɔ ndɛn bo abhɛn bátɛ́mtí yí nɛ batay baway. Nka bɛ́ mángwáy yi.’
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́chwɔ́p nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n Kios. Nɛ́pɛ́t nɛ́yi nɔ́kɔ́, sɛ́nók sɛ́chwɔ́p Sámɔs, nɛ ndǔ ntɨnywɔp sɛ́gháka Milɛ́tɔs.
Kɛ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ chɔŋ ngati bhɔ bhɛ, ‘Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ be wáwák. Fǎ ká mɛ bɛsí, be bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́.’” 
Mfórí nɛwú bɛyǎ mpok ɛnɛ́ mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ nɛkɔ. Mfórí nɛwú amɛm manyɛ́n anɛ ájwí ágbóko, mfori nɛwú amɔ bɛtaŋtí baghɛ́p nɛ amɔ́ batɨ̌ bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Mfórí nɛwú amɛm bɛtɔk bɛgho, nɛ amɛm baso, nɛ amɛm manyu nɛ amɔ́ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bɛtábhá.
Ɛ́fákári ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndɔŋ ɛ́rát, ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm amfay.
Kaká ká Ubánɔs mmu ákʉ́ bɛtɨk Kristo nɛ mɛ. Kaká ká nkwɔ mmʉɛrɛkɔŋ awa Stákis.
Mpok bɛkɔk kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ ató nkʉbɛtɨk ywi bɛ ándɔ́k ánsɔ́t aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ mbwɔt.
Kɛ mmɨk akwak yi. Bɛghárɛ́ bɛ́fú arɛ́ mɛnyu nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn nɛ́fù anyǔ nnyɔ́.
Bághókó nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Píta árɛ́mɛ́ mɛnkɛm, manyu áchók bhɔ. Báre chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó mandɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɔ Mandɛm achyɛ mbi ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ bɛ mankway bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap, mambɔŋ nɛpɛ́m!” 
Babhi áchí mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu anɛ́ Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ndǔ bapɛ́m ayɛsɛ́, kɛ Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ amɔt kɛ̌ áchyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ.
Wɔ, ɔchá ɛtayɛsɛ Ábraham mmu ágú nyaka? Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm nkwɔ bágú nyaka! Ɔ̌sɔ̀t mmʉɛt yɛ mbɔ agha?”
Nchí bɨ́tí bhe tontó bɛ́ bǎkaysi mɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ bǎkòŋo sayri mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ntɔ́ŋɔ́ bhe.
Mbák ɔkɔŋ ɛtayɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ chí máyɛ ɔchá mɛ, nɔ́ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbhak nkoŋo wa. Nɛ mbák ɔkɔŋ mɔ́ywɛ ɔcha mɛ, nɔ́ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbhak nkoŋo wa.
Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́twɔ̀ fakari, bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Acha, sɛ́nsɔ́t bɔakparɛnja bhɛsɛ sɛnu nɛ bǒbhɛn-ɛ?”
Ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, bǒ ɛtɔk Ninivɛ báfate mángati bhe bɛ bǎkʉ bɛbʉ́. Ɛwak ɛyɔ, bɔ́ bárɛm nɔ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bɔ bátɨk nyaka nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap mpok Jóna ághátí bhɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Nɛ́nɛ, mmu achí fá nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛka anɛ áchá Jóna; yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎpu ka bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka.
“Nkʉ́ yi nɛ Yesu mmu bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò?” Bɔ́ mankɛm bábhó bɛ́bɨ́k bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!”
Mɛ Pɔ̌l mmu Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ́ mbák mǔnto Yesu Kristo kɛ̌ nchí nsɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ́ bɛ́koŋo nkaysi ayi yímbɔŋ. Nchí fá nɛ manɔ́ ywɛsɛ́ Sɔstɛ́nes.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu yɛka abhɔŋ bɛghok bǒbati mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm kɛ áyàp mmu anɛ ákɛ̀m ɛtɔk nɛ yi kɛ afyɛ́ abhɛn bachi nɛ́nɛ.
Kristo atwɔ́ mbɔ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ ákʉ́ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ mɛ́mfákárí. Achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ɛnɛ ɛ́kwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi ɛ́cha ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí nyaka fá amɨk. Puyɛ̌ bo kɛ báté yɔ, nɛ ɛ́pú ndǔ mpǎy mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn fá amɨk.
Nɛ sɛ́ghɔ nɛ amɨ́k mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ Yerúsalɛm nɛ mbaŋ ɛchak amɛm ɛtɔk bo Israɛl. Bágó yí ndu ɛkotákátí, agú.
Akwɛ́n atɛp mánɛ́n amɨk, arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Acha, foŋori bhɔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap ɛbhɛn.” Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, asɛbhɛ.
Satan asɔt yi barɔk Yerúsalɛm, ɛtɔk Mandɛm, bákó ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ áchí tɛ amfay ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm.
Nɛ ánáŋ ántwɔ́, chɔŋ ankʉ bǒ mmɨk mangɔ bɛ báchí bǒ bɛbʉ́, mángɔ bɛ mɛ nchí chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ mangɔ bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ bhɔ ndǔ nɛtaŋ anɛ bɔ bátàŋ mɛ.
Mpok Mandɛm afyɛ́ Ábraham bariɛp, ayɨkɨ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛni yímbɔŋ, tɛ̌ndu yɛ̌ mmu apu anɛ acha yi bɛ yi ánkwáy bɛyɨkɨ ndu nnyɛ́n mmu wu.
Yí chí Ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ barak anɛ tɛtɛp. Bǒ mmɨk bápú kway bɛsɔt yi nɛ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ bápú kway bɛghɔ yi, nɛ bapu kway bɛrɨŋɨ yí. Kɛ chɔŋ mǎndɨ̀ŋɨ yi mbɔnyunɛ ǎbhák chɔŋ nɛ bhe, nɛ amɛm batɨ yɛka.”
Yesu ǎfù nyaka ɛtɔk Jɛríko nɛ bakoŋo bhi. Ngɛ́mtay bho báré koŋo bhɔ.
Bǎghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí bhe mbɔ bɔ̌bhi ndu bɛ́fyɛ bhe ntɨ? Arɛm nyaka bɛ “Mɔ́wa, ɔ́kɛ́ sɔt mbɔ ɛráká ndak, nɛnyurɛ anɛ Acha ányùrɛ wɔ, nɛ ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ ntɨ nɛ́nɛ́m wɔ amɛm, mpok yi áchyɛ̀ wɔ ntɛ́msí.
Ndu nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛni arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, Ɛtaya! Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́cha wɔ ɛ́pú. Kʉ nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ámfʉɛ́t mɛ ansɛm nti. Kɛ ɛ́kɛ́ bhák mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌yáŋ, ɛ́mbák chi mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́yàŋ.”
Jɔ̌n ǎghàti nyaka bho ɛ̌ti yi ambɨk, andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chi mmǔ anɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m nyaka ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, ‘Mmǔ anɛ átwɔ̀ mɛ ansɛm achá mɛ. Bápɛ́rɛ bhe mɛ, yí achi.’”
Mbɛ́p bɛ́, ‘Acha chí wɔ́ agha?’ Acha akɛmɛ mɛ bɛ, ‘Mɛ Yesu kɛ̌ ɔ́chyɛ̀ nɔ́ nɛnyok.
Ɛrɨ bɛ amɨ́k ágiri bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ ghɔ mbaŋ, nɛ bɛ́ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́nyɨ́rɛ́ bhɔ amɨk mpoknkɛm.”
Ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛ́t ɛ́mɔt kɛ ɛchí. Yɛ̌ndu bɛsɛ́ sɛ́yá, sɛ́chí mmʉɛt amɔt, mbɔnyunɛ bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́nyìɛ chi brɛ́t ɛ́rɛ amɔt.
Mbák mámkpɔ́t mbɔk batap ɛnɔk ólif mámfɛrɛ ndǔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bápɨ́, mánsɔt yɛ batap ɛnɔk ólif ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ mambat ambɨ-ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bápɨ́, nɔ nɛnyíɛ́ batap anɛ bábhárɛ́ nɛ́fù chi ndǔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bápɨ́. Bo Israɛl abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl báchí mbɔ batap ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ.
Mbák ɛkak ɛ́ndɛ́m bɛ, “Tɛ̌ndu mpú awɔ, mpú ɛ́pókómʉɛt.” Ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ ɛkak ɛ́kɛ́ bhak ɛ́pókómʉɛt kɛ́?
Yɛ̌ Símun nkwɔ́ anoko bájwíti yí. Bájwítí nɔ́kɔ́ yí, abhat mmʉɛt nɛ Fílip, ankoŋo nɔkɔ yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak. Nyu arɔp yi fuu ɛ̌ti bɛrɛmɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛ́n Fílip ákʉ̀, nɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm áfʉɛ̀t ntá Fílip antɔŋ nɔkɔ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, Yesu akɛmɛ yi chi bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ɛ́mbák mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngátí wɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ ɛrɨ bɛ sɛnkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ.” Jɔ̌n aka yɛ, ajwiti Yesu.
Yɛ̌ básyɛp mmu syɛp, yɛ̌ babhɨkɨ syɛp, ɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chi bɛ́ sɛmbak bǒ bakɔ.
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bɛ́rɛ̀m chi ɛnyǔ Kristo achi nɛ Nkwɔ Kristo.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ntá yɛka bǒnkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Tɛsalónika. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛká bo Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛtayɛsɛ, be bho bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha. Nchí fá nɛ bɔ̌mayɛsɛ Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti.
Mbák mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ, nɛrɨŋɨ anɛ bǎrɨŋɨ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo apú bhak ndɛ́ndɛm, kɛ bɛrɨ bɛ́fù ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎkʉ̀.
Básɔ́t Yesu bágó ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí, bágʉɛ́p ɛbháŋá bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ ɛnyǔ bábhɔ́ŋ bɛ́kɔ́rɛ ndɛn ɛyi bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ambɔŋ amɔt.
Mbɛ́p kpɨ́k be, mmǔ ǎkwáy bɛ́kɔ́rɛ Kristo ndǔ bakwɔ́? Ghatí ka mɛ. Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ̌ bágó ndǔ ɛkotákátí ɛ̌ti yɛká kɛ? Yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka achí anɛ bájwítí yí ndǔ nnyɛ́n Pɔ̌l?
Mmǔ anɛ ákɔ́ŋ batɨ, ǎkɔ̀ amɛm bɛdiɛ́rɛ́. Nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú bhak ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛnɛ ɛ́kway bɛkʉ yi ankwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok, ɔsɛ́ptí yi bɛ bɔángɛl máncha yi. Ɔkʉ yɛ yí ámbɔ́ŋ kɛnɛ́m nɛ kɛnókó mbɔ mfɔ.
bɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi amfay bho ndu bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ nɛwú, bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm nkwɔ bɛbhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ amfay bho ndu bɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ mámbák chak bɛsí bhi. Nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́.
Bárɔ́bhɛ bóŋóbóŋ amɛm ɛbhɨ nɛ ndǔ mmɨk njiɛ, mámbɛsɛ nɔkɔ amɛm bɔbasɛm nɛ amɛm babhok. Mmɨkɨ nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kway nyaka nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bɛrɨ́tí bo mbɔ bhɔ bábhak arɛ.
Kɛ ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɛ́n Lɔt afa ɛtɔk Sódom, Mandɛm akʉ ngó áfú amfay nɛ ɛkɛm mbɔ batay anɛ ádù, anyɛ mbɔ manyiɛp, ásɔ́ŋ bɔ mankɛm.
Mmu anɛ áchi ngɛ́p ákɛ́pɛrɛ ghɛ́p aghɛ́p. Mmu abhɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk sayri ndǔ bɛkɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ ndǔ bɛkwak bachɛ́bhɛ́bho.
Agha átàŋ ancha mmɨk? Chi ndiɛrɛ mmu anɛ ánókó bɛ Yesu chí Mmɔ Mandɛm. 
Árɛ́m nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ yi nɛ batɨ bhi bachi nyaka maknkay tontó bɛghɔ bɛyǎ nsi ɛnɛ bakɛmɛ.
Kɛ ngɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ bápú kɔ ndɔ́ŋ amɔt nɛ tɛtɛp anɛ achi ndu Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, mfate ngati Píta bɛsí bhap mankɛm bɛ, “Mbák wɔ mmu Israɛl ɔ̌kʉ̀ mbɔ mmu anɛ apu mmu Israɛl, ndaká yi ɔ́nù bɛkʉ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mámbák mbɔ bo Israɛl?” 
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu ámbyák yi. Tɨ́k ká yi sayri bɛ ámpɛtnsɛm ntá ya. Batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ nɛ mmɛ sɛ́nòŋ yi.
Kʉ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ángɔ́ bɛ́ bǎpú mmʉɛt gum gum ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka. Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ Yesu Acha ǎpɛ̀tnsɛm mandú mpok.
Chɔŋ Tíkíkɔs antwɔ́ awu angati bhe ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchi fá nɛ mɛ nɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́kʉ̀. Achi manɔ ywɛsɛ anɛ sɛ́kɔ́ŋɔ́. Achi nkʉbɛtɨk anɛ Acha nɛ yí achi mmu anɛ abhʉrɛ bariɛp ami.
Bǎchi bo Mandɛm. Bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛpúsí, nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí nkaysi. Bǎkɛ́ fyɛ́ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ bo bachak. Bǎkɛ rɔ mbɔŋ bɛ mántáká mɛnyɨ̌ŋ ɛbhɔ ndu nkwɔ ywɛka.
Bǒbhɔ kɛtɨ́knsɛm yɛ̌ chí ndǔ nɛway bho awap nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ baraká njɔ ayap nɛ barak ɛ́pusi ayap, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ aghɛp awap.
“Ɛwak ɛyɔ, ɛ́bhák ɛnyumɔt nɛ mmu anɛ achi amfǎy ɛkɛt. Ákɛ́ rɔ́ŋ kpɨ́k anywɔ́p bɛ ampɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ kɛ ambʉɛ. Ɛnyumɔt nɛ mmu anɛ achi ɛbhɨ. Ákɛ́ rɛm bɛ́ ǎpɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p ansɔt yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mbɔ ɛnyu ngáti nɛ́ bhe, kɛ nchí ghati bo mankɛm fá amɨk: Bák ká pɛ̌.”
Kɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká nɔ!” Atɔk yɛ atú mmu wu, abu yi.
Ɛchi ɛnyuyɔ mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re bhe nyaka Lɛ́vi mpok Mɛlkísɛdɛk atɛmɛri Ábraham. Yɛ̌ nɔ, Lɛ́vi ánáŋ achí nyaka ndǔ manoŋ Ábraham.
Lukas, ngaŋ anɛ sɛ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó, nɛ Démas bátò be bakak.
Bɛtaŋtí mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́pú kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Yɛ̌ chí mfay, yɛ̌ chi mmɨk ápú kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó mɛnkɛm yɛ ɛ́mɔt ɛpu kway bɛfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bhɛsɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ndu bɛkwak bhɛsɛ.
Mandɛm apu Mandɛm ɛbyɔk, ǎyàŋ sɛmbɔŋ chi ɛyɔŋ ɛmɔt nɛ kpák ndǔ nkwɔ yɛsɛ. Mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchí amɛm bakwɔ́ bho Mandɛm ankɛm,
Baghɔrɛ abhɛn báfú nɛ Yesu tɛ Gálili, bákóŋo, baghɔ nnɛm, nɛ ɛnyǔ bábhʉ́rɛ́ mmʉɛt yi amɛm.
nɛ mpok anɛ yi ágháká anywɔ́p, ǎbhɨŋɨ mamʉɛrɛ bhi nɛ bakokosi bhi, angati bhɔ bɛ, ‘Ŋák ká nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ́, mbɔ̌ŋ ághɔ́ŋɔmɛn wa anɛ ánɛ́mɛ́ nyaka.’”
Mmu anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm apu nɛ yi, apú kway bɛbhɔŋ akabhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ntá Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm. Apú kway bɛrɨŋɨ bhɔ, nɛ bɛbhak chi ɛpɔ̌ndak ntá yi, mbɔnyunɛ ndiɛrɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ̌ ákʉ̀ mmu andɨŋɨ bhɔ.
Mbɔk bǒ nkwɔ Fárisi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bárɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ bákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́pú chak bɛkʉ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt!”
Símun Píta nɛ Tɔmás anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ ɛfák, nɛ Natániɛl anɛ áfú Kána atú Gálili, nɛ bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi bati apay, nɛ bakoŋo Yesu báchák bati apay bachi nyaka ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt.
Kɛ ɛ́kɛ́ bhák nɔ nɛ bhe. Mǔngo ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛbhak mbɔ mɔ́nkwɛn ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka, mǔnti ambak mbɔ mǔbɛtok.
Mandɛm ákʉ́ nɔ bɛ bɛsɛ bo sɛ́pú pɛrɛ kɔ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛsɛ babhɔŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bakwǎŋwaŋ bákʉ̀, kɛ sɛ́rɔbhɛ kɔ chí ndu bɛtaŋ abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhak chak bɛsí bhi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛbhé Moses bɛ́yaŋ sɛ́mbak.
Mandɛm achyɛ́ mɛ́ akap, mbo bɛtɨk awu ntá yɛká mbɔ ɛsáyrí nte bɛkɛt, ngoko nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mɨk bɛ́tée ɛkɛt sayri, nɛ nɛ́nɛ, mmu achák ǎte ɛkɛt arɛ́. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ átè ɛkɛt ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɔ, abhɔŋ bɛ́sɔ́t mpok, ante yɔ sáyrí.
Ghɔ́ ka! Nchyɛ́ bhe bɛtaŋ bɛ bǎkway bɛyat nnyɔ́ nɛ ngá-nɛghay amɨk. Nchyɛ́ be bɛtaŋ amfay bɛtaŋ Satan, mǔmpap, nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛpu chyɛ be ɛsɔŋɔri.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ bɔ bárɔ́ŋɔ́, bátwɔ̀ chi nɛ mɛnɛmɛ nɛ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ̌ nchí sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá yɛka nkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Tɛsalónika. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka bǒ Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ be bho bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha. Nchí fá nɛ Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti. Mandɛm antɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, anchyɛ bhe kpák. 
Ɛnɛ́ bɔ̌mayi mǎnáŋ bárɔ́, bárɔ́ŋɔ́ Yerúsalɛm ndǔ ɛpa ɛyɔ, Yesu arɔk arɛ́ nkwɔ. Kɛ arɔk chi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, kɛrɔ́ŋ kpoŋoroŋ.
Be bǎkap mɛ ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbha kpát yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɔp. Nɛ́nɛ, bakáp anɛ bǎtó Ɛpafrodáytɔs ántwɔ́ ánchyɛ́ mɛ ákʉ́ mbɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ nchɛ́bhɛ́. Nɛ akap aywɛka áchí mbɔ akap ɛrítí ɛriɛp anɛ́ bǎchíɛ ntá Mandɛm, nɛ Mandɛm ǎbhɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ wu.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛbhé Mandɛm. Bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Kɛ́wáy mmu, Kɛ́kwɛn bɛrwɔp, Kɛ́ghɛ́p aghɛ́p, Kɛ́te ntísiɛ ákwárɛ́, Kɛ́nyiɛ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmu ndǔ bapu, Chiɛ̌ máyɛ nɛ ɛtayɛ kɛnókó.’”
Ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛyɛka ɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ bo maŋák, ɛ́mbak mbɔ ɛnɛ́ mmu anɛ afyɛ́ ngaŋ anyu bɛ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kɛ́mɛ bo abhɛn bábhɛ̀p be mɛnyɨŋ. 
Kɛ mbák chí Hɛ́rɔd, ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Chí Jɔ̌n anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ mámkpɔ́t ntí ywi kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Sɛ́noko nɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mmu Nyáŋá anɛ Mandɛm átó.”
Ɛwat ɛ́fú amfáy tɛ́mchók mbɔ ɛnɛ́ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ɛ́jwǐ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ bɔ bachi arɛ.
Chɔŋ mángwáy bɛyǎ bhap nɛ bɔakparɛnja, nɛ mánkɛmti bachak mbɔ basɛ́mɛ́ nɛnú ndǔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk. Chɔŋ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm mánjati Yerúsalɛm kpatɛ mpok ayap amfʉɛt. 
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ Seséria akó ɛtɔk, arɔk akaka nkwɔ́ Yesu abhɛn bachi arɛ́, asɛp arɔk Antiɔk.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ɛncha ntá baghɔrɛ́ nɛ mɛniɛ nɛ abhɛn báchí nɛ bɔ amɔ mpok ayɔ! Chɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri mɛ́ntwɔ fá amɨk nɛ Mandɛm ankʉ bǒ Yerúsalɛm mángɔ bɛběntɨ bhi.
Ɛnyumɔt kɛ ɛ́chí bɛ́ mbɔk yɛka nkwɔ bǎte kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakoŋo Nikolas bátòŋ,   bɛkʉ bɔ mankwɛn ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn.
Mpok ɛyɔ Ɔgɔ́stɔs abhak mfɔ Rom, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mánsɔt mpáy bho mankɛm abhɛn bachi ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi antɛn yi.
Ɛkʉ bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.” Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ nkwɔ́ mpú ghati yɛ bhe mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Sɛ́pɛrɛ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ sɛ́náŋ sɛ́kpɔt nsɔ́ŋtí ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk nɛ amɔ́. Mpok bo básɔ̀kɔti bhɛsɛ́, sɛ́nɨ̀k chí mmʉɛt bɛ́ Mandɛm ánjɛ́t bhɔ́. Nɛ mpok bo báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ́ ɛsɔŋɔri, sɛ́kɛ̀p chí ntɨ.
Ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ nkáp aywɛ áchí, arɛ́ kɛ̌ ntɨ ɛnɛ nkwɔ nɛ́bhak.” 
Bariɛp Mandɛm amɔ ntá Ábraham achí nyaka bɛ, “Nkúbhɛ́ mpok anɛ mmíɛ́ mburɛ, chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm, nɛ Sará ambé mɔ́mbakanɛm.”
Ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ nkáp ywɛ áchí, arɛ́ kɛ̌ ntɨ ɛnɛ nkwɔ nɛ́bhak. 
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ Kristo ákʉ́ nyaka mmʉɛt ɛyi mǔbɛtok ntá bo Israɛl ndu bɛtɔŋ bhɔ bɛ Mandɛm ǎbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami amɛn yi afyɛ́ nyaka nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhap.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, ngɔrɛ́ amɔt amɛm ngɛ́mtáy bo abhɛn bachi arɛ arɛm ntá Yesu nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛ, “Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábhé wɔ, achyɛ wɔ amɨ!”
Chɔŋ ɛndɨ ɛncha ntá bo abhɛn bábhak pě mpok ɛtayap átwɔ́! Tɛtɛp nchí ghati bhe bɛ mpok yi atwɔ, ǎghati bhɔ manchɔkɔ amɨk, anchóŋ ndɛn ɛyi, ansɔt nɛnyíɛ́ anchyɛ bhɔ manyíɛ́.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, ɛchi ɛnyǔ yɔ nɛ bǒbhɛn nkwɔ. Bághɔ̀ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifú ɛkɛn kɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ mámbyak bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ amfáy yap. Bɛkoŋo kɛnɔ́ ɛkɔ bárɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bho, mánkʉ nɔkɔ bɛpɔ̌ barak ɛpúsí.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághàti bho, máyi nɛ bɔ̌mayi bátwɔ́ bátee nɛfí, mánjaŋ nɔkɔ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ yi.
Báchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mángwɔ́t yi. Bafyɛ́ yi ngɛm amɔ, básɔ́t bárɔ́k ntá Páílet, mmu Rom anɛ achí nyaka gɔ́bhanɔ atú Judɛ́ya mpok yɔ. 
Ɛ́kʉ́ baghat bafʉɛt atú Misia, bárɔ́k Troas.
